latinus wos called kyngdō latinorum ¶and carmentis doughter euandri foond fyrſt latyn lettyrs thauranus bowt tyme wos kyng babulon aſſeriorum vnder thys man troy wos deſtruyed fyrſt occaſion batell grekys mony parrellys ſee wēt home hys penolopem moſt faythfull moſt chaſtyt woman red grekys parychit wrecchytly aftir deſtruyd troy bothe wat er land o went homward yane ¶and wos thee principall mirabilia oꝑa vide iudicū 13 anno mūdi iiijm lxxv et an̄ xpī natiuitatē mc xiiij ieſſe ſon obeth lyne criſt odyrwyſe called yſay fadre dauid thys tyme leued noaull man honeſty kyng ne gret gouerner bot hym mony tymes made mencion holy ſcriptur hym deſcendit criſt ſaueour thys tyme hely wos iuge biſſhop iſrael wich ij ſonnys ophni phinees coreket ſufficiently ponyſſhit bothe lord ſlayn philiſtions hely feell ſeit brake nec hely wos iuge next samſon linage aron wos fyrſt biſſhop god electe bot ythamar linage duryt cxx yere wych lynage hely wos fyrſt biſſhope abyathar laſt vide plara primo regum tyme saull wos kīg iſrael̄ aft er maſter hys hiſtories ̄ ioſephus ī viij boke saule wos firſt kyng ī iſrael̄ regnet xx yere wich wos kyng wos good man electe god bot afterward wrecchytly fayled wos ſlayn iij ſonnys hyllys gylboy tyme ſaul samuell wos iuge prophet iſrael holi man ̄ borne baran moder mony day ̄ mynyſtred foor lord child age ̄ wos hee biſſhope bot iuget iſrael dayes liffe ̄ wos veray prophet god ij kynges anoyntet saul fyrſt ̄ dauid samuell alone moyſes ar red thei prayed ther enmys old teſtament thys samuell saull dyuerſe opynions iſodyr ſayth samuell saul ruled iſrael xl yere ioſephus viij boke maſter ī hyſtories ſayn samuel iuge xij yere aloon aft er hym ſaul regne xx yere plura vide prio regum aſcanius vij kyng ytaly wos ſon eneas beldit cite albion ̄ wos cald kyng albano rum ¶thys aſconyus got siluiꝰ viij kyng italy wycch ſiluius fadir vn brute kyng bretan called englond leef kyngꝭ italy bot litill nobull thynges tyll cōmen romulꝰ ̄ remꝰ rome wos bilded ſhall tho kyngꝭ cū yane ꝓcede cronicls albion ye may ſe englond fyrſt began albion englōd wich boke namly maade venis padua wor bylded bowte tyme reſudw troyans homere gret poete bowte tyme wos wyche wrotte fened gloriuſli mony leſyng ¶incipit regnum britanie nunc dict anglia ¶afor yt ſpeke brute ſhall ſhewed ye lōde englōd wos fyrſt namd albiō ̄ c̄cheſō vos ſo namit nobull land sirrie ther wos nobull kyng myghty ̄ mā gret renōe wos called diecliſian yt wel ̄ wortheli gou er ned ̄ ruled thurgh noble chiualri ꝯquered landes hym ſo almoſt kynges world hym entēdāt hit fell thꝰ diocliſian ſpouſed gētill damiſell wos wōd er fair emes dought er labana ſhe loued hym reſon wold ſo gat vpō xxxiij doughtres wich eldeſt wos called albine ̄ thees damiſelles whan comē vn age bicomen ſo fair wos vōder wher diocliſian anōe let make aſompnyng ̄ cōmaunded lettres kynges helden hym ſhold cum certain day lett er cōteyned make riall feſt ¶at wich day thider cōen ̄ brought hem amirallis prince ̄ duke nobull chiualrie feſt wos rialy arayed ther leued ioye ̄ myrthe ynough wos wond er wit befeell thus diocliſian thought marie doughtres among altho kynges tho ſolempnite ̄ ſo ſpakene ̄ ded albine eldeſt doughter ̄ hir ſuſtres richely maried vn xxxiij kynges lordes gret honour ̄ pouer ſolempnyte ſolempnite wos done eu er kyng toke wyf lad ther cōtre ̄ ther maad hem quenes befell thus afterward dame albine bicome ſo ſtoute ſo ſterne ſhe told lytell pris lord hym ſcorne deſſpyt wolde nat done butt ſhe wold haue hir owne dyuerſe matres hir ſuſtres euerychone bere ſo euel ayenſt ther lordes wondyr wytt moch thought ther huſbondes nought ſo hy ꝑage comen ther fadre tho kynges ther lordes wold haue chaſtized fair maner vpon loue frendſhipp ſhold amend ther lith er ꝯdycions wos nought diden ther wyll ī thyng liked poer wher tho xxxiij kyngꝭ vpon tyme often time beten ther wyfes wened wold amended ther tatches ther wilkednes bot ſoche cōdicions fair ſpeche warnyng didden wors betynges eft ſones mochel wers wher kyng wedded albine wrot tach ꝯdicions wyf • albin letter ſent diocliſion hir fadre whē kyngꝭ herd albines lord ſent lett er diocliſian anone ſent lettres enſeled ther ſeales ꝯdicions tach ther wyfes ¶when kyng diocliſian ſaw herd ſo many playntes doughtres wos ſore aſhamed become wond er angre wroth toward doughtres thought bothe nyght day yf tho myght mend ſo miſded anone ſent lettres vn xxxiij kynges ſhold cū hym bring hem wyfes eu er ychone certane day wold ther chaſtiſe hem ther wikkedneſſe yf myght maner wiſe kyngꝭ comen tyme day tho wos ſette bitwene hym kyngꝭ diocliſian vnd er ſong moche honour ̄ maad ſolēpne feſte al vnd er lordſhipp ̄ thrid day aft er ſolēpnite kyng diocliſian ſent aft er xxxiij doughtres ſhold cum ̄ ſpeke hym ī hys chambre ̄ war come ſpake vn ther wikkednes ̄ ther cruelte ̄ ſpitueſly hem reꝓued vndernam ̄ hem ſaid yf wold nat chaſtiſed ſhold loue leſe eu er lady herden comē abaſſhed gretli aſchamed ther fadre ſaid wold make amendes ſo deꝑted ther fadres chambre dame albine wos eldeſt ſuſter lad hem hir chambre tho made void wer theryn ſo lefe wos among hem ſhe hir ſuſtres yfere tho ſayd albine faire ſuſtres wel know kyng fadre v hath reproued ſhamed deſpyſeed encheſone make v obedient vn owr houſbandes certes ſhall neu er while leue ſith come hier kyngꝭ blod myn houſbond ̄ whan ſhe thꝰ ſaid hir ſuſtres ſaid ſame ̄ tho ſaied albine full well wot fair ſuſtres owr houſbandes plened vn fader vpō v wherfor hath v thꝰ ſoule reproued ̄ deſpiſed wherfor ſuſtres counſell nyght houſbandes bene bedde one aſſent cutten hir throtes ̄ may bene pee hem ̄ better moo doo thing vnder fadres power ower ell anone ladis conſented ̄ grāted thys cōſell ̄ nyght wos cōyn lordd ̄ lady went bedde ̄ anone ther lordes ſlepe cutte heir houſbondes throtes ̄ ſo flow diocliſian kyng fadre herd thing bicome hugeli wroth ayenſt doughtres ̄ anōe wold hem haue brenet ¶but al baron ̄ lordes ſirrie coūceilled ſo doo ſuche ſtretnes owne doughtres bot onli ſhold voyde lond eu er ſo neu er ſhuld com ayene ſo dyde ¶and diocliſian wos ther fadre anōe cō maunded gone ſhypp ̄ deliu er ed hem vitailles half yere whan wos done ſuſtren went ſhip ̄ ſailed forth ī ſee bitoke ther frendes appolyn wos ther god· ſo long thee ſailed ſee till laſt come ̄ arreued ī yle wos wylderneſſe ̄ dame albion wos come lond ̄ hir ſuſtres thys albine went freſt forth ſhypp ſaied hir ſuſtres moche ꝙ ſhe oldeſt ſuſter cōpany ̄ fyrſt land haue takē ̄ moche o nam albine lond called albiō aft er myn name ̄ anōe al hir ſuſtres grāted hir good wyll tho vēt al ye ſuſtres ye ſhip tokē lond albion hir ſuſter cald ther went vp ̄ downe fonde nether mā ne womā ne child wyld beſtes diuerſe kyndes ther vitalles war diſpended thei failled fedde wyth herbes ̄ frutes ſeſon yere ſo leued beſt myght aftee token fleſſh dyuerſe beſtes bycame wonder fat ſo deſired mannys compane mānys kynde hem failled hete woxen wonder coragious kynd ſo deſired mānys companie eny othyr ſolace myrthe whan deuel ꝑceuyd went dyuerſe contreys nōme bodi eir likyng nature ſhad men come lande albion lay thoo wymē ſhad tho nature vpon conſaued ̄ broght forth geantys wich one wos called gogmagog langherigan ſo wer named diuerſe name nad maner come forth wer borne horrible geantes albion duelled caues ī hylles ther wyll londe albion lyked vn tyme brut arriued come totnes wos yle albion ther brute conquered ſkomfited thes geantes aboue ſayd ¶here geneth brut goten ſlewe fyrſt moder fader conquered albion named bretan owne name called englond name engiſt ſaxonie thys brute cam bretan bowte xviij yeer hely knaw nobull cite greet troy theer wos nobull knyght man grete pouer wos called eneas cite troy loſt deſtroed thurgh grece eneas al meyne fled then comeī lumbardy tho wos lord gou er nour lond kyng wos called latyne nother kyng ther wos wos called turocelyne ſtrongli wered vpō kyng latyne often tymes hym moche harme whē kyng latyne herd eneas comen vnd er feng hym wyth mochel honour hym helde moche herd hym wiſt well wos nobull knyght worthy hys body ̄ hiy dedes eneas helpet kyng latyne ī ̄ ſhortly tell ſo well ſo worthely ſlew turocelyne ̄ diſcomfited hym ̄ pepull al wos done kyng latyne yaf lond wos turocelinis thys noble man eneas mariage lauyne doughter moſt faire creature man wiſt ſo lyued geder ioye myrthe dayes theyr lyfes tyme aſconyus ſon eneas wedded wyfe vpō hyr begat ſon wos called silueyn ̄ ſilueyn whan colde ſum reſun man vn wittyng fadre yenſt wyll acquentyd hym damyſell wos coſyn lauyne wos kyng latynes dougter quene wos eneas wyfe brought damyſell wyth chylde whon aſcanius fad er wiſt anone let enquere wiſeſt maſters gretteſt klerkes chyld damiſey ſhold bring forth anſuered ̄ ſayed ſhe ſhold bring ofrth ſon ſhold kyll bothe fadre alſo modre ſo moder dyed beryng hym whan chyld wos borne fad er let calle hym brute maſters ſiyd ſhold doo moche harme ̄ ſorow mony dyuerſe place ſhold come gret honour worſhyp kyng aſcanius dyed god wold silueyn ſon reſaued lond made hym wonderly well beloued amonges pepull whan brute thatt wos siluenus ſon wos xv yere olde went vpon day wythe fadre play ̄ ſolace ̄ brute ſhold ſhote vn hert hys harew myſhapped glaced ſo ther brutkel led fad er ¶how brute wos dreuen lond helde hym grece myſchance befell pepull lond made ſorow ynowgh war ſore angreyd encheſon therof driuen brute oute lond wold ſuffer hym amonges ſaugh myght ther bide went then grece ̄ ther fond vijm men lynage ̄ kynred troy wor comē gret blode ſtori telleth men womē ̄ child wich wer holden thraldom ̄ bondage kyng pandras grece deth achilles wos bitrayed ̄ ſlayn troy thys brute wos wonder fayr man ſtrong huge age glad cheyr ſembland ̄ alſo worthy body wos wellbeloued emonges pepule kyng pandras herde ſpeke goodnes condicions anone made hym duell hym ſo brute bicome wond er priue ̄ moch beloued kyng ſo long tyme brute duelled kyng ſo laſt troy brute ſpakyn gedre kynred lynage ̄ acquantance ther plened vn brute ther ſorow ther bondage mony ſh • me ye kyng pandros done ̄ brute ſayn vpon tyme ye ben lord linage ̄ ſtrong man myghty ye ou • captayn lord ̄ gou er nour ̄ wyll cume mē commandmentes done maner thinges bryng ye v oute wrecchitnes bandage ̄ wil fyght wyth kyng trouth wt ye grace gret god ſhall hym ouercome ſhall make kyng lond done homage ̄ ſhall holde euermore brute tho gret pite ther bondage brought yn preuely went hem kynges court tho troy wē ̄ put wodis montaygens helde ſent vn kyng pandros ſhuld yeue leu ſauely wend lond wold longer duelle bondage kyng pandras wax tho ſore annoyd tho ſwore wold ſlae eu er ychone ordeneyd grett pouer went towardes feght brute men manli defended ferſly foughten kylled al kynges men none aſcaped token kyng ̄ hym helde priſon ordeyned counſell bi tweyn mygth done ̄ ſū ſaid ſhuld put deth ſū ſaid ſhuld exiled lond ſū ſaid ſhuld brent ¶and tho ſpake wyſe knyght called mempris ſaid brute tho troy yf kyng pādras wold yelde hym haue lyfe councell yeue vn brute duke ſoferayne doughter gennogen wyfe mariage hyr hondreth ſhippes wel araied hys treſour gold ſiluer corne wyne moch o nedeth haue thyng go oute lond ̄ ordayn v land elles ne none kynred comen v ſhall neuer haue pee lond amonges grece haue ſlayn ſo mony ther kynghtes frendes euermore contake ſhold amonges v brut tho folke conſented well counſell thyngꝭ tolden kyng pādras hee haue lyfe graunted moch axid none yaf vn brute gennogen douter wyfe hūdreth ſhippes o myche o neded vitalles o befor wos ordenyd brute tho toke wife men ſoke lond grece went vn ſee wynd wedre ther wyll com thrid day ile wos called lorgres brute anone ſent mē lond aſpye man er contre found nold cite al waſted ̄ forlet na therynne nether mā ne woman ne thyng duelling ī mydell cite founden old tempull feier lady yt wos called diane goddeſſe ̄ comē ayene vn brut told hym ſeyn found cōſelled hym gone doo ſacrifice vn dame dian ſhe woned yef anſuer thyng yt eu er men prayed hir ̄ namli vn yt hir honoured wt ſacrifice brut wēt yt ymage ̄ ſayd diane noble goddeſt lady yt thyng haſt myght ̄ ī thy pouer wyndes water wodes feldes ̄ al thyng world ̄ man er beſtes yt ther ī ben make prayer yt ye cōcell ̄ tell wher ī place ſhall haue counabull duellyng ̄ pepull ther ſhall make ī honor welfaier tempyll nobull wher ī ye ſhall eu er honoured done praer diane anſuerd ī man er brute ꝙ ſhe go euē forth thy wey ou er ſee ī fraunce toward weſt ̄ ther ye ſhall find ile yt called albion yt ile bicompaſſed ye ſee mā may cū therī bot bene ſhippes ī yt lond wer wōed geantes bot ſo bot wyldernes lond deſtenyed ̄ ordant yow pepull ¶how coryn becōe brute mā ̄ kīg goffar wos diſcōfid brute hade anſuere diane goddeſſe anōe let ancres wynd vp ſayled ī high ſee ̄ whē ̄ men ſailed xx dayes mo fond faſt beſide coſt ſee thouſand mē lynage kynred troy ther ſouerayne ̄ ther maſt er called corin whan brute wiſt whennes weer tho toke moch ioye ī ſhippis ̄ led forth hym corin ther becōe brute mā hym dyd homage ̄ ſo long ſailled forth ī yt ſe till comē ī gaſcoyne anōe arriued ī hauen liegers ther duellid viij dayes reſt ̄ ther ſayles amende ther wos nede tydyngꝭ ſone come kīg goffar lord lond yt moch pepill ſtrange lond arreuid lond hauen liegers wherfor hee ſore angreyd anoyde come arriued lond lyſens leue anone ordeyned hym gret pouer dryue brute ſhend pepull bout ſo kyng goffar wos diſcomfited pepull hym ſelf flede fraunce ther ſeke helpe ſocour ¶and tyme regned fraunce xij kynges xi aſſemaled gret pouer help goffar fight ayenes brute goffar duelle fraunce halfe yere mene tyme goffar fraunce brute hys companye deſtruyed lond gaſcoyne let take treſour kyng goffar ther let bryng ſhippes brute founden lond fair place couenabull theyr brute made faire caſtell ſtrong ¶when wos done kyng goffar come fro fraunce xi kynges hym brought xx men fyght wt brute compani brute vijm iijc men neuerthelees ij hoſtes mett gedre brute folke thorgh help hym ſelfe turyn coſyn ̄ corin well manly hym defended fought ſo tell lytell tym kylled fraunſhemen ijm mo anon tho alyue fled way ¶and batell turin brute coſyn ſlayn brute let enteer hym worthely whan ſpace ̄ leyſer caſtell made tho let call ſame caſtell tour cauſe name turin ther wos entyred yet day ther nobull cite c • lled tour kyng goffar wiſt turin wos deyd cō ayene men yaf ſtrong batell vn brute bot brute hys men ſo wery fighttyng myght longer endure bot meegre hym brute went ī caſtell men ̄ made yates faſt ſaue take conſell amonges brute corin yaf counſell ordeyned corin priualy ſhold goo oute buſſh hym wod til morne mornyng whan brute ſhold fight enymys corin ſhold cum folke one ſide ſla harme myght amornyng dauyng day brute went caſtell ̄ faught enmys ferſly defendid bot ī litell tyme brute folke ſlew viijc gofears men come corin buſſhement ſmot ground compani wold ſtond byed ſo kyng goffar comp • nye war deſcomfited faſt gun fle brute corin ther companye ferſly perſoed kylled moo fleyng batell ¶and maner brut victorie nertheles brute made moch ſorow coſyn turin ther wos ſlayn alſo loſt men ſay vijc xv wich nobulli let entier ſome caſtell tour ther wher entyred turin coſyn ¶how brute arriued totneſſe ile albion batell wos tuix corin gogmagog wos done brute wold longer ther duell fight leſe mo pepull kyng goffarus pepull mygth euery day encreſſe mo mo bruttes laſſenned therfor toke men went vn ſee wynd weder ther fyfte day afterwaard arriued hauen totneſſe comen ile albion ther nether man woman ſtori tels fond geautes thei woned hillis caues ̄ brut ſaw lond wos fayr likyng wos good alſo pepull diane goddeſſe hym behight ther wos brute wonder glad late aſſemble vpon day folke make ſolempnie ſacrifice gret feſt honour reuerens diane goddeſſe wich counſell firſt cū lond whan thar ſolempnite done vpon day ſat ther mete ther come vppon ſodanly xxx geantes kylled brute men xxx brute men anone ſturten vp fought wt geantes kylled euerychone bot one called gogmagog maſter geantes wos ſtronger heyr ony brute keped hym encheſon ſhold wreſtyll corin brute mā wos gretter hyer ony brute men thee gredyl ſted vpward ¶gogmagog corin vndir toke ther wreſtyll ſo gedre went wreſtilled long tyme laſt gogmagog held corin ſo faſt brake ij ribbbes ſide wherfor corin wos ſore angri ther toke gogmagog betwix armes keſt hym doune vpon roche ſo gogmagog brak peces ̄ ſo died euell deth therfor place called yit vn day faut gogmagog brute yaf cuntre vn corin ther corin called name cornwalle men called cornwailles ſo ſhuld men contre called eu er contre duelled corin mē thee made tounes ̄ houſes ̄ inhabited lond ther wyll ¶how brute made london called lond britane ſcotland albyne walis cambir brute mē wēt forth ̄ ſaw aboute dyuerſe place wher yt myght fynd good place couenabull yt myght make cite hym folke soo laſt come fayr riuer called temys ther brute biganne fair cite let calle new trey mynd remembrance gret troy wich place theer linage comin ¶and brute let fell doune wodes let erye ſawe landes let maw doune medoys ſuſtenā ce alſo pepull departed lond ſo euerychon haad parte certayn place duell brute let call lond bretene owne name folke let call breton brut gotē wife gennogen iij ſonnys war worthy dedes fyrſt wos called lotrin ye ſecund albanac thred kambar brute bore croune cite new troy xx yere aft er ye tyme cite made ther made lawes ye breton holden brut wos wonderly well belouyd emōg men brute ſonnys alſo loued wonderly well gedeer ¶and whan brute ſought lond length ̄ alſo ī breyd found land iuned bretane yt wos north land brute yaf albanac ſon let call albanie aft er name yt called scotland ¶and brute fond contre toward weſt yaf yt cambar ſon let call camber name cald walys whan brute regned xx yere ſayd died cite new troy ¶how lotrin wos brute ſon entroed wyth moch honour gouerned lond well worthely brute regned lotrin ſon wos ſecund kyng bretane wich gane regne ſecund yere samuell lotrin wos croned kyng moch ſolemnite land bretane whan wos croned kīg albanac cambar ij brether went gayn ī ther contre ther liued mekyll honour worſhyp lotrin ther brother regned kyng gouerned well wyſeli wos good man wonderly well beloued land fell ſo albanac duelled owne lond mekell hoonour worſhipe come kynge humbar hunlond grett pouer ariued albine wold haue conquered land gone vpon kīg albanac hym kylled batell ¶when albanac wos ſlayne pepull yt land fled vn lotrin tould hym wos kyng bretan brother wos ſlayn prayed hym help ſocour venge hys brother deth ¶lotrin ther anone let aſſemble bretans kent douer derewent norfolk southfolke keftefen lyndeſſey war enſembled ſped faſt ward ther enmys yef batell lotrin ſent camber brother ſhuld come vn hym thee pouer myght make hym help ſo good wyll ſo come gedres toke ther way preualy go ſeche humbar wher myght hym fynde ¶and ſo befell yt humbar wos ſide wat er yt wos gret reuer folke hym diſport ther come lotrin cambir brother ther folke ſodanly ony wiſt ¶and whan humber ſaw cū wos ſore adrad moch men wiſt afore alſo vn arayed anone humber drede lepyd ī wat er drenched hym ſelf ſo died men wer ſlayn none aſcaped thefor water called humbar euermore ſhall cauſe kyng humbar ther drenched lotrin went ſhippis toke ther gold ſiluer o moch fand vn hym ſelf pylfre gaf vn folke hoſt fond one ſhippis fair damyſell wos kyng humbars dought er ſhe wos called eſtrild ¶and whan lotrin ſaw hir toke hir hym hir fayrnes▪ hir wos ouer taken loue ̄ wold haue wedded hir tidīges come corin anone thought aueuge hym vpon lotrin far o mych lotrin made counand ſpouſe corins douhhter called guentolen corin haſt went hym vn new troy thꝰ ſayed lotrin certes quod ye reward full euell paynes haue ſuffred mony tymes brute fadre therfor ſen ſo wyll uenge vpon drew fauchon hight wold haue ſlayn thys lotrin kyng damiſell went tweyn made acorded ī man er lotrin ſhold ſpouſe guendolen wos corins doughter ſo lotryn nertheles whan ſpouſed guentolen corins doughter preualy come eſtrilde brought hir wich chyld ̄ gate vpon hir doughter wych called abren ¶and hit befell ſo anone corin dyed deid lotrine ſoke guendolen wos wyfe made eſtrilde quene ther guentolen wyffe went then gret ire wroth vn cornwaill ther ſeiſed lond hir owne hond moche ſhe hir fadres eyr ſhe vnder toke feautes homage al men lond afterward aſſembled gret hoſt gret pouer men venged vpon lotrin hir lord hym come yaf hym ſtrong batell ther wos lotrin hir hoſband ſlayn men diſcomfited v yere regne guentolen let take eſtrile abram hir doughter bynd b • h • nd ̄ fete ̄ keſt bothe water ſo drenched wherfor water euer called abram thee name damyſell eſtrildis doughter englyſſh men calleth water ſeuern walſh men callis abram vn day ¶and done guentolen let croune hir quene lond ̄ gou er ned lond full well wyſely vn tyme madan hir ſon lotrin goten vpon hir xx yere age maulyn mempris brod er maulyn ſtr • ue faſt thee lond ̄ mēpris begone regne xxxv yere dauid encheſō yt wos eldeſt ſon wold haue lōd maulyn woldnat ſuffre hym ſo yt toke day loue ̄ acorde ¶and day mēpris let kyll brother thurgh treſon hym ſelf afterward held lond anōe let croune hym kyng regned aft er became ſo lither mā deſtroid ī ye mē lond laſt bicame ſoo wikked ſo lecherous ſoke owne wyfe vſed ſynne ſodomye wherfo almyghti god wos gretly diſpleſyd wrothe hym vpan hym toke vengeance cauſe wikkednes day went forth huntyng foreſt ther loſt men wos hym wiſt ſhold done ſo went vp doune aſſay wich hem loued hym moſt ̄ beſt ſhe loued beſt ſhold beſt maried axed fyrſt doughter well ſhe hym loued ſhe aunſuerd ̄ ſaied better hir lyffe certes quod hir fadre gret loue axed ye ſecūd doughter moch ſhe hym loued ſhe ſaied paſſing creaturs world ꝑ foy quod hir fad er axe tho axed thrid doughter mych ſhe hym loued certes fad er quod ſhe ſuſtres haue told gloſyng wordes ſo ſhall tell trouth loue o aught loue fad er bring c er tayn loue ſhall tell moche ye bene worth ſo moch ſhall ye loued ¶the kyng hir fader went ſhe ſkorned hym become wond er wroth ſuore heuen ̄ erth ſhe ſhold neuer haue good hym bot doughtres yt loued hym ſo moch ſhold well auaunced maried fyrſt dought er maried maugles kyng ſcotland ſecond marid hanemos erle cornewaell ſo ordined ſpak bitwene ſhold depart reame bitwene two deth kyng leir ther fad er ſo cordeill yongeſte doughter ſhold nothyng haue lond cordeill wos wond er fair good condicions maners yt thee kyng fraunce agampe herd hir ſpeke ſent kyng leir hir father haue hir vn wyfe prayed hym therof kyng leir hir fader ſent hym word departed land yeffen vn two doughtres ſaied ſaied land wher wyth hir mary ¶and whā agampe kyng fraunce herd aunſuar ſent anone yene leir ſayed axed thyng withhir bot hir clothyng hir body anone kyng leir ſent hir ou er ſee ye kīg fraūce reſſaued hir moche worſhip ſolempnite hir ſpouſed made hir quene fraunce ¶how kyng leir wos driuen land thurgh folke ̄ cordeill yongeſt doughter helped ī nede thus befell afterward tho ij eldeſt daughtres wold bide tyll leir ther fad er wos deid wered vpon hym whilles wos liue hym moch ſorow ̄ ſham wherfor benōme hym holi ream bi twene deyned one ſhold haue kyng leir ſeiourne al liue tyme xl knyghtes ſquyers myght wurſhip fulli go ride whedd er wold ī contre hym liked play ſolace ¶so manacle kyng ſcotland kyng leir hym maner o boune ſaied half yere wer paſſed corneil wos eldeſt doughter quene scotland ſo noyed hym pepull anone ſhe hir lord ſpeke gedre wherfor knyghtis half ſquers hym wer gone nomo left wt bot xxx ¶and wos done leir bi gon make moch ſorow encheſon eſtate wos empeired ̄ men hym ſcorne deſpiet eu er wherfor wiſt done laſt thoght wold weind cornwaill rigan dought er come erle wife wos leirs dought er hym welcomed hym made moch ioye er dwelled wt xxx knyghtis ſquyers duelled ther ſcarſly xij month dought er hym weri companye hir lord ſhe hym gret ſcorne deſpitte ſo thatt xxx knyghtes brought vn x afterward v ſo left hym nomo ¶than made ſorow ynouh ſaied ſore wepyng allas euer come yt land ſaied yit better haue duelled fyrſt doughter anone went then fyrſt dought er g • ne bot anōe ſhe ſaw come ſhe ſuore god bi holi name moch ſhe myght ſhold haue nomo hym one knyght yf wold ther bied begon leir ayene wepe made moch ſorow ̄ ſaid tho ala long haue leued ſorow myſchefe fallen pooer ſū tyme wos rich bot haue frend ne kyn wyll ony good ¶but whē riche mē honoured worſhipped eu er mā hath ſcorne ̄ • ſpite wot well cordeill yongeſt doughter ſaied trought ſhe ſaid moch ſo mych ſhuld beloueid good ſo long wos loued honoured rich two doughtres gloſed tho thei ſet litell pris ſoth told cordeill bot wold nat beleue ne vndiyrſtond therfor let hir go fro thyng ſet litell pris wote neuer done ſith ij doughtre haue thus diſſaiued ſo moch loued moſt nedes ſeche hir land lyghly let hir gone fro reward yeftes ſhe ſaid ſhe loued mich o ſhe aght loue hir fad er maner reſon tho ſhold haue axed hir nomore tho wiſe behightyn thurgh tber fals ſpeche haue deſauid maner leir long tyme began make mone laſt ſhop ſee paſſed ouer fraunce aſked aſpied wher quene myght fonde men told hym wher ſhe whan come cite ſhe preualy ſent ſquyer vn quene tell hyr hir fadre wos comen hir gret neides ¶and ſquyer come quene told hir euery dele hir ſuſtres begynnyng vn ye end· cordeill quene anone toke gold ſiluer plente toke ſquyer counſell ſhold go bere vn hir fadre ſhold go c er tan cite hym aray waſſhen cum ayene hir ̄ bring hym honeſt companye knyghtes xl leyſt ther menye ſhold ſend hir lord kyng ſayne comen ſpeke dought er hym ſeen ſo ¶and whan kyng quene • thei com mych honour hym roſſayued ye kīg fraunce tho let ſend thurgh reame cōmanded mē ſhold bene al entendent kyng leir quens fadre maner thynges war vn hym ſelf kīg leir duelled ther moneth tolde kyng quene doughter two eldeſt doughtres hym ſerued agampe anone let ordeyne gret hoſt fraunce men ſent bretan leir quenes fad er comquer land ayene kyngdom cordeill alſo come hir fader bretane haue reame hir fadres deth anone went ſhip paſſed ſee come bretan foughten felous ſcomfited kylled ̄ tho lond ayene aft er leued iij yere held ream pee afterward died ̄ cordeill doughter hym let ētyr mekell honour leceſtre anno mūdi iiijm iijc xlix et an̄ xpī yere ¶how morgan conedag wos nevus cordeil werred wpon hir put hir hir preſon kyng leir wos deid cordeill yongeſt doughter regned x yere oſias kyng iuri aft er hir ragned conedage xv yere oſias cordeill yt wos leir yongeſt doughter aft er deth hir fader ye lōd v yere meyn tyme died hir lord agampe kyng fraunce aft er deth ſhe left wedo ther come morgan conedag wer cordeill ſuſtre ſonnys hir enmite moch ther aunt ſhold haue land bitweyn ordeyned gret pouer vpon hir wered gretly neuer reſt till hir taken ̄ put hir vn deth tho morgan conedag ſeyſed ale land ̄ deꝑtid bitwene held xij yere▪ tho xij yere gone ther bi gane bitwene gret debate ſo yt wered ſtrongly gedre yfere eu er moch diſeſe morgan wold haue land fro beyond humbet conedage held come ayenſt hym ſtrong pouer ſo morgan durſt abide fled awey wale conedage purſued hym ̄ toke hym kylled hym tho come conedage ayen ſeyſed lond hand held ̄ regned xxxiij yere tho died ̄ lieth new troy ¶and cauſe mater contennys moſt comediuſly ged er kynges bretan called enegland tyme certenly knawyn tyme world thes kynges foloyng regned therfor ſhall geder tyll comen vn guentolen kyng bretan called englond ¶how reignold yt wos cōadag ſon regned aft er fad er ̄ ī tyme reyned blode iij dayes ī tokennyng gret deth conedage regned reignold ſon wiſe knyght hardy curtes well ̄ nobully gouerned lond wonder well made hym beleued man er folke tyme rayned blode leſted iij day god wold ſone ther come gret deth pepull hoſtes nombre pepull foughten tyll myghty god therof toke mercy pytty tho gan ceſe reignold regned xxij yere ̄ died lieth yorke ¶how gorbodian regned pee wos reignold ſon aft er died lieth yoik reignold wos gonedag ſon rened gorbodian wos reignold ſon xv yere ̄ died lieth yorke ¶how gorbodian ij ſonnys one ſlew haue heritage ydoyne ther modre killed thatt wherfor land deſtruied gorbodian deid ij ſōnys yt become ſtout proude eu er wered ged er ye land ̄ one called ferres ̄ porres ferres wold haue ye land ye woldnat ſuffre ferres felon hert thought thurgh treſō ſlee brother preualy wēt ī fraunce ther abode wt kīg syward till vpō tyme whan come ayene ̄ fought wt brother ferres ful euell happed tho ſlayn fyrſt whē ydoyne ther mod er wiſt yt porres deid ſhe made gret ſorow encheſō yt ſhee loued hym thē ̄ thought kyll preualy ¶and preuely ſhe come hir ſon vpō nyght wt ij knyues therwith cut throt ye bodi alſo ī ſmall peces herd eu er ſuche curſed mod er yt kyllid hir owne handes hir ſon long tyme aft er laſt reproue ̄ ſhame mod er yt encheſun one ſon ſhe murdred ̄ ſo loſt bothe ¶how iiij kynges courtaſly held breten ther name ye ſhall heyr ij brethern war deid nad left behynd nother ſon ne dought er ne nōe kynred yt myght haue ye heritage ̄ moch ye ſtrangeſt mē driuē ſcomfited ye febleſt ̄ toke ther londes ſo eu er cōtre gret ̄ ſtrife vnd er emong thynges ther amōges ī ye contre ou er come tho ̄ thurgh ther myght ̄ ſtrenght tuke ye londes ̄ eu er tok c er tayn cōtre ī contre let call hī kyng ̄ con thē cald scater ̄ wos kīg ſcotland yt wos called dawaliere ̄ kīg loegers ̄ land wos lotrins thatt wos brute ſon thrid called rudac kyng walis iiij called cloten ̄ kīg cornewaill cloten ſhold haue land reſon cauſe thar wos mā wiſt nōe ſo right heir o butt ſtrongeſt ſet litell bi hem wer leſſe eſtate therfor clotē nomore lād amōg hem cornwaill ¶of kyng donebant clotens ſon wone lond cloten ſon yt called doneband deth fadre come hardy man fair curteys ſo paſſed kingꝭ fairnes ̄ wortheneſſe none knyght wiſt well fader lyued moſt rightfull heir lōd ſhold haue reſon kynges moch ſtrength toke hym lond ¶and aft er ward doneband ordeyned gret pouer conquered fyrſt land logeris aft er wold haue conquered land ſcotland wailles scat came mē yaf batell rudac come ayene walys men help hym ſo fell rudac wos kylled alſo scater ī playn bataill ſo doneband victorie conquerid land well maintined pee quiete neuir befor ſo well mayntined ¶how doneband friſt kyng euer bore croune gold bretan thys doneband let make hym croune gold wered croune vpon hede neu er kīg bifore ordyened ſtatut man done neu er ſo moch harme myght comē tempull ther ſhold man hym myſdo gone ther ſafete pee aft er goin lond cūtre hym pleſed owt ony harme▪ ony man ſett hond vpon hym ſhold leſe life doneband made toun malmeſberi toune alſo viſe regned well worthely xl yere died lyeth new troy ¶how bronne belin deꝑted bitweyn lond deth doneband ther fadre twix aft er yt doneband wos deid ſōnys yt deꝑted land bitweyn ther fad er ordeyned ſo yt belyn eldeſt ſon ye land bretan humbar ſouthward brotherbrenne land humber scotlād moch belī better part brenne therfor waxed wroth wold haue lond ̄ belyn brother wold greunte hym nomore wherfor cōtake roſo betweyn two brenne yonger brother myght ne ſtrenght yen belyn ̄ therfor brenne thurgh cōſell hys folke wēt fro then ī norwey kyng olſinges prayd help ſocour cōquer ye lond vpō belin brother vpon connaund wold haue doughter wiſe ̄ kyng olſinges grāted belyn anōe brother wos go norway ſeyſed ī hond land northhūberlōd ̄ toke caſtelles ̄ let arayed keped coſtes ſee brenne ſhold arriue ī ſied yt war take ¶the kyng ol ſinges let aſſemble gret hoſt deliu er yd doughter brenne pepull yt ordeyned ̄ damiſell samye long tyme loued kyng wos called gutlaghen hym ſhe told hir counſel̄ yt brenne ſhold hir haue hir lede hym eu er ſo ſhold leſe hir ſhe myght ſake brenne whan gutlagh herd tydīg lay aſpy brenne mony ſhippis myght haue ſo two fletes metten gedre long tyme faught ſo brenne turned ayene wer diſcomfited kyng gutlagh toke samye put hir ſhyppe brenne ſham fulli fled then man diſcomfitied ¶and kyng gutlagh wold haue went owne contre ther come vpon hī ſych gret tempeſt ·v dayes laſted ſo thurgh tempaſt wos driuen ī breten iij ſhippis mo ̄ tho keped coſtes ſee toke gutlagh samye folke preſented belyn ̄ belyn put ī preſon ¶how belyn drofe land kyng gutlagh dē marke samye hit long brenne come ayene gret nauye ſent brother belyn yt ſhold yeld ayene land wife folke caſtels alſo el wold deſtru land belyn drad thyng h • malas ̄ wold thyng aft er ſaid wherfor brenne come folke fought wt belyn brenne diſcōfited ̄ folke ſlayn ̄ ſelfe fled xij mē ī fraunce belyn yt wos brennes brother wēt yorke toke counſell myght kynd gutlagh kyng gutlagh profered come man hold land hym yeldyng bi yere pound ſilu er eu er ̄ ſikerneſſe cōuenyant holden gutlagh ſhold bring hym good hoſtages ̄ ſhold homage folke yit ſhold ſwere vpon boke ſhold neuer broken ne ſaled ¶belyn tho bi counſell folke grāted hym axyng ſo gutlagh become man belyn vnder toke homage oth ̄ bi writyng ſame conuenantes vpon thes couenants kyng gutlagh toke ſamie folke ̄ went then turned ayene denmarke eu er mor aft er couenants holden truage payed till tyme honelus kyng denmark alſo land thurgh wife gildeburgh ſpouſed ſho wos ye righ heir lond ¶this belin duelled tho pee worſhipfully hym held among baron made iiij· riall weyes one eſt weſt called watling ſtret northe vn ſouth wos called ikelme ſtrete ij weyes made ī boſſyng thurgh land called foſſe foſſedike maintened well good lawes doneband fadre made ordened tyme befor ſaied ¶how cordment wos made twene brenne belī thurgh cornewen ther mod er brenne belenꝰ brother long tyme duellid fraunce ther conquered gret lordſhyp thurgh mariage wos duke burgoyne thurgh dought er duke fewyn ſpouſed wos right heir thee lond brenne ordeyned gret pouer folke alſo fraunce come land fight belī brother belin come ayens hym gret poer bretōs ̄ wold tho haue yeuen hym batell ther mother cornewyn tho liued herd brother wold haue deſtruyed othir went bitwene hir ſonnys made accorded wt moch peyne ¶so laſt tho ij bretheren mych blis went gedre new troy called london ̄ ther duelled yere toke ther counſell go ̄ conquer fraunce ̄ ſo brent tounes deſtrued land bothe length breyd kyng fraunce yaf batell poer wos ouer comen yaf truage vn belin brother ¶and wēt forth vn rome conquered rome lumbardy germani toke homage feaute erles baron al come land bretan duelled ther breton ioye reſt tho made brenne toune briſtowe ſith went ouer lordſhipp thee gretteſt world wich incredebyll thyngꝭ ar wretē wos ſo ſtrong ī nyght wos deſtrued myght ſhewed power god wich power bot ſparke ̄ duſt ſaied ſothe wos incredabull made man handis dethruyed man galowis fettres ̄ manyclys chynes colers ſych ther gret pride cruelnes god ſuffrid myſchefe man er wyſe ſhall bi ſhewed ¶he ſon ſame name wich ſon dofouled worthy manys wiffe thei called hym collatyn wyffe wos called lucre tarquynꝰ yt wos ſeuynth kīg ſon foor ſaied come vn ladyes howſe abſent hir howſbond ſoꝑ ̄ logīg wer ſlepe roſe ſuerde hond ̄ wt ſtrengthe feir rauychid womā whē wos go ye nexte day aft er ſhe ſend vn hir fadre hir houſbond ſhe gret kynne thus ſhe ſaied vn ¶this kyngꝭ ſon come heder o freynd myſtriſt thus defilyt chaſtyte loſt name eu er hir frendys ſe hyr wepe petuyſly cōplayn ̄ cōforthid hir o cold ſaied wos velany vn hir wos ayenes hir ſhe anſwered ſayd· yet ſhall ther neu er woman excuſe hir bi lucre thou ſhe cōſentyd thys deed yet ſhall ſhe dye wt payn deed wt word ſhe knyffe redi vnd er hir mātill wich ſhe ſmote hir ſelff hert cruelnes petuꝰ deth pepull rome roſe exiled kīg eu er ̄ ꝓgeny thꝰ ſeeſ ſit thes kynges rome ̄ neu er wos none ¶of gou er nan rome till emꝑours gan aftyr tyrant wos deid roman ordeyned yt ther ſhuld neu er kyng ī rome bot wold bi gou er ned fro yt forth bi conſules whē tho kīges regned cc yere xl made ſtatute yt ij conſules ſhuld choſen ſhuld goueren cite peepull cauſe thes tow wor choſen yf wold make exceſſe thee ſhuld gou er ne ther wos thyng obeyed bot yf cōſented alſo ſhuld ſtond ī ther dīgnite paſſyng yere cauſe dominacio • long tyme ſhuld vſurpe vpō wos righfull tyme empyre rome dilatid paſſyng xij myell ne lordſhipp paſſing xij myell fyrſt conſules yt wer made called luciū brutū thes two mē gret thīgꝭ ther tyme yet pepull bare heuy ther dominacion wher foor choſe man wich ſhuld haue auctorite thei clepeed hym dictator ¶in ſame tym ther wos gret diſcencion twix pepull ſenate wherfoor choſin tribunas wich war iuges ou er pepull ̄ defendit hem wrong ſayeth yſid dictator choſe laſted ·v yere tribunas war remeued euery yere ¶bot ye muſt vndir ſtond ye ſhall haue heir conſules namys yt gou er ned rome twix ſeſyng ye kynges beginyng emꝑours war long write ſpecially whē wer eu er yere new ſen yt oon man myght choſen ſo oft tyme red alſo endurynge ther gou er nance wer gou er nours rome vc yere ̄ lxvij moſt famus men thes ſhall reherſed aft er forme cronyclis o ſtond ī boke wos ychon aft er incipit hiſtoria libri eſdre anno mūdi iiijm vic lix et ante criſti natītatē vc xl zorobobell cōmandment god founded tempil ̄ made ꝑfite bot wos long vt pꝫ patet eſdre 6o aftir pepull ieruſalē come fro babulon thes ij ruyled iheſus hee preſt o gou er nour zorobobell duke thys maner gydyng kepid vn herodes tyme hee preſtis ſhuld principall dukis vnd er bot duke wos eu er tribe iuda propheſi iacob vnd er good gydyng preſtis rede pepull haue recedit fro varay truthe faythe afoor tyme iues kyngis mony tymes ran ydolatry eſdras preſt kynrad aron tyme excedid mē ī holynes throgh who gret wiſdō iues ſtait holpin cambiſes ſon ciri regned kyngdom perſa rum wich commaunded myghtili tempull ieruſalem ſhold bildid ayene fadre cōmandid ſhold byldid cambiſes made curſed iuge fleid hilt lyue ̄ mad ſon ſit fad er ſkyn thurgh drede ſhold drid falſhed iuge rightwiſli ¶this cambiſes mony namys holx ſcriptur boke eſdri artharxerſes aſſuorus hiſtoria iudith yt wasdoon vnd er hī called nabogodonoſor olifernes prince cheualry ſubdued mony landes lord laſt come vn bethelem ther wos ſlayn iudit woman vt pꝫ patet iuddith 2 et 13 ereneides regned perſis half yere darius regned perſes wich bi mocion zorobobell cōmaundid thee werke ye tēpull take ayene ̄ ꝯmaunded prince wiſe ſhuld let bot ſhuld help yt could vide plrā ī eſdre ho de ho tēpore ābiguū pp̄ diu er ſitatē docto rum circa annū mūdi iiijm vijc xxxiiij et an̄ xp̄i natī iiijc lxv abiuth ſon • zorobobell ye lyne criſt wos bowt tyme· foloyng vn ioſeph nothyng inſcriptur matheu euangeleſt nombris genologi therfor certayn tyme dewly cannot bi knaw ioachī wos biſſhop tī aft er ioſophꝰ wos called ioſedech vndir ieruſalem wos belded ayene vt dicit et ho idem pꝫ patet neemie 12 ccxliiij yere rome wos made thee roman ordyned ij cōſules ſteid ther kyng ye wich ſhuld gouerne yere aloin· leſt bi tariyng ſhuld proude yt ſhuld corec yf excedit errit brutus wos fyrſt conſuler lucius ſecund ̄ ther man called dictator nome office wych ſhuld go pepull ayens ther enmys titus puphius marcus conſules roman complayned gretli condecions conſules power put x men excedyng coſt comyn pepull eu er ych went like kyng need cauſed leue dygnite triſted neuer reſt wos ſo ſtrong ayens artharxerſes wos kyng perſa rum vnder whome eſdras come ieruſalem neemias wos butteler ſame kyng aft er ward ſent bylde walles ieruſalem xerſes rened aft er hī ij monethes segdianꝰ vij monethes hī lityll circa annū mūdi iiijm vijc lix et an̄ xp̄i natītatē iiijc xl eliac hym reherſed lyne criſt ī math po ſcriptur eſdras holy man conyug worſhipfully wos emong pepull thys man come fro babulō odyrr meued veray cherite went ayene bobulon myght wyn mo iſraell ſaaue ſawles bring home hym tyme repared law holy bokys wich caldes brent happy wittynes world left ſcriptur fond new litter lighter faccion wich thurgh holy goſt fulfilled come ayene ieruſalē gret multitude kynges preualeges ſhuld teche pepull yt law repayred ther died good age neemias hebru butler kyng artraxerſes lord commandment went babulon ieruſalem wher yaf xij yere ledīg pepull v yere gon repare yates wallis ieruſalem wich werke endit ij yere iiij monethes gret inpedimentes halfe pepul ſtoed armeid cite withſtond pepull odyr naciōns intendyng deſtruy part labured armes holdyng ton hond ſtonys wallis ī notobull odyr hond ſwoord ne vide plrā libo ſuo permenides pheloſophurs namly morall thynges war bowte socrates mathe primo bot nothyng dedes wreten ſcriptur elyaſib elyſaphat ſuccedid ioachym byſſhoppryke vt dicit euſebius et magiſter hiſtor camillus wos dictator rome whoes day myſcheuys playes wer ordand peſtelans ſhuld ſees rome thes playes sent auſtyn tretis delygently repreuyng falſhed goddis wich deſired pleſed ſych writch playes ſhamfully thes playes wer vſed naked men ̄ womē honeſt mē ne womē wold tho playes ne yet behold vide plura augꝰ de ciuitate dei darius nothus regned perſes xix yere plato thee diuyn pheloſopher ariſtotill diſcipull wos tyme nobull famus clerkis tytus quintius wos flumiordan aſke yene tribute yefen eſdra vij yere rent pp̄ ſabbā tre arſamꝰ ſuccedit hym regned yere darius ſon arſamy regned ꝑſes xxiiij yere darius wos myghty man bold wich aſked grekis tribute wos ariſtotiles moſt ſotell famuſt ppiloſophur leuyd tyme senocrate moſt chaſt pheloſophur tyme dyuers mo ¶bi cauſe kīgꝭ bretan next aft er leued ī peeſe moſt pte lytyl wretē therfor ſhall ſet ged er tyll cōmī caſſibulon kīg breton wich wos brother lud whan crombatrus deid regned guentholen yt wos ſō man good ꝯdicions ̄ welbeloued gouerned lond well wiſeli regned xxvi xere died lyeth new troy ¶how kyng seiſell regned well gouerned land guentholen guentholen regned ſon seiſſel well ̄ wortheli well gou er ned ye lōd fad er done befor regned xv yere died lieth new troy ¶how kymor regned seiſſell fader begat howan regned fader peeſe seiſſell regned ſon kymor well ̄ nobli xix yere peeſe afterhym regned howan hys ſon x yere died lieth ikaldoune ¶how kyng morwt died thurgh myſchaunce thurgh beſt howon regned marwith ̄ become ſo weked ̄ ſo ſterne tyll laſt gret vengeance come went vpon tyme ſee ſide mete gret beſt yt wos blake horibull hideus wened bene whale ſee bent arblaſt ̄ wold haue ſlayn beſt quarell myght ſmyte hym ſhot quarelles beſt anone come hym gret haſt hym deuored lyfe ſo died wickednes thurgh vengeaunce god regned ix yere ¶of grādobodiā yt wos morwith ſon yt made cāmbregge morwith wos deid bretens crosned grādobodian ſō ̄ grandobodian long tyme regned ī goodnes made tēpuls tounys grādobodiā made toune cambregge ̄ toune grauntham ̄ wos wel beloued rich poer honourd rich helped poer grandobodian iiij ſonnis arthogaile heſidur higamꝰ petitur regned xi yere died lieth new troy ¶of artogaill wos grādobodians ſon wos made kyng ̄ ſieth put doune wikkednes grandobodian regned ſon artogaill v yere become ſo wikked ̄ ſo ſterne yt briton wold ſuffre hym kyng put doun ̄ made heſidur brother kyng bi come ſo good ̄ merciabull men hym called kyng pytte ¶and whē regned v yere ſo grete pitte brother artogaill yt wos kyng ̄ anōe forſoke dignite ̄ toke brother croune ayene ̄ made hī kyng ayens britans ¶and afterward artogaill become ſo good cōdicion yt welbeloued ye land become ſo bonair fre right reſon man er men regned vi yere died lidth grantham ¶how heſidur wos made kīg aft er ye deth brether deth artogaill briton crouned tyme heſidur ij bred higamꝰ petitur gret ſpite ſcorne ordined help vpon kyng ther brother ſo toke hym put priſon ye ſecūd yere regne ̄ deꝑted land twix higamus leued vij yere ̄ tho petitur lond made toune pickering briton come toke heſidur priſon made hym kyng thrid tyme petitur deid bretās toke heſidur anoon ̄ made hym kyng thrid tyme tho regned īpees xiiij yere aft er died lieth karleill xxxiij kīgꝭ rened ī pee eche aft er od er raft ye deth heſidur deth heſidur regned xxxiij kīges ich aft er ī pee ̄ wt ony long tariyng ſhall tell thē long eche regned ſtori telleth ¶the fyrſt kyng tho xxxiij called gerbodia regned xii yere aft er regned morgan ij yere aft er rened cighnus vi yere ̄ aft er regned idwalan viij yere ̄ hym regned rohugo xi yere ̄ regned voghen xiij yere hym regned lond moch honoured gud folke tēpred amēded wikked folke lud loued duell troy ī place lond wherfor name new troy left tho wos cite called ludſtone name changed thurgh variance letter called london thyng ye wich herd bi drem ī dew ordir wos fulfilled wos likly hym yt ſhold ye ſame ꝑſō whō daniell ꝓpheſied ̄ yt toke hardynes fight wt darius kyng ꝑſa rum ſacrafis ̄ cōmanded iues aſke wold haue granted ſhold kepe ther lawis ̄ ſeuent yere ſhold wt tribute vide mrm̄ ī hiſto hoſt alexand er oroſius ſayth wos xxxijm foote men iiijm hors men ſchippes clxxx vn c er tayn whedre meruell ſhold wos biſſhop aft er fad er manilius papiriꝰ ̄ fabiꝰ wer cōſules rome papiriꝰ whhen wos chyld wos veray wiſſe ̄ fenyd mony fayr leſing myght keip maſter cōſell ſenetours cā man wos ſo nobull werur gret tributis artiliꝰ regulꝰ nobull cenytour ower come iij kyngꝭ lxxiij citeys ſubduit dragon cxv fote kyllyd aft er ward whan wos ou er cruell ayenes emnys ̄ denyeng yef peſe bot wold pay myghty tribute almoſt beyng ī diſpare fought ayeneſt ou er come hym ̄ hoſt toke hym neu er theles yet wold fayn haue pee bot moſt fayethful mā leu er dye ī paynes gret thē yef reſt ̄ pee curſet pepull louyng ſent augꝰ hogely exaltis emulius fabiꝰ ̄ gaius wold haue deliu er ed regulꝰ bot obtened ptholomeas eugites time wos kīg egipt victoriꝰ prince myghty man ſubdued syriam ̄ ciciliam ̄ moſt ꝑte plrā iohē ſuꝑ daniel̄ haniball moſt curſed kyng peno rum affricano rum myghtely hated romās deſtrued almoſt vtt er maſt end neer cite rome deſtruyed ſo mony noble men roman kylled tyme iij buſſhell goldī ringes drow ther fyngeres alſo ī acertayn water ſlayn body thes roman made wer brige hoſt myght pa laſt cipio noble ſenytour direckid hoſt hym ſcumfited almoſt cipio hoſt roman war ſlayn lucatiꝰ conſul symꝓnyꝰ valeriꝰ fulniꝰ lutinꝰ gaius scipio reuled rome tyme roman pee yere alon wos taken myracul ſo long reſt afoor tyme ī iiijc ̄ xl yere roman neu er reſt thes conſules yere wos done congregatit ſtrenght ytaly ther hoſt viijm armed men dreed frenchman dred ſtrongly aft er ward roman ſubdued epiphanes ſon philopator regned egipt xxiiij yere cleopatra doughter gret anthiocus wos wife antiochus magnus tyme rened syrry wich moch myſchefe iues vt pꝫ patet math onias tyme wos biſſhop ieruſalem onias tyrannyde antiochus fled mony iues egipt fenyng hym fulfyll propheſi yſaie 19 wete bild tempull bot ſynned ſayed wyſſe thought kyng egipt gracioſly reſaued gaff hym lond helipolees ther bild tempull symon ſon biſſhop ieruſalem aft er fader flede circa annū mūdi v·mxxxiiij et an̄ xp̄i ntītem clxv eleaſar lyne criſt bowt tyme hī thyng wreten ſcriptur bot math nombres hym vt pꝫ patet primo onias pius wos iues biſſhop tyme holy man welbeloued god man alonli good men bot ill mē alſo laſt vn righwiſli wos ſlayn andronito· vt pꝫ patet 2o machabeo rum 4o paulus therencius scipio affricanus wer ſenetous rome thes ij ereckyt hoſt yeneſt haniball ther almoſt roman hoope died ther wos ſlayn xliiijm roman nobull man cipio offricanus brought yene ſtate roman pepull wich ſtoode deſſpare eu er haue rekou er ed fought haniball manleli ſcumfited spayn ouer come affricam ſubduet gret antiochus brought ser uand al aſiam made tributary remans man ſo nobull ſo victorius bi vn kynd cūtre owtlayed ̄ ther died philometor ſon epiphanes cleopatra regned ī egipt xxxv yere kyng yet child nobull antiochꝰ hogely oppreſſit wt mōy diſſaytes bot ye roman ſent legats wich cōmāded antiaco yt ſhold ſeſe tyrannyde yenſt hym marcꝰ publiꝰ made cerkill boute antiochi thꝰ ſayng ſenetours rome ye pepul cōmā dith thow go cerkell till thow haue anwſar mat er antiochꝰ ſeyng yt myght cōtinu tyranyde ſayed yf thꝰ cōmādid ye ſenetour roman pepull muſt nedis turne ayene ſo woed angre wos yt loſt ſeege alexand er ̄ turned poer releuys ye iues vengyng hym vpō cauſe myght vēge hym myghtier pepull vtꝫ ī lio machabeo rum primo et 2o mathathias holy mā louīg moſt worthy hated ī hert ꝯu er ſaciō al ſynners alonly triſtyng ī lord god iſrael vtꝫ prio macha 2o man v ſōnes ſame loue vn god mā woſ biſhop ī iſrael bot iij ſōnes wer iudas machabeꝰ wos biſhop iij yere wos ſon mathathias macabeꝰ moſt named mā yt eu er wos ī iſraell wich neu er none like hym foor ne aft er wos ī batell myghty man offred hī dye mart er lawys god ionathas brother ſuccedit hym xix yere wich grew ī u er tu gou er ned ſtedfaſt ſtode ī lawis god aft er falſly ſlayn criphone ij ſōnys plrā vide iuda et frē eiꝰ libro macha antiochꝰ epiphanes ſon antiochꝰ myghty tyme kyng syrry mā heed vn fort wt ī ̄ curſed therfor figured antecriſt mōy mart er cruelly made falſly diſpoſid hym entyr ī egipt fad er bot obtened roman lettyd hym moſt vnhapy werkes ̄ wos ī hoſtage rome ye ꝓpheſi daniell completed hym ye may ſe boke machabeo rum qvintus flaminius marchus catho thiberiꝰ graccꝰ weer ſenetours rome tyme ſo contiunall ſo mych batell lerned men gentyles trew fayth bothe wer wery writte actys haue mynde ī wich batellis men merueled gretly ſtedfaſtnes romās tribulacion drede herdnes myght feere bot euer contynuid batell certanly thes roman aft er worldis honeſty wer moſt wiſe men wer therfore machobees deſired ther companye circa annū mūdi vm lix et ante xp̄i natītatē c·xl mathan ſon sadoch lyne criſt gat iacob vt pꝫ patet math 1o symon ſon mathathias wos biſſhope viij yere ſymon veray wiſe man hys youth vn tyll age wos eu er good conuerſacion euer u er tuus ̄ laſt ſlayn brother elay vt pꝫ patet prio machabeo iohannes hyrcanus ſon symon wos aft er fadir xxix yere nobull man kynred wos fore hym man aftir deceſſe left wife veray wyſſe woman v ſonnys gouerne iuri holdeſt wos called ariſtobolꝰ vnpacient man vnhappy mother iij yonger brether preſenit ſlew thurgh honger ſo loyn leued kyng biſſhop yere vide plura libro machabeo rum publius lucinius luciꝰ emilius▪ lucius lucinius lucius cenſorinus wer cōſules rome who tyme cartagines roman wered ſtrongly bot roman ſabduit intendyng haue deſtrued cartagines vtterly bot emong roman ther wos notabull wiſſe man calldd cipio nauta emong mony notabull conſellys ij gaffe ſpecealli ī mīde fyrſt cartago ſhuld deſtrued thurght occaſion forand batellis inward concord ſhuld bide emong roman ꝑpetuall ſtrength continuall exorciſe batell ſecund wiſe teathur ſhuld belde rome ſayed moſt enmy myght pepull yt vſid place nuryched ſlouthe prouoked lechory wiſely notabull man yaf counſell tymes foloyng declare vide plura ī augꝰ de ciuitete dei et oro libro quarto yet counſell nobull cite cartagie wos deſtruyed cipio ſenetours brent xvij dayes continually mony men ther wer ſold mony men ran fyer willely ¶corinthus ſame yere wos deſtruyed thee roman wich wos richeſt cuntre world ptholomeus tyme regned egipt wos famulier thee roman ſo long prediceſſurs regned kepyd fidelite roman knaw euery man ther cauſe pouer roman encreſed ſo ſtrongly bown odir pepull bot vertu wich abundantly regned nomli rightwiſnes wich bown thyng vſed long keped meſurnes loued rightwiſnes ſo long wer neuer ouer comen o ſoon wer corrupped red thei wer eu er ower comen hit ī certayn reuelacion god ſhewed sent briget lord god beris witnes thes oold roman noon world puer naturall reſon leued rightwiſly lyghttis faythe ſhewed tyme criſtyn relegion ſhall ſhewed afterwerd regnū iudeo rum reſtituitur ariſtobolꝰ wos fyrſt kyng preſt ī iuri man regned yere loyn toke hym dyame kyngdom held hym content fadre yaf hym ī hys teſtament bot put modir ī preſon bred therfor periched wrechidli brother antigonꝰ wich wos counſell helpet hym vide mrm̄ ī hiſtoriis ¶antigonꝰ brother kyng wos ſlayn thurgh enuy quene alexander wos biſſhop ariſtobolus ſtood xxvij yere wos tyrend though appered ſobur ī begīyng bot made knawyn wos ī ſtomoke· ſlew bred ī xij yere ſlew lm old ſaage fadres gret u er tu cauſe told hī myſgydyng whē ſhuldie hed left ij ſonys bi hynd hī hircanū ariſtobolū bot c er tanly ſaied wyfe ſhuld regne ſhe ſtood ī grace pepull seruiꝰ flaocꝰ lucius celius fabius publiꝰ tyme wer ſenetours rome tyme batels emong ſelf gan wich fyrſt cauſe ̄ begīyng wos graccꝰ myghty mā well knawyn wt nobull roman bi gan ſeke cauſe yenes cauſe myght nothīg loyn meued comyn pepull thē ſayng ye lōdes poſſeſſions ſhuld deuyded equaly ̄ alſo money etcc cauſe ther wos īſurreccion ī wich graccꝰ wos ſlayn mony myſcheuys fell aft er vide oroſiū ¶in tyme thes mē ther wos child born rome hauyng iiij feete iiij armes ij faceſſe iiij een hill ethna ſpytted flamyng fyer horobli deſtrued place ne abowt ¶̄ thes mē bering ruel cartago cōmādid reſtored ̄ wos fulfilled roman pepull ̄ ther wos myhhty batell ī cite rome ¶fabiꝰ wt lytell hoſt ower come kyng armenie ther wer drynched c lxxxm wat er reme ptholomeꝰ alexand er wos kyng ī egipt tyme wos borne lureciꝰ poeyd wich aft er ward wos mad luffe woman ſlew hym ſelf ptholomeꝰ ſon cleopatre regned aft er hym vnd er saluſtiꝰ nobull writer hiſtories wos borne ptholomeꝰ dioniſiꝰ wos aft er man ī tyme virgyll oracius wer borne anno mūdi vm c xxx iiij et an̄ xp̄i natītatē cv iacob natural fad er ioſeph lyne criſt reherſit luke mathe litell hym īſcriptur alexandra wyfe alexand er wos biſſhop ī iuri ix yer ſhe mych tyrannyde yef ſhe wos made biſſhop bi hir ſenyt holy relegiō hircanū hir ſon ſhe ꝓmotit biſſhoprik ſhe ordant yt ſhuld regne aft er hir ¶this womā ī ye line byſſhoppis put cowntyng yeres ſhe vſed office biſſhop wos lefull hir hircanꝰ ſon alexandra regned xxxiij yere hircanꝰ aft er ther deceſſe mod er ſuccedit ī kyngdom wich lytill ꝓſperite ꝑcialite pepull anōe wos owercumē aft er ward wos reſtored thurgh help arabees made trubutari roman ̄ ſo ī perſe lityll tyme bot ī name kyng laſt died wricchydly wos begyled thurgh fraude partho rum wich antigonus hyered ayenes hym vide plene mrm̄ hiſtori ¶the hereci pharaſeys bowt tyme began emong war iij ſektis iuri pharaſey saducey ̄ eſſey thes wer deuided fro cōmyn vſe iues ̄ wer īſeckt wt mōy errours ſayed wer holier thē men leued ſtratlyer thē men vide plus alias virgill moſt excelēt poetis wos magnified thys tyme ̄ meruelus thinges emong neopol̄ wos vexit dethly payn myghty wormys virgill keſt worme made gold ponde water lay c er tayn ſeſon ther take vp ī toun cite full wormys till worme gold put ī water ayene īfinite wormys whē ī wat er wormys went ther way ¶alſo wreten ī croniclis rome virgill conyng cōdēſit thicked ayre ſo walled gardyn ayr ̄ made brige ayr bi wich mygh paſe eu er tyme yt lyſt alſo aſkyd marcellū neopolicanū neueu vn emꝑour yf wold haue bride taght kill birdes fle taght driue fleys cite marcell ſhewed emprour deſyrid teche fle kyll fleys comyn pepull wer ſoor auexed fleys mony meruellis vide mrm̄ radulfū ceſtern oracius flaccꝰ saluſtius criſpꝰ hiſtoricꝰ wer tyme quītus cipio gaius luciꝰ tyme war cōſules rome pompeꝰ marcꝰ craſſus iuliꝰ ceſar tī wor dictats rome o ſayd afor ther wos mōi dygnites ī rome wych ſū dureth yere ſū ij yere emong dignites dictator excedit itduret vyer bot whē comyn pepull ye lordſhipis rome encreſing wer made iij dictator tyme wos pompeꝰ iuliꝰ marcus craſſꝰ dictator becauſe pompeꝰ wos gret honour aged boed rome kepe comyn pepull rome marcꝰ craſſꝰ wos ſend ſubdu ̄ fight wt regiō perthꝰ thurgh treſō wos taken ſlayn iuliꝰ ceſar wos ſend ye weſt part world ſubdu wt hym vij legion pepull whē ſubduit lūberdi fraunce v yere wer ſpendid wich wer aſſyngned te ̄ lōger ther bi autorite toke v yere hym ī wych ſubduid caſſibolon kyng bretan fraunche men rebeled ayenes hym ſame iulius aft er cōquered thes cūtreys vn rome roed ayene reſſaued certayn worſhip cōquerours wor foor hym bot wos denied hym alſo entre cite īſtigacion lord called pompay wherfor iulius ceſar wos noyed fors myght entyred cite ̄ robbed comyn treſour led hym deꝑted emong v legiones wer ser uandes went spayn fight ayen pompoy pompay gou er nan cartago bot aftar iornay ī itali pompay counterd ged er wich batell pompay fled vn kyng egipt ſame kīg ſpeciall luffe vn iuliꝰ ceſar ſmot pompays hed ſend vn iulius ceſar yet enmyte twix thes two iulius weppid ſaw pōpayes heed iulius excedyng witte foor men fought batell lij tymes man aloyn excedit marcus craſſus wich ſayed haue foughten xxxix tymes thys man toke fyrſt empire rome pon pompay nobull men roman wor ſlayn laſt v yere empire iuliꝰ ceſar ruler world ſlayn counſell houſe thurgh treſon lordis cathon moſt named pheloſopher ſeyng iulis ceſar haue victori fauort toune called vticam ſlew hī ſelfe iuxta illud ¶mauult cato mari quam deroget vrbis honori bot auguſtyn wos excuſed ſyn ¶this time iuri wos trebutori romās ꝑcialyte ij bretheren ariſtobolus ercanus bothe enuy odirkeſt roman myght regne ¶this tyme iij ſonnes appered heuyn toward eſt parte world wich lytill lytyll wer brought body gret ſigne wos affrica aſia ̄ europa ſhuld brought monarch lordſhip anthom ſenetour lucus antonij ſhuld turne lordſhip marcus cicerio tulyus moſt excelent retricion wos conſull rome tyme ¶how breton graunted vn caſſibolan wos ludd brother land who tyme iulyus ceſar come twyes conquere lond bretan deth kyng lud regned brother caſſibolon become good man mych belowed bretōs ſo goodnes curteſie graunted hym reame euermore hym ayres kyng goodnes let noriſch worthely bothe ſonnys wos ludis brother made eldeſt ſon erle cornwaill ̄ yongeſt ſon made erle london kyng caſſibulon regned come iulius ceſar wos emprour rome ī land wt pouer roman wold haue thys land thurgh ſtrength caſſibalon ouer come hym ī batell thurgh helpe breton drofe hym land went ayen rome aſſemled gret pouer tyme come ayene land gif batell caſſibalan bot wos diſcomfitied thurgh ſtrenght briton thurgh helpe erle cornwaill erle london brother thurgh help gudian kyng ſcotland corbond kyng kyng north walles bretaill kyng ſouthwales ̄ thys batell wos ſlayn nennon wos caſſibolams brother wherfor made moch ſorow ſo went iulius ceſar land roman left lyue tho caſſibalan went ayene londō made feſt vn folke tho hym holpen feſt done ther euery man went cuntre ¶of debate wos bitwix caſſibolom erle londō truage paied rome befell thus vpon day yt gentilmen ye kynges houſhold gentilmē ye erles houſhold l̄ondon mete went fere play thurgh debate aroſe emong enelyn wos erles coſen london kyiled irenglas wos ye kynges coſin wherfor kyng ſwore enelyn ſhold honged bot erle london yt enelyns lord wold ſuffre hym wherfor kyng gretly vexid wroth towarde erle thought deſtru preualy erle ſēt lettres iulius ceſar yt ſhold cum ī land helpe hī hī venge vpon kīg ̄ wold help hym myght emprour herd tidyngꝭ full glad ̄ ordeyned ſtrōg pouer come yene thrid tyme land erle london helpe hym vijm men thrid tyme caſſibalon ouer comen diſcomfited made pee emprour iijm ponde ſyluer yeldyng yere truage land euer half yere paſſed emprour weent vn rome erle london hym durſt abid land caſſibolan regned xvij yere pee tho died xvij yere regne lieth yorke ¶how lordis land deth caſſibolan encheſon heir made andragen kyng deth caſſibolon myche none heir lefull body begottyn lordes lond bi ye comyns aſent crouned andragen erle cornwaill made hym kyng regned well worthely wos good man well gouerned lond regned viij yere died lieth london circa annū mūdi vmclix et xp̄i natiuitatē xl ioſeph lyne criſt abowt tyme wos borne wos huſband vn lady antigonus byſſhope tyme iuri antigonus ſon vn ariſtoboly euery ſide fals obeyed roman gret plage brouaht vn land deſtruy hircanus vnkyll mygh regne kyng ſo hircanuu expulſed falelus wos kylled· herod wos flemyd bot whē herod come vn te rome told senetours thes thynges emprour creatit hī kyng ſēdīg hī hoſt wich toke ieruſalem antigonum byſſhope taken led anthony ſenetour wich made hym ſekyr ſo wos herod confirmed kīgdō ̄ ſtrang regned iues ſo kīgdō iues ſeeſyd iacob ſaid titꝰ liuiꝰ hiſtoricꝰ ouidius wer tyme incipiūt imꝑatores auguſti • et dictus eſt auguſtus quia augebat populū octauian wos emꝑour rome lvij yere vi monethes x dayes octauian neuew iuly wen wos yonge man toke empire vpon hym florichyng youth ſpend vm batels chortly aft er mony batels brought world monarche mā felow dayes pee ī world thurgh prouiſion veray god temporall pee myght glorify natiuite ſauyour criſt iheſu octauian wos fayreſt man myght hegh witt moſt fortunate thynges lakked vice fleſhly luſt man made world meſured lij yere regne wos lord iheſu criſt borne ſauer world wich granteth eternall pee louery ¶hic nota ſecund ieroīmū anna emeria wer ſiſtirs emeria wos borne elezabeth mother iohn̄ baptiſte ſhe wos fy • ſt wedded iochym ſhe toke mari mother criſt ¶the ſecūd houſbond wos cleaphe gat hir maria cleaphe wich wos wedded alphe procedid iamys leſſe symon cananeus iudas taddeus ̄ ioſeph wich called barſabas ¶the thrid tyme anna wos wedded salome ſhe toke mari ſalome wich weddid zebedi ̄ cō iamis iohn̄ euāgeliſt firſt mari wedded ioſeph brod er cleaphe fore ſayd ¶thys tyme sibilla tiburtina ꝓpheſied criſt ſayed emꝑour auguſt ſhold trow god aft er fulychnes panyms ther ſhe ſhewed hym fayr virgyn heuyn holdyng chyld hir army ſayed hī chyld gret thē tho therfor hī worſhipe ¶the monch rome bowt time mightili encreſed whē wos ſo bi world diuerſe ꝓuynſis batiles wer raſed ſodanli men meruellyng werſeſid put holly prince rome opynly myght ſhewed ſych vniuerſall peeſe come neuer labur batell bot power veray god natiuite peeſe ſhuld regne world herod aſcolonita wos kyng ī iuri xxxvij yere herod ydumeus wos fyrſt ſtrang kyng regned iues maiſter ī hiſtoriis ſayes wos nobull mā faythfull begynnyng thyng hym nobully wos veray gentyll vn roman pepil louyd peeſe old age wold awr mekyll pleeſe roman herd byrth criſt dredyng expulſit kyndoom ſtranger wrycchitly fell kylled innoſentis diuerſe chylder laſt wos hatfull pepull fell ſeeke died wretchydly ¶mari mother criſt borne foor ethe natiuite criſt xvi yere ther bowte ¶of kymbalyn wos androgeus ſon good man well gouerned lond bretan deth androgen regned kymbalin ſon yt wos good man well gou er ned lond moch ꝓſperite pee lyfes tyme tyme wos borne iheſu criſt ſauyour ſwete virgin marie kyng kymbalin ij ſonnys guidar armoger good kynghtes worthy kyng kymbalyn rogned xxij yere died lieth london xp̄s natꝰ ē ex virgine maria ano mūdi vm c lxxx xviij begynnyng xlij yere octauian emperour wich gan regne marrhe xxxi yere herod vijc li yere rome belded ſext moneth conſauyng iohn̄ baptiſt viij kalend aprill ſext fery nazareth galalee virgin mari wos ꝯſaued criſt ſaueour ſame yere borne xp̄s natus eſt beginnith ſexte aage ende world heir begyneth criſtes natiuite ſext age duryng vn finall iugement lord god hauyng yeres mony lord knaweth ¶when yt lord iheſu criſt wos borne well oylle ſprang yonde tybur rome ran day ¶the goldyn ymage fell wich romalus made put palas ſayng ymage ſhall fall vntil mayd beyr chyld ¶when herod diſſpoſed hym kyll chylder iſraell commanded letter emperour cum vn rome onſwer accuſaſion childir alexiū ariſtoboli ¶and ther wer iij herodes gretli ſpaken ther yll dedis fyrſt wos callid aſcolonita vnd er man borne criſt chylder iſraell wer ſlayn ſecund wos called antipas ſon fyrſt herod vnder iohn̄ baptyſt wos hedit criſt ſuffyrd deth thee thred wos called agrippa ſone ariſtoboly ſone fyrſt herod wich kylled iamys preſenyd peter ¶the fyrſt herod ſaw ſonnys alexium ariſtobolem thurgh pretens letter emperour ſend ſtriue ſucceſſion kyngdom diſpoſed made antipatron wos hys fyrſt goten ſō bi wer talkīg deth ther fadir keſt thē away went emprour complayn wrong ther fadre ¶and thee meyn tyme iij kynges colan come herod vn ieruſalem come yene hym thought war aſſhamed cum ayene hym cauſe wer deſſaued fond chyld trowed therfor meynſeſon ſeſſed kyll chyldyr iſraell went vn rome thee citacion emperour toke way cite tarſum wher brent ſhyppes wich iij kynges colan ſhuld haue ſailed ther cuntre ¶then aft er yere certayn dayes herod come fro rome yen • e acorded ſonnis confirmacion kindō wos made much boldyr kylled chyldir bethelem wer ij yere age vndir· yt ſpace nyght aage emong thes ther oon chylder ariſtobolus alexiū wer ſuſpeckyt ſo mych promyſed barbour gret reward ſhuld take • • ut ther faders throte hym ſhaue herod herd greued ther kylled bothee ſonnys herod agrippa ſon ordand kīg wher foor antipat er holdeſt ſon wos bout puſyn hys fadre wich herod agrippa vndyr ſtoed preſenit ther hys brother wich emprour herd ſayed leueyr hog herodes tyll ſonnys hys hoggys ſporeth ſonnys kyllis thatt herod wos lxx yere age wos ſtrikyn gret ſekenes hondes feit ī mēbres leche myght cū hym ſtynke ſo died antipater ſune priſon herd tell ioyed gretly therfor cauſe wos ſlayn ¶then ſtroffe archelaꝰ herodes ſucceſcion fyrſt herod fore emꝑour emperour ther thurgh conſell ſenetours half iuri idumya gaffe archelaꝰ vndir name tetrarche partte deuided ī galali yaf herod antippe ituriā traconitidē yaf philippe herod brether ¶and ſame yere criſt come frō egippt ̄ archelaꝰ accuſed mony tymes iues exiled ī viēnam ī fraunce place wer ſet iiij tetrarches repreuyng īſtabulnes iues ¶and yt ſame yer octouiā emꝑour died anno criſty xij iheſus criſt xij yere age herd doctor ī tēpull lord ihū criſt xxx yere age baptiſed iheſu criſt lord thynges inri crux xp̄i xxxiij yere age iij monethes dyed ſeruandes anninus rufus wos byſſhop ī ye iury bowt tyme valerius graccꝰ wos hym xi yere man opynly ſold biſſhopryke moſt yaf ſo ther wos mony ī litell poncius pilatus wos iuge ̄ proctur ī iuri vnder emꝑour ̄ vndyr man iohn̄ thee baptiſt gan preche ¶and lord ſuffered deth wich dampned deth vn rightwiſly dreed emꝑour tyrus certayn kyng gat child pila poer mās doughter wich mā heght atus child mod er name belſer put gedir wos called pilatus pilatꝰ ye iiij yere age wos ſend fad er wich kyng lefull wyffe gotten child euyn age pilate becauſe lefull goten child ꝓceded age excedit baſterd pilatꝰ • full enuy kyllid brother lefull getyn child wherfor fad er ſend hym rome plege tribute yt payed vn rome intendyng wold neu er redeme hym ¶in wich tyme kynges ſon fraunce wos pleage tribute wich excedid hym ſtrengthe cheualri alſo kylled hym therfor roman ſend pilate ꝓphetabull man commyn well ile ponto taam curſſed pepull wich kylled eu er iuge come curſed man gou er ned vnhappy pepull thretyng ꝓmys wt law yeftes none durſt contrary pleſour wherfor called pilat ponto ¶herod antipa yong conu er ſacions yeftes meſſīgers drew hym hym made hym prince iure vndir hym tyme pilat gedered mych money herod knawyng went rome mygit reſ • ue emꝑour yt herod yefen hym wherfor herod pilat wer enmys gedre vn paſſion lord pilat ſend iheſus criſt vn herod clothed white cloth wer made frendys ouidius naſo ponto bout tyme died iiij yere exile tibirius tyme wos emꝑour rome ̄ regned xxiij yere leued ī yere lord iheſu criſt died ſūwhat man werkes gretly viſed ther ſhuld thyng ſodenli done wyſſe wer ſtudious bokis fayr ſpech frech witt saue wold oft tyme feyn hym ſelfe thyngis wold wer done od er ¶this emꝑour vndir ſtode traſted criſt ̄ worſhio •• hym god sum men ſaieth laſt wos cruell yenes pepull bot wos gret reſon pety eu er gracius ſubiectis poer men pee dayes ̄ pepull ſaied ayeneſt criſtyn folke ony mercy deſtrued exiled pilat euer deceſſed wors ſuccedid hym euſibe wretin lord xxx yere age choſe xij apoſtilis wich made cred yt beleue made hit aft er reſureccion criſt aft er holy goſt ſend vn thei choſin mathia poſtill ich made aꝑte ſhewed heir aft er ¶and mathia wos choſyn twix ye day aſcenſion witſonday place iudas ſcarioch ye tratur wich iudes ī hiſtori thꝰ red ¶ther certayn man ī ieruſalem yt heyght rubē ſent ierom tribe yſachar wyfe het ciborea wich c er tā night whē wold luſtili knaw wife ſhe dremed yt ſhe ſhuld bere child myſchef yt child ſhuld t̄t ur kīg peple yt regiō ̄ ye chyld wos borne called iudas fad er mod er abhorrit well kill ther child nuryſh trator kyng pepull therfor put hym panyer leep ſee floyd ile scaryoth wher lady place child hir houſband ſhe fened hir child bot ſhe faled aft er lityll ſeſon ſame lady quene cōſaued child hir huſbond ̄ wos age iudas mony tymes angred ̄ cauſed hī wepe ye wich ye quene ſawe bet iudas mōy tymes ſhe knawlech iudas wos kynges ſon ne wherfor iudas kyllid kyngꝭ ſon dred payn law ̄ fled wt c er tan exile ieruſalem ̄ come ther gat hym pilate couurt wos iuge becauſe oo curſed mā drew therfor drew pilate ̄ ſtoid gretly hys fauoure vpon certan day pilat lokyt owt hys pale ī orcherd man wos called rubē wych wos verey fad er iudas pilat deſired haue appuls iudas went gedre apuls ruben ran iudas lette hym becauſe toke appuls wt ony leefe aft er yt chyed iudas ſmot fad er heed wt ſton ̄ kylled iudas fled way ſecretly aft er yt deed bot wos ſaied yt ruben died ſodenly pilat yaf iudas ye goodis yt rubē ciboria rubēs wife yt mod er iudas delt curtaſly hyr man ſhuld wt wiffe yt ſhe wepid weiled ſhe put hir ſon ſee yt ſhe maried yeneſt hir ꝑſaued iudas kylled fad er weddie moder ciboria mod er ̄ wife meuyd hī leef ſyn fol • ed criſt gafe ſinnys ̄ made proctor ̄ poſtel fals wos criſt nedith reherſſe ſame yere mathew wos choſin ̄ holy goſt wos ſend ī ſaid afor apoſtils wer ſparpild ī world gedyrd ged er ī ieruſalem ̄ made credo heir foloyng belefe petrꝰ credo ī deū patrē omnipotētē creatorem celi et terre andreas et iheſum xp̄m filium eius vnicū dominū nrm̄ iohānes qui cōceptus eſt de ſpiritu ſc̄o natꝰ ex maria virgine iacobus paſſus ſub pōcio pilato crufixꝰ mortuus et ſepultus thōas deſcendit ad īferna tercia die reſurexit mortuis iacobꝰ aſcendit ad celos ſedet ad dexterā dei ptīs omnipotentis philippꝰ inde vēturus eſt iudicare viuos et motuos bartholoꝰ credo ſpiritum ſanctum matheꝰ sanctam eccleſiam catholicam symon sanctorum commumonem remiſſionem peccatorum iudas carnis reſureccionem mathias et vitam eteernam amen iheſu criſt ſaiueour roos deth lyue ſaied diſcipules power heuen erth geuyn vn go ye thus ī al world preche teche wn eueri creatur ſhall yow end thee world ¶her choſe lxxij diſcipules xij apoſtolis wich ſend ī al world p̄che ne red ther war mo ord er emong diſcipuls criſt thee preſtys byſſhoppis chirche god yit kepe forme appoſtill biſſhoppis ſuccede diſcipuls preſtis wich ij ordirs chyrche geuen godly gerarche vt patet decreto damaſie pape iohēs wrot aſia ī greke lāgage principio erat verbum etcc lucas wrot ī grecia greke lāgage fuit diebus herodis regis iude ſac er do etc marcus wrot ī ytalia bot ī greke langage initiū euāgelii ihū criſti etcc matheꝰ wrot iuri ī hebru langage liber gen er acōis iheſu criſti c ¶her begyneth ordir popys rome continuys lyne criſt afoor ī th • god l • ſt hi • 〈◊〉 anno domini xxxiiij petur iue fyrſt pope wos bliſſed man glorius poſtyll criſt wos heed chyrche ierom xxxvij yere held hiſ biſſhoprik eſt v yere ſaid maſſe made lord alone ſaid pater noſter ¶thē come anthiociam ther boed vij yere techyng way trowth symon magus flemed way ſeſon prechid pepull wer circumſiſit wych wer pōto galati capadecia aſia bithinia ¶thē herd yt symon magus deludit roman thurgh lufe faith come rome iiij yere claudius emprour ther preched word god ſhewd falſed symon magus turned mony aman fayth ſend prechours bi diuerſe prouynſe criſtyn relegion myghtyly encreſed ¶he ordand feſt lentyn fore eſtyr aduent emyring dayes faſtid criſtē pepull merour friſt ſecund comynge lord pope rome xxv yere vij moneths viij dayds ſlayn nero eiꝰ plurima oꝑa vide actibꝰ apoſtolo rum gayus tyme wos emprour rome regned iij yere x monethes gayus wos full vicius leuyng ij ſyſtres myſuſed hee gat doughter wich child ſet twix keis iupit er tempull fened afterward iupat er gettyn hyr wherfoor cry thurgh cuntre men ſhuld worſhyp hyr goddeſſe ¶this mon alſo made ymage like hym ſelf ſend oon patronie preſedent ieruſalem vndir roman cōmaundyng hym ſhuld compell iues doo worſhip therto thes enormytes mony owr lord ſuffyrd hym ſlayn rome pale ¶of kyng gynder kymbalin ſon wold nott pay treuage rome land caſſibalon granted wos ſlayn romayn deth kymbalin regned gynder hys ſun good man worthe wos ſo hygh hert yt wold pay rome tribute kyng caſſibalon graunted vn iulius ceſar wherfor emprour wos tho wos called claudius ceſar wos ſore annoyed ordāt gret power remans com land conquere tribute thurgh ſtrength haue kyng kyng gynder armager brether aſſembled gedired gret hoſt yfere briton yaf bataell emprour claudius kylled roman gret plente emprour afterward one wos called hamon ſaw ther pepull theer whaerfaſt ſlayn preuali keſt way armes toke armes • ed breton armed armuro come batell kyng ſayed maner syr ye good hert goddis loue roman enmys anone ſhall ſlayn diſcumfited euerychon ̄ kyng yaf kepe vn wordes ne ſpeche becauſe armes yt vpon hym wened briton tratour eu er held hym next kyng preualy vnder ſhulders armes ſmot kyng wherfor deid fell doune erthe whan armag er ſaw brother deid caſte away armes toke hym brother armes come botaill among briton bad hertely fight faſt lay doune roman armes wened kyng gynd afore wos ſlayn wyſt begone britans ferſly fight kyld roman ſo laſt emprour ſoke felde ̄ flede faſt o myght folke wyncheſtre fals traitour hamon ſlayn kyng faſt anone gan fle haſt myght armager kynges brother purſued full ferſly fers hert drofe hym vn water ther toke hym anone ſmot bothe hand ̄ hede foot hewed body peces tho let caſt water wherfor water called hamanus hauen afterward ther made fayr toune yet ſtandeth yt called ſouthamton afterward armager went wyncheſtre ſeke claudius ceſar emprour rome ther armager hym toke claudius emprour thurgh concel roman left lyue made pee armager maner ye ſhall ſay claudius emprour ſhuld yeue vn armager gennen fair doughter haue wife ſo land fro tyme forward ſhuld empreurs poer rome uppon ſuche conueant neuer afterward emprour rome ſhuld take none tribute land bot feaulte wer acorded vpon conand claudius ceſar ſent reme doughter gennen ſhe wos comen claudiꝰ ceſar yaf hir armager wife armag er ſpouſed hir london mych ſolempnite ̄ myrth tho armager crouned made kīg britan ¶of kyng armager whoſe tyme ſent petre preched antiochie apoſtoles diu er ſe cuntreis armager regned well worthely lond gou er ned claudius ceſar remembrans acord reu er ence honour dought er made lond fair toune caſtell let call toune name clauceſtren called glouceſtre wos done emprour toke leue tho went rome armager tho kyng gou er ned lond well nobely life tyme armag er gat ſon wife thatt wos called weſtmer ̄ while armager regned ſent petre preched antioche ther made nobull chyrche wich ſat fyrſt chair ther dwelled vij yere ̄ aft er went rome made pope till nero emprour let martir tho preched opanly appoſteles diu er ſe landes right fayeth armager regned xxiiij yere died lieth london ¶how kyng weſtmer yaf berynger yland forlet ther berynger made toun berewike armager regned ſon weſtmer wos good man ̄ worthy body well gou er ned land hit befell ſo tydyng come day king rodrik gaſcoine come land houge hoſt pepull wos duellyng ſtaynſmore kyng weſtmer herd tho tydynges let aſſemble houge hoſt britans come kyng rodrik yaf hym batall ̄ kyng weſtmer kylled rodrik hondes playn batall whē kyng rodrikes men ſaw ther lord wos deid yolden kyng weſtmer ̄ bicome men eu er ̄ yaf cōtre wos forleten wher ī myght duell ̄ doughter kyng coill conſtance made kyng ̄ crouned mych ſpouſed kyng coilles doughter wos heir land wich conſtance regned well ̄ wortheli gou er ned land begat wife elene ſon wos called conſtantine conſtantine ſon ſon ſent eline fond holy croſe holy land conſtantine become emprour rome hit befell ſo tyme ther emprour rome wos sarzyn ̄ tyrant thas wos called maxence put deth beleued god ̄ deſtruyed holy chrche pouer ſlew criſten men myght fynd emong let marter ſent katrin mony criſtī pepull drede deth yt fled ̄ come lond kyng conſtantine told hym ſorow maxence criſtīte wherfor conſtātine pitte gret ſorew made aſſemled gret hoſt agret pouer went ouer vn rome ther toke cite kylled ther wos wer myſbeleue myght ther fynde tho wos made emprour good man gou er ned hym ſo well londes hym wer attendaunt vnd er gouernance ¶and duell ̄ tyrant maxence yt tyme wos land grece herd tydynge hee become wode ſodanly died ſo endid lyfe conſtā tine went land vn rome toke hym mod er
