hand ther wt among hygh law held hym kīg whan tydynges come conſtantine emprour wonder wroth toward erle octauian ſent taberne wyth xijm men deſtruye erle falſenes ariued porteſmouth ¶and octauian wiſt aſſē led agret pouer breton diſcōfited taberne taberne fled then scotland ordened ther gret pouer com ayene land tyme yef batell octauiā ¶when octauian herd tell aſſemled gret power com ayen towardes taberne moch myght ſo tho ij hoſtys metten gedre vpō ſtanyſmore ſtrongly ſmot gedre tho wos octauian diſcomfited fled then vn norway taberne ſeyſed land ī hand tounes ̄ caſtelles moch ther ſith octauian come yen fro norway wt gret pouer ̄ ſeiſed land ī hand drofe roman wos tho made kyng regned ¶how maximian emprours coſyn rome ſpouſed octauians doughter wos made kyng land octauian gouerned land well nobully none heir ſaufe doughter yong chyld loued moch lyfe mych thatt waxed ſeke wos ī poynt deth myght longer regne wold haue made one nepheus haue ben kyng wich nobull knyght ſtrong man yt wos called conan meriedoke ̄ ſhuld haue keped kynges doghter ̄ haue maried hir whē tyme bene lordes land wold ſuffer yaf hir councell maried ſum hygh mā gret honour might ſhe haue hir luſt cōſell thee emprour conſtantyne hir lord counſell accorded choſe tho cador cornwaill wende ye emꝑour meſſage ̄ toke way ̄ went rome tolde emprour tydyng well ̄ wyſely ̄ emꝑour ſent land wt coſyn yt wos vnkyll ſon nobull knyght ſtrong wos called maximian ſpouſed octauians doughter wos crouned kyng land ¶how maximian wos emprours coſyn conquered land amorican yaf conan meriedok kyng maxmian becom ſo riall thoght conquere land amarican gret rich herd tell wos land ſo ne left man wos worthines knyght ſquyer ne none othir man ne toke gret damage lond left home behynde man kepe land bot toke hym fro land xxxm knyghtes wer doughty menys body went ouer ī land amorican thor ſlew kyng yt called imball cōquered lond ¶and whē ſo done cald conan ̄ ſaid mich o kīg octauian haue made yow kīg bretō thurgh ye werlett diſtrobled yt ye wer kīg yeue yow land amorican yow ther maketh kynge ¶and moch ye ben breton wyll thys land haue ſame name called amorican bi called litell bretan land fro whens ben comen ſhall called moch bretan ¶and ſo ſhall men knaw bretan fro conan meridok thanked hendely ſo wos made kyng lytell bretan ¶and done maximian went fro then vn rome tho made emprour conſtantine conan meriedok duelled lytell bretan mych honour ther let ordand ijm plough men land erie land harow ſowe • effed hem richely wer ¶and miche o kyng conan none knyghtes ne none pepull wold take wyfes nacion fraunce hee tho ſent gret breten erle cornwaill men cald dionothe yt ſhuld che • e thurgh land xim madens ſay viijm mene pepull iijm thee gretteſt lordes ſhuld ſpouſe ¶and whē dionoth vnd er ſtode made acōmandement thurgh land bretan mony o nōbro come aſſemled ged er maydens ther wos man durſt withſtonde commandmētes mich land take hym warde kepe done thinge good liked ¶and thes maydens wer aſſemled let cum fore iym att london let ordan ſhippes haſteli ̄ o mich thē neded vyage toke doughter wos called vrſula wos fayreſt creature thot man wyft wold haue ſent hir kyng conan ſhuld haue ſpouſed hir ̄ made hir quene land ſhe made preuali god vowe chaſtyte hir fadre wyſt ne man el wos leuyng vpon ethr ¶how vrſula xim maydens wer hir company went toward litell bretan wer martired coloyn vrſula choſe vn hir company xim maydens ſhe wos ladie maſtreſſe wēt ſhipp tyme water called thamſe cō manded hir kyn hir frendis almyghty god ſailed toward litele breton bot whē wer comen hygh ſee ſtrange tempaſte aroſe wos goddis ¶and vrſula wt hir ſhippes hir company wer driuen hundland thurgh tempaſt ariued hauen cite colonie kyng land wos called gowan tho cite wiſt tyding ſo mony faier maydens wer ther arriued toke elga brother houſhold wt hī wēt ſhippis ſe faire company whan ſaw thē ſo faire companie wold haue ou er layne ̄ take fro ther maydenhod vrſula good mayd concelled prayed warned taught wer hir felowes ſhuld defend ther myght rather ſuffre deth ſuffren ther bodi diffoylled tho maydens become ſo ſtedfaſt god defended thurgh grace ſo nōe pouer ſhame ¶wherfer kīg gawan wax ſore anoyed yt wroth ſlew eu er ichō anōe right ̄ ſower tho maydens martred loue god lieth coloyn ¶how kyng gowan come deſtruy land man gret power thot wos called gracian defended land wos done kyng gowan wos sarazen called brother elga ſaid hym ſhuld go conquere land tho fair maydens wer borne ¶and ordened tho gret pouer pehites denmarke orkenay norway come land brenttounes ̄ ſlew folke ̄ caſt doune chirches houſes ̄ relegiō robed land length ̄ breed ̄ put deth tho wold forſake right beleue criſtyndom ¶for mich o ther wos ſouerayn moght helpe kyng maximian taken hym worthi men whē wēt conquere litell kretan ſame tyme ye tell ſent albone martired thurgh woed tyrant dioclician ſame place wher abbaye made ſent albone while yt wos apaynem ¶but conu er ted hī god thurgh predicaciō clarke wiſe mā yt called ancibell wos herbored nyght houſe incarnacion ihū criſt ijcxxvi yere mē ſhuld vnd er ſtand ſent albone ſuffred martirdō fore ſent edmūde wos martired therfor ſent albone called fyrſt marter englond ¶this gowans brother ̄ folk yt wer ſarazenes wēt thurgh land ̄ deſtrued thīg yt found ̄ thīg ſpayred whē tydyng come rome kyng gowan begon ſtroye land emꝑour tho rome ſent ſtrong mā ̄ gret pouer yt wos called graciā xxiiijm men well fightīg caſt tho ſarezenes lande ariued porteſ mothe ¶maximian myght cū hym ſelf moch o wos choſen emꝑour aft er deth conſtantine wos ſent elene ſon ¶whē gracian wos ariued wt hoſt let ſpi preueli wher kyng gowan myght befounde vpō hym ſodanli lain ther beddes deſcomfited hī ̄ ſlew ī ther beddis eu er ichone none aſcaped ſafe gowan fled moch ſorow cōtre ¶sone aft er befell yt maximian wos ſlayn rome thurgh treſon gracian wyſt tydyng let croune hym kyng land ¶how gracian made hym kyng whan maximian ſlaī afterward breton kylled hym wikkedneſſe gracian begone regne become ſo wikked ſo ſterne ſo moch ſorow breton yt ſlew hī emong ¶tho kyng gowan vnd er ſtond gracian ſlayn done deth aſſembled gret pouer ̄ come ayene ī land firſt done harme tho moch tho deſtrued land ye criſtē pepull yt wos ī moch bretan ſo yt mā wos ſo hardi nempne god ̄ yt ſo anōe put ſtrange deth ¶but biſſhop lōdon wos tho yt called goſſelin ſcaped wēt then rome ſech ſocour help deſtru ſarazenis yt deſtruyed lond ¶and ye romās ſaied yt ſo oft annoyed ther ſendyng aft er folke ī bretan help bretens wold ſo ¶and ſo biſſhop goſſeline wēt thēs wt ony ſocour helpe tho went kīg litell bretan yt called aldroie ̄ thrid kyng aft er gowan meriedok ſayed ¶the biſſhop prayed kyng aldroie helpe ſocour kyng pitte hert herd biſſhop fled ̄ criſtyn men wer ſo ſlayn gret bretan thurgh paynems ſarazenes graunted hym conſtantine brother hym helpe pouer folke araye hors armur ſhyppes thīg neded viage ¶and thyng redy called biſſhope ̄ hym ſayed take heir helpe ̄ ſocour cōſtantine brother vpō couenaut god yef hī grace ye paynems ̄ ye ſarazenes ſhend diſcomfited ye make hym kyng biſſhop grauntid good ¶conſtantine ̄ biſſhop toke lefe kīg aldroye ̄ betoke god toke ther men xijm went ther ſhippes ſailed toward gret bretan ariued totneſſe ¶when bretans herd tidynges yt come ſocour wer ſtrongly holpen ̄ ordeyned huge nombre pepull come vnd er fenge hem mekyll honour gowan anone wyſt thynges aſemled ſarezenes come ayeneſt yaf batal conſtantine ſlew hym hondes tho ſarazenes wer diſcomfited ſlayn nōe aſſcaped tho conu er ted vn god ¶how conſtantine kynges brother litell briton wos crouned kīg myche breton worthenes anone bataill went london crouned ther conſtantine made hym kyng land byſſhoppe goſelin ſette croune heed annoyntid hym o befalleth kyng bene tho bigan criſtyndom ayene ī land anōe kyng conſtantine wos creuned anone ſpouſed wife thurgh counſell breton begat iij ſonnys hir ¶the friſt wos cald conſtance aurilambros thrid vter conſtance eld er brother come age made hym monke wyncheſtre conſtantin ther fadre thurgh treſone wos ſlayn befell tyme pehite come hym vpon day meſſage ſayed wold ſpeke kyng preuali councill kyng let voied chambre men ther wer withyn ther bode mo bot kyng pehite ̄ made countinance tho hee wold haue ſpoken ye kīg ī ere ther kylled hym wt long knyfe went quaīteli owt chambre od er chābre ſo laſt man wyſt wher wos bicomen ¶when kynges men wyſt ther lord wos ſo deid made ſo moch ſorow wiſt done ¶for myche ij ſonnes aurilombros vter wer ſo yonge nōe myght kyng thrid brother wos mōke wencheſtre ſaied befoor vortiger wos erle weſtſexe thought priuyly hert thurgh quētance kyng went wyncheſtre ther conſtance monke ̄ hym ſayed conſtans quod fadre deid ij bretheren ben goſſeline biſſhope london noriſſh ben ſo yong none may kyng ¶wherfor councell yow ye forſake habit come ̄ ſhall make ſych meyn vn breton ye ſhall made kyng ¶of conſtans yt wos kīg cōſtantine ſon mōke wyncheſtre wos made kyng fadres deth thurgh conſell vortiger wos erle weſtſexe mich aurilambros vter ij brether wer yong age vortiger let ſle hym kyng hym ſelf vortig • r conſceled conſtance ſo mych tyll forſoke abbot went hym anone wos crouned kyng aſſent breton ¶this kyng conſtance whan wos crouned made kyng wiſt ne knew bot litell world na coude thing wat knyghthod axed made vortiger chief maſtir conceller yaf hym hys pouer ordeyne mych reame apertened hym ſelf thyng entermelled onli bare name kyng ¶when vortiger ſaw land warde gouernall wyll thought preuy treſon ſle conſtance kyng myght hym ſelf crouned made kyng regne let ſend hundreth knyghtes pehetes worthieſt al land heeld wyth hym duell kepers body wold wende thurgh land ordeyne thynges apperteyned kyng ¶and vortiger honoured ſo moch hondred knyghtes ſo moch yafe gold ſilu er ſo riche iuelles robe hors thynges plente wherfor held hym lord kyng ¶and vortiger told yf might kīg ye wer thurgh treſon wold make hem richeſt land laſt thurgh gret yeftes yefuen largeli cried thurgh court thatt vortiger wer better worthy kyng conſtance wherfor vortiger made ſemland bene wroth departed then court ſaied moſt gon elles thinges done ſo tratour ſaied encheſon ſhuld hym ſlee ſay conſtance ¶when vortiger wos gone befell ſone tho hundreth knyghtes pehites broken dores ef kynges chamber ther hym ſlew ̄ ſmote heed bore vortiger ther duelled vortiger ſaw heed wepped full tenderly eye nerthelees wos ſomedell glad deth ¶and anōe let take houndreth knyghtes pehites bynd ther handes hynd led london ther wer dampned deth fals tratours anone bretans land bi commune aſſent crouned vortyger made hym kyng land anno domini clxxiiij sother martir wos pope auicetū ix yere wich decreit nūne ſhuld towch pall awt er ner pit ſence ther ſhe ſhuld wompull hir heed mony ꝑellis ſaw bout matimony ther ordand woman ſhuld called lefull wyfe bot ſhe wer bleſſed preſt elentherꝰ martir wos pope aft er sother xv yere wich ordand criſtyn men ſhuld fureſe mete reſonabull wos mannys mete nota alſo man vn acuſed acrime ſhuld put dignite degre til conuyckyt thurgh enſampull criyſt wich keppid ſtyll iudas ſcaryoth cuſed criſt knaw hym gylty ſum euer among apoſtils dyngnite ſeruis boode firme ſtabull ſend alſo legatis vn lucie kyng bretan wich baptiſed hym pepull fagus domianus legate wich pope ſent fyrſt preched englond criſtyndom durit bretan cc yere vn tyme diocliſion emprour ſent albone wos martired marchus antonius lucius comodus wer emprours bot marcus dyed anone bown ſhuld reſaue god eſtyr day ons •• yere alſo ordant ye veſſell awter ſhuld glas tyn tre o ī old tyme cōſecracion glorius blode wos made ī tre veſſell tyme paſſit worſhip chirche grew glaſin caliſtus marter roman pope zepherinus v yere ordand cimitori via apia wher moni martires beried alſo hee ordand faſt emering dayes keped antonius aurelius wos empeour iij yere man lacked kīd lechory laſt wos martired emong gret multitude pepull myſſecheuus leuyng antonius macus rened hym vij yere man leued obſtinatl • therfor wos kylled wos prediceſſur alexander wos emprour antonius regned xiij yere man bi inſtance mother criſtin woman techyng origen wiche come rome conuert hir· wos made ſo good vn criſtyn mē ſoffrid haue ther counſels ther prayer ſelfe bot neu er laſe tyme curſed officer hym made mony martirs anno domini ccxliiij vrbanus wos pope caliſto viij yere old ̄ yong wos veriy vertuus halouyd veſſell chirche made gold ſyluer man laft pope heod ̄ went agrippam ̄ xim virgin hym ̄ clargy ſaid laft dignite holines bot appetite tho virgin ̄ wrote hym boke popis ther virgin wos martired tho virgin poncianus marter ſuccedid vrbanus ̄ ordant pſalmys ſhuld ſaied day nyght thee chirche god preſt ſhuld ſay confiteor fore thee maſſe anteros martir wos pope aft er man man ordand biſſhop myght remeued vn made lyfe martirs writtyn wos ſlayn beried cimitory ſeut calixt maximiaꝰ aſclepio rignat britannia annis quaſi triginta vſque ad aduentum conſtancij latim vacat philip wos emꝑour hym philip choeſſe hī philip ſon regned vij yere wer fyrſt empr • urys euer wer criſtyned ̄ ſlayn hoſt bequethe hyr treſour ther deth hit ſhuld diſpoſid poer men ſent laurens aſſynacion maſter pope deꝑtid treſour bowt rome wich gret cauſe martirdome vt quid dicunt decius wos emprour iij yere hym cornelius martir roman wos pope aft er fabius iij yere man toke vp bodyes petre paule gret honour put worſchipfull place beata lucina lucius wos pope aft er cornelius iij yere hym lityll writtyn gallus ſon volucianus wer emprours ij yere fought emilianus wer ſlayn emilianꝰ thrid moneth wos ſlayn valerian wos emprour ſon galiene xv yere man wos vertuus manly begīnyng bot aft er wos geuyn vice moch wricchidnes ſo ſon galiene valerian went vn ye lōd perſe ther gret blod martirs wich ſpied wos takyn kyng perci whē take hym put bothe euyn kepid hym gret bondage thys intent kepyd ſo eu er ſhuld ryde valerian ſhuld ly doune ſhuld ſet foot vpon bake wold take horſe herd galiene ſon wos left rome yt cauſed wos ſo cruell ayenes criſtyn men ¶and wos viij ꝑſecucion chirche made thi emprour made roman lee ther kyngdoms thee wich wer neuer recouered ayene emprour gen er peſtelans wos thurgh world ther treſpas stephanꝰ merter lucius wos pope iij yere man ordaned yt man ſhuld vſe haloed clothis bot worſhip god sextus marter roman wos pope sſtephanus ij yere man ordant maſſe ſhuld ſayed vpon autor wich fore wos died dyoniſius roman pope aft er hym ij yere man deuided perichys chyrche yerdes aſſigned chirchis certayn preſtis felix martir wos pope aft er dyoniſius ij yere ordaned memori martirs maſſes ſhold ſayed alſo ordant thee dedicacion chirche eu er yere ſhold ſayed claudius emprour valerianus ſubduid goth nobully deſſeſet anno criſti cclxxiiij euticianus mertir wos pope felex viij yere man ordand corne benys ſhuld bliſſed thee auter bereid iijc ̄ xl iiij martirs hondes aurelius wos emprour claudius v yere aurelius fyrſt criſtī men wos gentyll wherfor victori eu er place gloriuſly wos deſſaued curſit mē purſued criſtīmen myghttely namly fraunce ther bood aft er neu er good fortune bot ſlayn wos ix perſecuciō ye cherche criſtin fayeth tacitus wos emꝓur man wos bot regned bot iij monethes ſlayn ponto probus wos emprour hym v yere iiij monethes man recou er ed fraunce yene wych occupyed barbory men ̄ yaf pānonias licens haue vynyerdes whē made almoſt thynges well pee ſayed knyghttes wyth litell tyme ſhall neceſſari anone hee wos ſlayn syrmiū carus hys ij ſonnys carmus numerianus wer emprours probus bot ſoyn war deid ̄ ther fadre wos dronchid ij ſonnys wer ſlayn thes iij regned bot ij yere dyaclician maximian cō thes iij emprours tho regned eſt weſt fyrſt thing dioclecian brent criſtyn menys bokys myght fonden thes ij tyrantes harme criſtyn men euer ony x yer laſted ther perſecucion o red xxx dayes xxm men wer ſlayn criſtis cauſe ī englond faith wos almoſt deſtruyed tyme maximian gaius wos pope enticianꝰ man ordant man ſhuld accuſe biſſhope clarke ſeculari iuge pagon herityke ſhuld accuſe criſtyn man alſo ordant wos worthe ſhuld aſcēde gre gre ord er fyrſt benet collet ſubdekī dekī ̄ preſt laſt wos martired vndyr dioclicion ¶arcellinus amartir wos pope gayus xi yere iiij monethes man wos perſecutit ſoor dreid deth offrid iij cornys encenſe ſacrifice ydols afterward opynly repentid ſuffyrd payn deth fayth chyrche god bodi lay vn beried iij dayes dreid curſe god aft er thurgh uiſion ſent petre ̄ marcell beried peturs foote wos ¶and knawe ye ther weer xxxiij pope roome martired yche petre wos fyrſt melchiades wos laſt thē wos laudabull man gregori deſire biſſhoprik galerius wos emprour dioclicion ij yere another hym called conſtancius ſo wos empyre tho dayes deuidee conſtance aft er conquered spaȳ come gret breton ther wedded kynges dought er gat gret conſtantine ſame conſtacius died breton lyeth yorke o martin ſays crounycls left lyue conſtantine wos getyn elyn wos kyng bretayn fraunce circa annū domini iijcviij silueſter wos pope aftet melchiades glorius confeſſor mony way worſſhipped chirche god writyng glorius man victorius bataill gouernyng commyn pepull wos veray wiſſe neceſſite beleue compayr dewout pytty holines ſo writtyn bokys holi docturs dowt nowmbred emong ſentis grekys ſayn end lyfe wos made monke ye may heir hī crounyclis englond hee wos kyng ī englond helena quene moder conſtantine repayred yene holy croſſe tyme ſhe made lxx colleg ſhe glorified ſtate holi chirche nycholas byſſhop mirree cete hole man wos tyme athanaſius wos tyme biſſhop alexandrin glorius doctor made cymbalum quicumque vult ſaluꝰ eſſe etcc marcus pope aftar silueſter ij yere viij monethes man ordaned cred ſhuld opynly ſong chirch biſhop hoſtienſe ſhuld conſecrate pope ſhuld werre pall iulius wos pope marcus xi yere man wos exiled x yere ſuffred deth vnder conſtātyne ſecūd eonſtantinus ij bretheren regned xxiiij yere laſt end wos ꝑu er tit bi heryſe aryanes biſſhope called euſebi purſued chirche god ſtrongly end man wos ſhuld go conſtantinople gret counſell ī wich thought haue condempned biſhop clerkys trew beleue went fore vn chambyr voyed ſich thynges natur requireth anone ſodenly bowel fell ther wos deid o ye liberius pope iulius xix yere ̄ vij monethes thē wos ſecūd diſcorde chirch tuix liberyn felix heeryſi arrians wich fauyrred leberius conſtancius emprour called ayene liberyn exile cauſe fauered thees heriſe chirch deiecit liberyn toke felix pope odir wos expulſit o harityke chirch bot felix obtenet emprour put ī liberiꝰ expulſit felix felix wos pope deth liberin declared conſtantin emprour heritike none wos martyred ¶and wos fyrſt euer thee chirche rome infamet pope prediceſſurs liberin wer ſentis yaf holy ſampuls iulianus apaſtota wos aft er conſtantyn emprour ij yere viij monethes cleped apoſtata hee fled conſtantyne wiche killep brether fere deth wos made criſtyn man monke bot afterward counſell negromē ser aſked duell whether ſhuld emprour duell ſaid ſhuld emꝑour vpō condiciō yt ſhuld ſake criſtin faith vttyr emny criſtī men ſo yaf leue iues ſhuld byld ayene tempull ſpite criſtyn mē toke goodis yt criſtī mē diſtruied mōy ioninianꝰ wos emꝑour aft er hym viij monethes iulian wos deid hoſt choſe hym emꝑour criſtī man ̄ ſaid wos lefull criſtī mā lord ou er ſo mōy hethī pepull thei anſuerd ſaied rather thē ſhuld forſake empire wold criſtined thꝰ toke dyngnite bot ſone wos deid ̄ ī meruelꝰ maner hee wos laid ī cloſe houſe aft er iornay made ſtone newly whited wt lyme wich made comforth thought fyer charcoill ayre thes ij mor • fond deid valentinian brother balent emprour ioninianus xi yere departed empire ̄ yaf brother eſt keped hym ſelf weſt part balentinianus wos lord iulian apoſtata happid tyme go tempull fals goddis doo ſacrifice myniſteris ſtood therwith water haloid ther giſe wich ſtrenkilled lordis valentenianus ſmot miniſter keſt wet er vpon hym ſayed wos rether defouled ther bi clenſed cauſe iulian exile hī bot lord god opyn confeſſion name rewarded hym empire brother valent fell opinyō wos liue ¶a synodus hundreth l biſſhoppis gedred vnd er damaſe pope conſtantinople ayenes macedomū heritike wich deuyed holy goſt veray god wos credo made ſong holydayes chirche auguſtinus notabull ſarmons epiſtils deceſſid marcianꝰ valentinianus wer emprours tyme vij yere whoys tyme wos gret sinody foro reherſed euſticem dioſcurus wer condempned ¶in tyme marcianus wos emprour rome vortiger wos kyng bretan called englond whoys tyme saxon come bretan made mony kynges wit playn crouniclys vij cauſe tediꝰ mannys reſon reherſe mony diu er ſe namys gedre o vij kynges englond tyme emprours popys ther cronyelis englond ſhall ſet geder tyll becūmyn vn alured whoys tyme danys com ī englond popys emprours thynges thee ſame tyme ſhall ſet gedre circa annū domini iiijcxl ix ¶how wardeyns tho childrin kepe conſtantine ſonnys lad lytell bretan treſon ̄ falſeneſe vortiger engiſt begīnith fift parte cōing danys thys tyme come saxon wer pagons fyrſt bretōnow called englond vnder vortiger wich wos crouned kyng lond time tho thies ij chylder kepyng wich conſtantine ſonnys ſay aurilambros vter thurgh ordinance goſlī biſſhop london ther faderes deth ſay conſtantine durſt duell ī thys land tho chyld conueyd vn kyng lityll breton moch tho wyſe treſon vortiger tho wos made kynd thurgh conſtance ther eldyr brother wos ſlayn wherfor hundreth knyghtes pehites wer put deth beren blame vortiger wiſt ther nether conſented ¶and ſo kepers tho tow childer dred leſt vortiger wold put deth thurgh treſon falſnes done ther brother forne therfore wer lad ouer litell bretan ̄ kyng reſaued moch honowr let noriſſh ̄ ther duelled till become fair knyghtes ſtrong fers thought auenged vpon deth conſtantine ther brother ſaw ther tyme ſo ye ſhall tell afterward ¶hit wos long aft er yt tidīges come ouer ſee kynred tho hundreth knyghttes pehites wer dampned put deth thu • gh vortig er ī land therfor wer wōdirly wroth ſuore yt wold auenged ther kīnes deth come ī lond wt gret pouer ̄ robbed ī mōy place ̄ killed ̄ ſorow yt myght whan vortig er wiſt made moch ſorow ſore anoyd ī place alſo tydynges come hī aurilambros vter brother ordined aſſembled gret hoſt cum mekell bretan yt ſay land auenged vpō conſtance ther brother deth ī half brought ſo moch ſorow ne wiſt whider wende ¶how engiſt xi thouſand men come land vortiger yafe place called thongcaſtell ſone ſorow tydyng come vortig er yt grete nauye ſtrangers wer ariued ī cūtre kent wylt whens wer ne wherfor wer come land ¶the kyng ſent anone meſſenger thider ſum ſhold cum ſpeke hym wit folk wer axed ī cūtre wold goo ¶ther wer ij brether maſters ̄ princeſ yt ſtrong cōpany yt wos cald engiſt yt horſſe engiſt went kyng told encheſon wherfor wer comen ī land ¶and ſayed ſyr cuntre called saxonie land eermayne wher ſo moch ſorow pepull ſo mony lond may ſuſteyne ¶and maſters prince haue lond gouerne rule make cum men woman boldeſt ben amonges fight beſt may trauaill ī diuerſe landes ¶and ſo ſhul yef hors hernes armuri ̄ thing nedeth aft er ſhall ſay gone contre wher mowe lyuen ther aunceſtres fore ¶and therfor ſir kyng yf ye haue ought company come land ̄ wyth good wil ſerue land kepe help defend enmys yf ye nedeth ¶when vortiger herd tydyng ſayed wold gladly withold vpon ſich couenant myght dalyu er land emnys wold yef reſenable londes wher ſhuld duell eu er engiſt thonked goodly ̄ man er companye xim ſhold duell kyng vortiger moch thurgh ther boldnes deliu er ed land clene emnys tho prayed engiſt kyng ſo mo • h land myght make hym cite ̄ hys meny ¶the kyng anſuerd wos done conceill breton ¶engiſt prayed hym eftſones moche place o myght compaſ ſo thonge ſkyn wher vpon myhht maake maner hym duell ¶and kyng hym granted frely ¶tho toke engiſt bull ſkyn cut ſmale myght thuong round well arayed engiſt preualy ſend letter cuntre wher come fro hondreth ſhippes fyllid men wos ſtrong bold alſo well fightyng batellis ſhuld alſo bryng ronewen doughter wos faireſt creature man myght ſe ¶and tho pepull wos comē ſent aft er toke caſtell moch ioy hym ſelf vpon dey went vn kyng prayed hym ther worthely wold cum ſee new maner made place compaſſed thuong ſkyn ¶the kyng anone graunted hym frely hym went thid er ̄ wos well payed caſtell ̄ fair werke ged er ther eten dronk wt moch ioy ¶and whan nyght come kyng vortiger ſhuld go ī chamare take ther nyghtes reſt ronewen wos engiſt doughter come cup gold ī hir hand kneled fore kyng ſaied hym waſſaill kyng wyſtnot wos mene ne ſhuld anſuer moch hym ſelf ne none breton coud engliſh ſpeke ne vnd er ſtond ſpekyn ſame longage breton done yit ¶neutheles latimer told kyng full vnd er ſtondyng therof waſſale ſhold anſuer drynk haill ¶and wos fyrſt tyme waſſaill drink haill come vp land tym vn tyme well vſed land ¶the kyng vortiger ſaw fairnes ronewen armes laid bowt hir nec iij ſwetly kytſed hir anone right wos namered vpan hir deſired haue hir wif aſked engiſt hir fadre ¶and engiſt granted hym vpon couenant kyng ſhold yef hym cūtre kent thhe er myght duele pepull ¶the kyng graunted preuely good wyll anone ſpouſed ye damyſell yt wos moch ꝯfuſion ſelf ¶and therfore breton become ſo wroth cauſe ſpouſed womā myſbeleue wherfor went hī ̄ nothyng toke kepe ne help hym thing done ¶how vortimer wos vortigers ſon made kyng ̄ engiſt wos driuen vortimer wos ſlayn engiſt went kent ſeiſed land hond hym hys men come lityl bataill crouned hī ̄ made hī kīg ̄ wold ſuffre vortig er longer regne encheſō aliance bituix engiſt ̄ hī britōs ordined gret hoſt driue engiſt cō panie land ̄ yaf hī iij batallis yt fyrſt wos ī kent ther wos lord ſecūd wos tetford ̄ thrid ī ſhire athiſ half cooll ī ¶and ī botell met catagren ̄ horne engiſtes brother ſo ych ſlew bott moch o cūtre wos yef lōg horne thurgh vortiger tho bataill come land ¶and whan vortiger herd tell engiſt come ayene grett pouer lond· aſſemled breton tho went ayens engiſt haue yef hym bataill folke ¶butt engiſt drad ſore breton thei driuen beforne diſcomfited hym ſtrength wherfor engiſt prayd hym loue day ̄ ſayed wos cūyn lād fight haue land ayen might accord wt breton haue luffe grace ¶the kīg vortiger thurgh counſell breton graunted loue day thus wos ordeyned thurgh breton ſaame day ſhuld holdin faſt ſide saliſberi vpon hyll ¶and engitt ſhuld come thidre iiij hundreth knyghtys mo kyng mony wiſeſt men land ¶and yt day kyng come eſtangill called northfolk southfolk merchemerich ſay erldom nicholl ¶the vi leceſtre ſhiere northhamtō ſhiere hertford huntyngdon ¶the vij oxunford glouceſtre wyncheſtre warwik derbyſhire ¶how vortiger went wale bigan ther caſtell wold ſtond morter tempred blod engiſt deꝑted land maner betwen men deliu er ed vortiger priſon ſuffred frely gone whidre wold toke way went wale ther breton ſelf ther ī kepe ̄ defend nede wer ¶maſōs ī haſt tho wer fet ̄ bigan werk vpō ye hill breigh c er te thꝰ fel werk yt ye maſōs made day doun fel nyght ̄ thei wiſt might ther kyng wos ſoro anoyed chance wiſt doen ¶wherfor let ſend wiſeſt clerkis alſo lerned mē yt wer thurgh wale myght found ſhuld hym tell wos beſt done ¶for ſhuld tell wharfor foundment ſo failed vnder werke ſhuld hym tell wos beſt done ¶and wiſeſt men long tyme ſtudied ſayed kyng ſhuld done ſeke chylde borne woman neu er man done chyld ſhuld ſle temꝑ blod mort werk ſo ſhuld werke eu er endure ende ¶how kyng let ſech merlin thurgh wale ſpeke hym kyng herd commanded meſangeres anone wend thurgh wale ſeke chyld yf myght hym fynd ſhuld hym bring forth thē vn hym recorde witnes thyng tak lettres ne wer deſtrobled man ne lette ¶and tho meſſangeres went then ſped ſo faſt thatt come toune called karmardine o paſſed forth ther way funden ij child xxiiij yere age chydīg yf • haſty wordes ſayed donebat quod ye wrong chide ſtrife wyth ¶for ye haue wit ne reſō haue certes merlī ꝙ wit ne reſon make force mē tell ꝯminly ye haue thyng god almygfty ſith ye neuer fadre eu er mau knaweth well mother ¶the meſſingers kynges vortiger herd ſtrife tuix tow gromes axed ſtood beſides whens marlyn wos borne alſo hym noriſſhed folke hem told gret gentyll woman hym bare karmardīe wos called adhan neuer myght man wit fadre ¶when kynges meſſangeris herd tydyng went anone hym wos wardayne toune toold hym kynges letter ſhewed hym wherfor wer comen theder ¶merlyn moder anone wer ſent fore wardayne toune cōmanded ſhuld gone kīg wos ordand maſſengers ¶merlyn moder went then ̄ come vn kyng ̄ ther wer vnderfonge moch honour kyng axed lady yf child wer hir ſon hī begate ¶the lady anſuered full tendirly wepyng ſayed ſhe neuer company man worldly ¶but ſir quod ſhe o wos yong mayden ī faders chambre gret linage wer cōpany yt often tymes wont play ſolace beleft allone chambre wold gone forth byrnyng ſone ¶and tyme ther come fair bachelar ̄ entrid chambre ther allone come wher wiſt neu er ne yit wot dores wer faſt barred game loue ne myght ne pauer defend fro ̄ oft come vn fore ſayed man er ſo begot child neu er myght wit ¶of anſuere merlin wherfor kyng axed whi caſtille myght ſtond gonne ner proue merlin herd mother ſaid ſpake kyng man er ¶sir wos begoten ax ye falleth yow ne nōe wit telleth encheſon wherfor brought wherfore ye haue ſent aft er certis quod kyng wiſe cowncelers haue done vnd er ſtond mort werke haue gone behoueth tempred wt blod foundamēt ſhall faill eu er more· ¶sir quod merlin ye ſle blod temꝑ wt mort ye quod kyng el ſhall neu er caſtell ſtand councelars done vnd er ſtand ¶tho anſuerd merlyn kyng sir ſayed let cum fore tho wiſe concelers wyll preue ſay well ne trewly ¶and wiſe mē wer com marlī axed blod wer encheſon make werke ſtand endure tho wiſe wer abaſhed coud anſuer ¶merlyn tho ſayed kyng sir ſhall tell encheſō wherfor werke thꝰ faleth ̄ may thand ¶ther vnd er montayn ther ye haue belden tour gret pond wat er ye botom ye pond vnd er wat er ther ij dragōs yt white reed yt fighten god ayens werke ¶doo ye myne depe till men come pond doth men take way wat er ye ſhall ſe dragon haue told ged er fightē ayens werke ¶and encheſon wher fore fundament faleth ¶the kyng anone let digge vnd er til yt mē come yt pond ̄ let done way yt wat er ther fond ij dragon marlyn told egorly foughten ged er ¶the white dragon egrely aſſayled reed ̄ laid hī ſo ſtrongly yt myght endure bot drew reſted ī ye ſame caue ¶and reſtyd hym went ̄ aſſayled ye reed dragon angrely held hī ſo ſore yt myght ayens hī endure drew hī reſtid aft er come ayen ye white dragon ſtrongly fought wt reed dragon bote hym euell hym ou er come fled then come ayen ¶off ſyngnificacion thas ij dragon thot wer thee bottom ponde foughten gedre kyng vortig er men ſaugh batayll gret meruell prayd merlyn telle hym myght betoken ¶sir quod merlin ſhall yow tell ¶the reed dragon betokeneth yourſelf white betokeneth folk saxonie fyrſt ye toke held land thatt fightten ayens yow yow haue driuen enchaced ¶but breton linage ouer comen driuen way ſithen commyng ayene ſaxons recouered land held eu er driuen briton lond ther deſtruyed criſtīdō thurght land ¶ye firſt ioy ther cūmynge turned gret damage ſorow ¶for tho ij brethern conſtance wos kyng wich ye let ſla shall cum bi quinzeme paſſed gret pouer litell bretō ſhul venge deth ther brother ̄ ſhall brin yow fyrſt ſarow afterward ſhall ſle gret part saxon ̄ ſhall driue remenant land ̄ therfor abyed ye longer make caſtell ne none werke bot anone go el wher life ſaue god take treuth haue ſayed thinges ſhall fall ¶and vnderſtond ye well aurilanbros ſhall kyng bot ſhall enpoyſened litell tyme ſhale regne ¶of kyng aurilambros purſued vortiger engiſt diden merlen modre deꝑted kyng turned ayen karmardine ¶and ſone aft er tydyngꝭ come breton aurilambros ̄ vter brother wer ariued totteneſſe wyth gret hoſt ¶and anone thee breton aſſemled went vnderfonge aurilambros ̄ vter wt gret nobulnes vn london croned aurilambros made kyng vn hym humage anon axed wher vortiger kyng myght founden wold avenged brother deth aft er wold vpō paynems ¶and told hym vortig er wale ſo lade hym thid er ward ¶vortiger wiſt well tho brether come hī conquere fled then ī caſtell wos cald gerneth ſtood vpon hygh mantayn ther hym held • ¶aurilambros vter brother ther folke beſeged thē caſtell full long tyme caſtell ſtrong well arayed ¶soo laſt keſt wildfyre brent houſes men ther aray o mych o caſtell vortiger brent among ſo died moch ſorow ¶tho engiſt kent regned ther hard tydyng anone fled ̄ wold haue gone scotland haue ſocour aurilambros men met ī northcuntre yaf hym bataill engiſt men defended while myght ̄ folke wer diſcomfited ̄ ſlayn • ta ſon fled vn yorke aurilambros hym foloed egrely otta litell ayens ſtod aft er ward put hym merci ¶and arilambros vnd er feng hī ̄ men yaf cuntre galeway ī scotlond ther duelled ¶the kyng arilambros wēt thurgh ye lond put away name engiſtland engiſt aft er name called tho let call ayen gret bretan let make ayen chirches houſes relegion caſtelis cite burghes ̄ tounes saxon deſtruyed come londō let make walles cite wich engiſt folke caſten doune ¶the breton lad hym mount anbrian ſom tyme houſe religion tho wos deſtruyed thurgh paynyms ¶wher knyght called anbry ſome tyme wos found houſe therfor hyll wos called mount brian wos called ambreſbury ſhall ſo euermore ¶how aurilambros redreſſe lond gret bretan deſtrayed thurgh saxon kyng aurilambros let mēd ̄ redreſſe houſe amleſburi ther put monkes ther bennonnys littell plaace wos called saliſburi ther saxon kylled bretans wher engiſt ſhuld haue made loue day ī wich tyme ther wer ſlayn mlxi knyghtes thurgh treſon engiſt ¶the kyng therof gret pitte th • ught make ī mynd monumēt ſton myght endure ye wordes end thing toke ther counſell ther wos beſt done ¶tho ſpake kyng byſſhop london wos called ternekyn ſhuld enquere aft er marlyn coud beſt tell thīg myght beſt made· merlin aft er wos ſought ̄ foūd ̄ come ye kyng ¶and kyng toold hī monumēt yt wold haue made ¶tho anſuerd merlin kīg ̄ ſayed ther bene gret ſtonys ī irland ̄ long vpō ye hill kyan yt mē called geāts karoll ̄ wer ī place thei ther wold endure eu er ī remēbrance thoo knyghtes yt heir entered ¶per • oy ꝙ kīg hard ſtones ī land ī irland ¶soth qd merlin ¶but ī land ther none ſoch geantes ſet grete good ſelf eu er tyme wer woundet ī ony man er hurt weſſhen ſtones wt hote wat er weſſhe ther anoon wer hole ¶how breton wēt ſech gret ſtons ī irland thes breton herd thing went ſwore emong wold gonne ſeche tho ſtonnes toke vter kynges brother ther cheftayn vm men merlin counſelled go vn irland ſo diden ¶and kyng irland wos cald guillomer herd tell ſtrangers wer ariued ī lond aſſē bled gret pouer ̄ fought ayens folke diſcomfited ¶the bretans went till come moūt kylian climed vp vn moūt ¶but ſaw ſtones man er ſtood gret meruell ſayed bitwyn ſelf man ſhuld hem remeue ſtrength ne engyne ſo huge wer ſo long merlin thurgh craft remeued ̄ brought ī ther ſhippes ̄ come ayene land merlin ſet ſtones ther kīg wold haue ſet ſame maner ſtoden irland ¶and kyng ſaugh made thanked merlyn richeli rewarded place let call ſtonhenge eu er ¶how paſſent wos vortigers ſone kyng guillomer come land tratour called cappa enpuyſened kyng aurilambros men ſhall vnd er ſtand ſtat paſſent vortigers ſone leued ſame tyme come land gret pouer ariued north cuntre wold ben venged faders deth vortiger ¶and ſtrongly truſted vpon componye brought hym land germayne conquered north cuntre vn yorke ¶and kyng aurilambros herd aſſembled gret pouer breton went fight paſſent wos diſcomfited pepull paſſent aſcapped thēs wt ſum men fled then irland come kīg guillomer prayed hym help ſocour kyng granted hym good ſayed wold help hym vpō yt couenant ſelf muſt gone pouer breton wold venge vpon breton rather cum land token ſtones ſtrength called geantes karoll kyng guillomer let ordē ſhippes went ſee xvm men ariued wale gon rob moch ſorow ¶hit befell ſo kyng arilombros lay ſeke wynchſter myght helpe ſelf ſent name vter brother pouer helpe wale thed er ward went moch o myght kyng irland paſſent herd tell aurilambros ſeke hym ther come sarizen called coppa ſayed sir duell ye pee hoſt ̄ hyght thurgh quentize ſhall ſle kyng aurilambros ſeke ſayed paſſent ye doo ſo ſhal yow richely auaunce ttoraur coppa put vpon abbyt relegion let ſhaue hym brod croune come vn kynges court ſayed wold help kyng hys maladie· tho ſayed tretour coppa vn kyng sir ben good comforth ſhall yef ſich medicin ye ſhall ſwete anone right luſten ſlepe haue good reſt ̄ thee tratour yaf hym ſich poyſin ſlep anone right died hys ſlepyng ye trator ſayed wold gone feld till wer waked ſo ſcapped way man ſuſpeccion cauſe habbit wos clothed alſo brood ſhauynne croune kynges men wiſt wos deid become wondir ſori faſt ſought tratour myght fynd hym coppa turned ayene hoſt fro whens come ¶when aurilambros deid ſterre morne wos ſeī clere light bught beme wos ſeyne hed horribull dragon kyng aurilambros wos thus deid ̄ enpoyſened wyncheſter morne aft er wos deid bowt tyme prime ther ſeyne ſtere gret clere beme ſterne wos bright er ſon bought beem pered dragōs heed ̄ mouth come ij huge lightes wer bright ony fier brennyng ¶and one beme toward france ſtryght ou er ſee thiderward ¶and beym rome vij bemes full clere long light fier ¶this ſterne ſeyn mony man none wiſt wat betokened ¶vter wos kynges brother yt wos ī wale wt hoſt bretōs ſaw yt ſterre ̄ ye gret light yt yaf wōdred ther gretli myght betokē ̄ let call merlī prayed hī tell myght betoken ¶of betokenyng ſtere merlin ſaw ſtarre ̄ beheld long tyme ſithen quoke weped tendirli ſayed ala ala ſo nobull kyng worthy deid ¶and doo vnd er ſtand aurilambros brother enpeyſened ſe well ī ſterre ̄ yourſelf betokēd bi heed dragō ſeī bought beem yourſelf ſhal kyng ̄ regne ¶and beem ſtandeth toward eſt vnd er ſtōd yt ye ſhall get ſon ſhal conquere al fraunce landes yt belongeth croune fraunce ſhal worthier kyng ̄ honour eu er wos ony auncetours ¶and bi beem ſtrechys toward irland betokened ye ſhall get dought er ſhall quene irland ¶and vij bemes betokene ye ſhall haue vij ſonnis eu er ichon ſhall kyng regne wt moch honour abyde ye longer heir goth yef bataill enmys ̄ fight wt bodely ye ſhall ou er cū haue victori ¶vter thanked hertely merlyn toke men went toward enmy ̄ foughten gedre mortali ſo diſcomfited enmy diſtroyed ſelf kylled paſſent wos vortig er ſon ¶and breton killed guillomer yt wos kyng irland ̄ men ¶and vter anone aft er bataill toke way toward wincheſter done entere aurilambros kīg wos brother ¶but tho body borne ſtonhē ge moch honour done made remembrance pendragon werfor called ſo ye ſhall ouer take wyth loue fe igerne erle cornewaill wife ye deth aurilambros vter brod er wos crouned regned well worthely remembrance dragon wos likened let make ij cum ayene ī man er wiſe ¶wherfor kyng wos full wroth wrath hym deffied deidly enmy erle went then cornewaill wife caſtell tyntagell ¶and kyng let ordin gret hoſt come cornwaill diſtruy erle myght put hym ī ſich caſtell ſtrong well arayed tyntagell wold yeld hym kyng kyng anone beſeged ye caſtel ther duelled xv dayes yt neu er myght ſped eu er thought vpō igerne vpō hir laid ſo moch loue yt wiſt kyng kyng told councell ¶sir qd merlin ſhall done ſo moche thurgh craft yt yt ſhall make cū nyght ī ye caſtell tyntagell ſhall haue lady ¶how vter bigat igerne wos erlis wife cornewaill arthur kyng merlyn thurgh craft coud changed kynges figure ī likneſſe erle ̄ vlfyn garlois chā berlayn figure iordan wos erles chambirlayn yche wos tranſfigured od er lekeneſſe ¶and merlyn ſo done ſayed kyng sir qd may ye go ſodenly caſtell tyntagell axen entre ther haue kīg toke priueli hoſt gou er ne ̄ lede knyght mich loued toke way toward caſtell wt hī toke vlfȳ chābirlayn ̄ merlin ¶and come theder porter went bene hys owne lord ̄ tyme come go bede ¶the kyng went bede igerne erles wife dyd hir bigat vpon hir ſon wos called arthur ¶and vpō morow kyng toke leue lady went ayen hys hoſt ¶and ſame nyght kyng lay igerne bedde yt wos erles wife kynges men yaf gret aſſaut vn caſtell erle men manli defended laſt befell ſo ſame aſſaut erle hym ſelf wos ſlayn caſtell taken ¶and kyng none turned ayen tyntagell ſpouſed igerne moch honor made hir quene ſone aft er tyme come ſhe ſhuld deliu er ed beyr child ſon wos called arthur aft er gat doughter called amya ̄ ſhe come age nobull baron called aloth wos lord leon wed hir ¶when vter long tyme regned ther come vpon hī gret ſekenes wer ſorow ¶and ī meyn tyme tho yt kepe otta wos engiſt ſon oſſa brother tho wer priſon let gone gret yeftes yt hom yaf went ¶and tho ij bretheren wer aſcappid come ayen ther cūtre ordined grert pouer begon eftſones vpon kyng ¶how kyng vter cheſe aloth kepe land breton while wos ſeke moch myght ſeknes moch kyng vter wos ſeke myght nott help hym ſelf ordined aloth ſon eleyn tho choſen wardeyn cheftayn folke ſo anone bretans aſſemled gret hoſt yaf batell otta folke otta laſt wos diſcomfitid ¶hitt befell thus afterward thes breton dedignacion aloth wold hī attendant wherfor king wos anoid wond er ſ • let put hym litter hoſt emonges folke ¶and lad hī veroloyn tho fair cite ther yt ſent albon wos wt māli defended ¶the kīg let ordeyn gōnes engynes brek walles ̄ walles wer ſo ſtrōg yt nothīg myght myſdoo ¶otta ̄ pepull gret deſpite yt kīg liggyng ī lytter beſeged toke concell monges ſtand vp ī morow ̄ cū ̄ yef batall kīg ſo ̄ ī yt batall wer otta oſſa ſlayn tho yt aſcapped lyue fled ī ſcotland made colegū ther chyftayn ̄ ſaxons wer lyue ̄ aſcaped fro bataill brought ayan gret ſtrength emōges ſayed yt kīg vter wer deid ſhuld well cōquere ye land amonges thought enpoſin kīg ordeyned mē dede yaf yeftes gret plente thyng done ordined hem thid er ward ther yt kīg duellīg clothed hem ī pouer wede bett er ſped therlyd purpoſe neu er theles ther falſnes quātize might neu er cū nyghthe kīg ¶but ſo laſt aſpied yt ye kīg drāknōe oth erlycour wat er cler wel yt negh beſide ¶and thes fals tratours vpō day preuali wēt ye wel put therī poyſon ſo yt ye wat er enpoyſened anōe aft er o kīg dronkyn ye wat er begō fuell ̄ ſone aft er died ̄ o mōy dronk wat er died alſo ¶and anōe wos aſpied folke toune let ſtop well eu er ¶when king wos dred folk bere hī stonhenge gret ſolempnite biſſhoppis barōs werther hī bery beſides aurilambros brother aft er turned ayen tho eu er ychone ſend arthur ſon ̄ made kīg land moche reu er ence fadres deth xvij yere regne ¶how arthur wos ſon vter crouned fadre deth drofe colegrin saxon cheldrik almayne lond arthur wos made kyng ye lond wos bot yong age xv yere wos fair bold doughty body meke folke wos good curtas large ſpendyng made hym wonderly well beloued among men ther wos need ¶and begone regne ſwore ye ſaxons neu er ſhuld haue pee ne reſt till driuē lond aſſembled gret hoſt faught wt colegrī wich aft er time otta wos deid ſaxons mayntened colegrin wos diſcomfited fled vn yorke toke toune ther hym held ¶and kyng beſeged hī ther myght nothyng ſped cite wos ſo ſtrong toune kepped cite well orpedly ¶and meyn tyme colegrin let toune bladulf fled hym ſelf cheldrik wos kyng almayne haue ſocour ̄ kyng aſſemblid agret pouer ̄ come ariued ſcotlond vc ſhippis whē arthur wiſt tidīg pouer ̄ ſtrength nough fight ayens cheldk let ſege went london ſent anone letter king litill bretan called hoel nepheu ſuſtres ſon ſhuld cū hī wt pouer yt myght aſſemblid gret hoſt ariued ſouthinton ¶and kīg arthur wiſt wos glad nough ̄ went ayens reſaued moch honour ſo tho ij hoſtes met aſſembled toke ther way euen vn nichol cheldrik beſeged wos taken ¶and come vpō cheldrik pepull wiſt wer yt wer ̄ egrely aſſeilled ¶the kīg cheldrik ̄ meny defēdid māly bi ther pouer kīg arthur mē kylled ſo mōny ſaxōs neu er wos ſeyne ſich ſlaught er ¶and cheldrik ̄ men yt wer left lyue fled way ¶and arthur purſued droue oute wod myght ferther paſſe cheldrik men ſaw well wer brought moch diſeſe ̄ yold arthur man er wyſe ſhold take ther hors ther armur muſt onli gone ō fote ther ſhippis ſo wold gone home ther land neu er cū ayen land ¶and vpon aſſurance thyng yeuen hym good hoſtag • ¶and arthur coūcell men granted thyng reſaued hoſtages ther vpō wēt ther ſhippes ¶and wer hy ſee wynd changed deuell wold thei turnd ther nauy come yen land ariued totneſſe wēt ſhippes toke land clen robbed moch pepull ſlew taken armur myght find ſo wēt forth till thei come vn bathe men toune ſhittē faſt ther yates nold ſuffre cum toun defendit well orpedly ayens ¶how arthur yaf bataill vn saxon com ayen ī land ̄ beſeged toune bathe ̄ ou er come arthur herd tydyng let hong anone hoſtages left hoel bretan nepheu kepe marche toward scotlond halfe pepull hym ſelf wēt helpe reſcu toune bathe come thed er hee yaf ſtrong bataill childrik kylled almoſt peple had· man myght hym withſtond ne endure vnd er thee ſtroke ſwerd ¶and ther bothe wer ſlayn colegrin ̄ bladud brether ¶and cheldrik fled then wold haue gone ſhippis arthur wiſt toke xm knyghtis cador erle cornwaill let ̄ ſtop cumming ¶and arthur hym ſelf went toward marche ſcotlād meſſing er told hī yt ſcottys beſeged hoil bretan ther lay ſeke therfor haſted hym thed er ward ¶and cador purſued aft er cheldrik toke er might come vn ſhyppis kylled cheldrik pepull ¶and cador done viage haſted hī ayen faſt o myhht towardes arthur fond hym scotland ther reſcued hoel britan ſcottys fer wt mounref ther held arthur purſued ̄ fled then lymoigne wer thatt cūtre lx iles gret plente briddis ̄ gret plente egels wer woned cry fight ged er make gret noyſe whan folke come rob land moch o myght ſo scottis wer ſo gret rauenours yt toke al yt thei might fīd ī ye lād lymoign wt ani ſparīg ther charged ayen folke scotland wende ¶how kīg arthur axed merlin auēturs vi laſt kīgꝭ yt wer regne ī englond land ſhuld enden▪ sir qd merlin yere incarnacion ihū criſt mccxv ſhall come lamb wyncheſtr yt ſhall haue white tong ̄ trew lippi ̄ ſhall haue writē hert holineſſe ¶this lam ſhall make mony goddis houſes ſhall haue pee moſt ꝑt lyfe ſhal make faireſt place world tyme ſhall fulli made end ¶and ī ye end life wolf ſtrange land ſhall hym moch harme ̄ ſorow thurgh wer end lamb ſhall maſter thurgh help red fox yt ſhall cum northweſt ſhall ou er cum ̄ wolf ſhall dy wat er tyme lamb ſhal lyue bot ſhal die ¶his ſeede ſhall ſtrange land ̄ thee land ſhall gou er nour litel̄l̄ tyme tyme ſhall come dragon melled wyth mercy eke wyth wodeneſſe ſhall̄ haue berde goot ſhall̄ yef ī englond ſhadow ſhall̄ kepe land colde ̄ hete ̄ foot ſhall ſet wyke ̄ london ſhall enbrace habitacions ſhall opyn mouth toward wale ̄ trimbilyng hidour mouth eres ſhall ſtrech toward mony habitacions cūtres breth ſhall full ſuete ſtrange land ¶and ī tyme ſhall reuers renne blod brayn ̄ ſhall make ī place land walles ſhall moch harme vn ſeed aft er tyme ¶then ſhall ther cum pepull owt north weſt regne ſhall lad thurgh wikked hare dragon ſhall doo croune kyng aft er ward ſhall fle ower ſee cummyng ayene dred dragon ¶̄ ī tyme ſon ſhall reed blode mē ſhall ſe thurgh world yt ſhall tokyn gret peſtylence deth folke thurgh dynt ſuerd pepull ſhall bene fader le tile tyme dragon die thurgh hair ſhall meue ayens hym vn end life ſhall fully endit ī tyē ¶this dragō ſhal hold ī tyī beſt bodi world ſhall die ſides march ſtrange land land ſhall duell fad er le wt good gou er n men ſhall wepe deth ile ſhepey vn hauen mareil ¶wharfor ala ſhall ther ſong fadroles folke ſhall ouer lyuen land deſtruied aft er dragon ſhall cū goot kar ſhal haue horne berd ſiluer ther ſhall cum noſthrell domp ſhall tokyn hunger ̄ ſorow gret deth pepull moch land begynnyng regne ſhall waſted ¶this goot ſhall go ou er france ſhall opene flour lyfe deth tyme ther ſhall riſe egle cornwaill ſhal haue fetres golde pride ſhal pere land ̄ ſhal deſpiſe lordes blood ſhal flee ſhamfully bere gauerſech aft er ſhal made breggis men vpon coſtes ſee ſtonys ſhuld fall fro caſtels ̄ mony tounes ſhall made playn ¶in tyme ſhall ſeme ye bere ſhall brenne ̄ bataill ſhall done vpō armes ſee feld ordeyned ſheld ¶and bataill ſhal die mōi whitte heedis wherfor batal ſhall called white batiill ¶and forſayed bere ſhal̄ done goot moch harme ̄ ſhal̄ cū ſouthweſt blod ſhal̄ goot leſe moch ̄ land till time ſhendſhip ſhal̄ hī ou er cū ſhal clothe lion ſkyn ſhal̄ wyn loſt ther ¶for pepul̄ ſhal cū northweſt ſhal̄ make goot ſo ſoyr drad hee ſhal venge enmys thurgh cuncel two owles fyrſt ſhal̄ perel vn done old owle ſhall wend away certayn tyme aft er ſhal cum ayen land ¶thes two owles ſhall gret harme mōy ſo thei ſhal̄ councel goot arere ayens forſayed bere ̄ laſt goot owles ſhal̄ cum burton vpon trent ſhal̄ wend ouer dred bere ſhal fle ſwan fro company burton toward north ther ſhall wt hard ſhoure ſuan ſhal̄ taken ſlayn wt ſorow bere taken heded alther next neſt ſhall ſtand vpon broken brige ſon ſhall caſt bemys mony ſhall hym ſeke vertu hym ſhall cū ¶in ſame ſhal̄ die ſorow care pepul land ſo mony landis ſhal vpō bolder afterward tho two owles ſhal moch harme forſayd flour lyfe ̄ hir ſh̄al̄ lede diſtreſſe ſo ſhe ſhall paſſe ou er ſee fraunce make pee betwen thee goot flourdeliſe ther ſhe ſhall duell til tyme hir ſeed ſhal cum ſech hir ſhall ſtyl till tyme ſh̄al hem clothe wt grace ſhall ſech owles ̄ ſhal put deſpitous deth ¶and ſhall goot brought diſeſe grett anguiſſh ſorew ſhall leue life goot ſhall cum wyndeſore bore ſhall haue hed white lion hert pytuus lokīg ¶his viſage ſhal̄ reſte ſeke mē breſt ſhal ſtāchīg therſt therſty worde ſhal goſpell bering ſhal meke lamb ¶in fyrſt yere regne ſhal haue gret payne iuſtifie vn trew tyme ſhall land multiplied aliandes ¶and bore thurgh ferſeneſſe hert ſhal̄ haue ſhall make wolfe becum lambis ſh̄al̄ called thurgh world bore holines ferſnes nobulnes ̄ mekenes ſhal done meſurably ſhal vn burgh ieruſalem ſhal whette teth vpon yates paris vpō iiij landes spayn ſhal tremble dred gaſcoyne ſhall ſwet fraunce ſhal put winge gret tayll ſhall reſt englond ſoftely almayn ſhall quake dred ¶this bore ſhal yef mantel ij tounes englond ſhall make reu er rene blod brayn ſhal make mony medous reed ſhall get moch aunceſtres deid ſhal beyr iij crounes ſh̄al put land gret ſubieccion aft er ſh̄al releued tyme ¶this bore aft er deid doughtynes ſhal ētered coloyn land ſhall fulfilled al good boor ſhall cum lamb ſh̄al haue foot leed heed bra hert loppe ſwynes ſkī hard ī tyme land ſhall pee fyrſt yer regne ſhal make cite world ſh̄al ſpeke ther ¶this lamb ſhall leſe tyme gret paart land thurgh hidous wolfe ſhall recou er yeue lordſhip egle land egle ſhal well gouerne till tyme prid ſhall ou er cum ala ſorow ſhal die brethers ſuerd aft er ſhall land fal forſayd lamb yt ſhall gou ¶in fyrſt yere regne ſhal haue good grett plente land toward alſo land ſhal̄ haue gret preſyng til̄ tyme ſhal̄ ſuffre pepul̄ lyue mich pride chaſtiſyng wherfor god wyl̄ wroth ¶than ſhall ariſe vp dragon north ſhall ful̄ fers ſhal̄ meve ayens forſayd moldwarp ſhal̄ yef bataell vpō ſtone ¶this dragon ſholl gadre ayen company wolf ſhal̄ cum weſt meve ayens tho forſayd moldwerp ſied ſo ſhall dragō bynd ther tayles ged er ¶than ſhal̄ cum lion owt irland ſhal fall companie wt hem ſhall trembull land ſhal called englond aſpyn leef ̄ tyme ſhal caſtels fellid doune vpō thamyſe ſhall ſeme way land ſhall ye moldwarp ſhall haue man er pouer ſaf onli ſhip wher mawend ¶and aft er ſhall gone lond whan ſee wt draw aft er ſhall yef thrid part lond haue fourth part pee reſt aft er ſhal life ſorow life tyme ¶and ī tyme hote bathe ſhal̄ becō cold aft er ſhall molwarp die auentou • ſli ſodanli la ſorow ſhall drowned flod ſee ſeed ſhall become fadreles ſtrange lond euermore ſhall land deꝑted iij partes ſay wolfe dragon lyon ¶and ſo ſhal euer ſhall land called land conqueſt ſo ſhall rightfull heyris englond ende ¶how arthur ouer come guillomer kyng irland ſcotes become men guillomer kyng irland hard tidyngꝭ kyng arthur entred glaſtenbury ordeyned gret pouer iriſſh men come ſee iriſſh pepull ſo come scotland ouer ſee ariued faſt ther kyng arthur wos hoſt anone wyſt ther went towardes yaf bataill ou er come anone right guyllomer fled men ayen irland ¶and done ̄ diſcomfited arth• turned ayen ther wos place ther left scotys wold haue ſlayn biſſhoppes abbotes folke cuntre lady open heed cō befor kyng arthur cried mercy ſayed ſir gentill kȳg myghty haue mercy pytte vpon u o ſelfe right law hold maynten criſtindom full gret diſhonour ſhuld kyll beleueth al̄ myghty god ye done goddis loue haue mercy pytte v ſuffre v haue moch ſorow pyne saxones mony tyme paſſed thurgh lond bot ynough often tymes haue v done ſerow diſeſe ¶for caſteles haue taken beſtes ſlain eten moch harme haue v done ye wold v kyll hit wer honour kyng kill cry mercy ¶for ynough ye haue done v v ou er cūmyn loue god ye wyll ſuffre v life ̄ haueth merci criſtē peple yt beleuen ī criſt o ye doo ¶whē kīg arthur herd ſorow pytte yaf liyfe lym harme fell doune fete ̄ kyd become leige men toke homage ¶and aft er kyng arthur turned ayene hoſt come vn yorke ther bydyng made viage ¶and tho yaf loegers aloth ſpouſed ſuſtre yeftes gret plente tho gawen coſin bot yong age men ſeruid yaf rich yeftes thanked moch ther good ſerueſſe ¶how kyng arthtr ſpouſed gūnore wos gūnores coſī erle cornwaill aft er conqured guillomer irland arthur brought land pee reſt good ſtate wos well eu er cuntre tho toke ̄ wedded wife called gūnor ̄ made hirquene fair lady gentill cador erle cornwaill noriſſhid chambre wos coſin neu er child gedre neu er theles kyng arthur loued hir wond er well derly ¶and anone o wynt er paſſed let aſſemble agret hoſt baron ſayed wold wend irland conqure land ̄ taried long ne paſſed ou er irland ¶and guillomer kyng let aſſemble gret hoſt yaf bataill kyng arthur guillom wos diſcomfited yeld kyng become man hī feaulte homage held land fro yt tyme forward ¶and aft er paſſed kyng arth• forthermore cō quered gutland iſland toke homage folke ye land ̄ ther duelled xij yere pee regned ioy myrthe ther wered man ne woman vpon hī ¶and become ſo curtas large honorabull emprours court rome ne none od er thurgh world wos accompted kyng arth• ony man wiſt ne none ſo well pr • ſed ¶and therfor beſt knyghtis man er landes come vn ther duel̄ reſſaued good reuerence ¶and knyghtys ſo good nomā knew werſt therfor kyng arthur made round table ſhuld ſit ther mete ſhuld elike hie euenly ſerued tabull yt none ſhuld make vaūce yt werhier ¶and kyng arthur thatt table briton ̄ frenſhmē norman ̄ flemynges burgōs mauſers ̄ loherms landes half monte go rye lād breton ̄ ye gret cornwail̄ wale irland ̄ ſcotland ̄ ſhortely tell lādes yt wold worſhip cheualrie ſeche come kyng arthur courte ¶how kyng arthur went fraunce conquered yt land froll roman kylled syth befell kyng arthur thurgh conceill baron lordis wold go conquire fraunce tho called galle thurgh roman tho held land ther pouer ther gou er nance ̄ roman take yt land nobul̄ knyght worthy bodi yt wos called froll ̄ wiſt yt arthur come ordend hoſt gret pouer ̄ fought wt kīg ̄ folke wer diſcōfyted fled vn paris ̄ entred cite ̄ cloſed yates ther hem held ¶arthur wyſt yt frol̄ wos gone paris purſued aft er come thed er ̄ hī beſeged cite ſo ſtrong wel̄ araied tho yt wer therin defēded well manli ¶kȳg arthr duelled thermore thē moneth ther wos ſo moch peple ī cite ̄ diſpēdid al̄ ther vitails yt wer ī ̄ ſo gret hunger bicom amōges yt died wond er thikke withī cite hunger come • frol prayed accorded kyng arthur haue pee wold yelde vn toune alſo ¶froll ſaw longer myght hold toune ayens ther wil̄ truſt gretli vpō ſtrēgth ̄ ſēt kīg arthur ſh̄uld cum fight body body ſo ſhuld deꝑte fraunce betwene two ¶kyng arthur anone grāted ̄ wold none peple vndertoke bataill hī ¶and vpon morn bothe come well araied paris ther ſhuld fight anone ſmyten ged er ſo ferſly ſo well foughten ſidis man coud deme better ¶and ſo befell froll yaf arthur ſuch ſtroke kneled ground wold nold o frol̄ withdrew ſwerde wounded kyng arthur forhed blood fell doune eyn face ¶arthur anone ſtert vp hertely felt hurt man ſemed almoſt wo • toke tabourne good ſuerd ̄ drow vp high ̄ yaf froll ſuch ſtroke ther clafe hed doun ſholdres ſo helme myght warent ſo fell doune deid place ¶and thē tho cite made gret ſorow froll eu er ichon yeld kyng arthur toune alſo become men humage feaulte ̄ vnd er fenge toke good hoſtages ̄ kyng arthur aft er went forth hoſt conquered augien angiers gaſcoyn pehito nauerne burgon berri lotherne turyn peithers land fraunce cōquered holli ¶and whē cōquerd ̄ taken bi humages feautes turned ayen paris ̄ ther duelled long tyme ordined pee long tyme ou er al̄ cūtre thurgh fraunce ¶and whē pee wos made ou er al̄ thurgh noble kynghthod yt alſo worthines ¶and mā werhe neu er ſo gret lord durſt meue ayenſt hī nod er ariſe make ye lōd france ī quiet ī pe woned ther ix yere mō • gret wond er ̄ reproued mōy proud men lither tirantis chaſtiſed afterther deſeruiſe ¶how kīg arthr auaūced al̄ mē yt trauild ī ser uis aft er ward befell thus eſtren ther held feſt paris richly gan auaunce knyghtis ther ſeruice holpen comqueſt ¶he yafe ſtoward wos called key augien angiers bedeler botler yaf normandie tho wos called neuſtrie holdyn chamberlayn yaf flaund er mance dorell coſyn yaf boloyne richard nephu yaf pountif yaf large landis feys wer eſtate ¶and arthur thus knyghtis feffed auerill next ſueyng come ayene bretan land whitſontied nex ſewyng councell baron wold cronned kīg glomergon held ſolempne feſt let ſompne knyghtis erles baron ſhuld come thedre eu er ychon ̄ ther scaterkyng ſcotland cadwere kyng ſouthwales forne neu er none ſuch ne ſo ſolempne laſted xx day wt moch honour myrth ¶of lett er wos ſent rome prid kīg arthr thrid day kyng arthur ſat mete amang kynges amonge ſittyn feſt byfo • come xij eldren vpon life lymme thou haſt rome amendis make thy myſdedis thou haſt done ¶and ſo thow cum ſhall paſſe hill ioye ſtrength ſhall ſech wher eu er thow may bee founde thow ſhalt haue fote land thyn ne ſhatt deſtruy aft er ward thi bode ſhall doo wyll ¶when lett er red al̄ men herd wer annoied wer ſolempne feſt ̄ ye bretōs wold haue ſlaī meſſang er kīg wold ſuffre ̄ ſaid yt thee meſſangers ſhuld haue harme may bi reſō nōe de ser ue cō māded worſhipfulli ser ued ̄ aft er mete toke cōcell kyngꝭ erles baron anſuer myght yef ayen meſſangers ̄ cōcelled onys ſhuld aſſemble agret pouer landis wich lordſhip māly auēge vpō emprour diſpite ſend ſuch lett er ̄ thei ſwore god ̄ namys ſhuld hī purſue brenne moch myght ſayd • old neu er faill kȳg arthur rather deid let write lett er ſend emprour ſame meſſangers maner ¶off bold anſuere kyng arthur ſent emprour rome roman vnderſtondeth amonges rome yt kyng arthur breton frely holdis ſhall hold att rome haſtile nat yef truage axen truage conſtātine yt eleyns ſon emporour rome honour ther belongeth maximian king cōquered france almayn mount ioye paſſed cōquered lumbardie thes ij wer myne aunceſtres held ſhal̄ haue thurgh goddis ¶of ye reu er ance yt kīg arthr ye emꝓurs meſſang er s· letter made enſeled kyng arthur thes meſſangers yaf gret yeftes meſſangers toke ther leue went then come court rome ayene told emprour wortheli wer vnd er fong alſo ſich rial companie ſerue wos riale ſerued emprour romo ony kyng leuyng world ¶and emprour ou er ſeyne letter herd ther ſaw arthur wold ruled aft er hym let aſſemble ordeyne huge hoſt deſtruy kyng arthur yf myght ¶and kyng arthur touching pouer parti ordeyned pouer knyghtes round table ¶of ye kīgis ̄ lordis yt cō helpe kīg arthr ayēs ye emꝓ • kyng scotland irland gutland denmarke almayne eu er xm men duke normandie gaſcoyn flandres pehito boloyne iiijm gerin charthres xm hoell bretā xijm ̄ hī ſe • f land xijm arbalaſtters archer folke foot man coud • nombre wer redi wend kīg arthur lād gūnore wife toke kepe nephus wyſe knyght hardi wos called mordred trew o ye ſhal̄ heir afterward kyng arthur toke reuame mordred ſaf onli croune▪ ¶and aft er kyng arthur toke hoſt went ſouthamton ther yt ſhippis wer brought folke aſſembled go vn ſee wynd ̄ wedre o ſone myght ariued har • let o ſone myght went lond ther ſhippis ſpred ou er cuntre ¶how kyng arthur fought geant ſpayn wos called dinabus kylled eleyn wos kyng hoels coſyn litell breton kyng arthur duelled cuntre lytell tyme men told ther wos comen gret gegn • ſpayn rauiſſhed fair eleyn coſyn vn hoel̄ lytill bretan brought hir vpon hill called mount ſent barnard ther man ī cuntre ſo bold ne ſo hardy durſt fight ne cum nye place ther geant dulled called dinabꝰ moch ſorow ī cuntre ¶when kyng arthur herd tydyng called key bedewere cūmanded gon preuely eſpy wher geant myght • unden come rinage ther men ſhuld go mount wos encloſed wat er yit eu er ſhal ¶and thei ſaw abrinnyng fire vpon hyll ther alſo hill nygh ther wos vpon fire brennyng ¶key bedewere come next hill • ōden widew openhed ſittīg beſides tombe ſore wepyng ̄ gret ſorow made oft ſhe ſayd eleyn elein key bedewere axed ſhe wherfor ſhe made ſo moch ſorow ſay tombe qd ſhe ſorow myſauentur fair lordes ſeke ye geant may heir fynd ſle anone ¶be ſtyll good wife qd ther diſmay ye tell v ſoth whi thow makeſt ſo moch ſorow wepyng ¶sirs quod ſhe damyſell noriſſhid breſt yt called ellin nece hoell kyng breton heir lieth body tombe wos takn noriſſhe ¶and ſo ther come deuell geant rauiſſhed hir alſo lad v away ¶and wold haue forlayn mayd wos ſo yong tend er age ſhe myght ſuffer ſo gret ſo houge geant ¶and certis cū o wont yow kill therfor wend ye hen beſpake thes two meſſengers ſayed vn hir wherfor go ye hen ¶certis ſyrs quod ſhe elin wos deid geāt made abyde done haunte muſt nedes ſuffer god wote leu er deid deill ſo moch payn ſorow haue forlieth ¶when key bedewer herd woman told turned ayene come kyng arthur told yt ſeyne • arthur anōe toke wt hī wēt preueli nyght yt nōe hoſt wiſt come morow erli geant faught wt hī ſtr • ̄gli thee laſt hī ſlew ¶and arthur bad bedewer ſmyt heed bring ye hoſt ſhew wond er wos ſo gret huge ¶whē thei come ayen ye hoſt told wherfor ̄ ſhewed hem heed ̄ eu er mā glad ioifull ye worthy dede yt kīg arthur done yt wos ther lord ¶and hoell wos ful ſorowful̄ nece yt wos ſo loſt ̄ aft er whē ſpace let make fair chapell ladi ou er elins tombe ¶how kynh arthur yaf bataill emhrour wich bataill emprour ſelf ſlayn arthur pepull tydynges emprour aſſembled gret pouer well ſaraſyns ſo offris died ¶and deth offris tho regned gentill criſtyn man moch loued god almyghty land northhumberland heritage cald oſwald wos kyng land ¶but moch wos frend edwyne held gret part lād cadwalin ſame cadwalyn wered vpon drefe toward ſcotland ¶and cadwalyn ſaw wold abyde cadwalyne nold longer hym purſew toke ſome folke peanda brother law prayed peanda purſew oſwald till wer taken ſlayn cadwalyne turned home ayene ¶when oſwalde herd tyding cadwalin turned home ayene wold longer fle aboid peanda yaf bataill peanda wos diſcomfited fled come ayen cadwalyn ſayed wold neuer hold fote land yf ſo wold venge oſwald ¶cadwalyn let aſſemble gret hoſt fight wt oſwald ſo peanda come northhūberland ̄ yaf bataill vn oſwald ſame bataill oſwald ſlayn heid ſmyten wos entered abbay bardeney ī wich place god hath wrought mony fair miracull ther ̄ el ¶and anone oſwy brother ſeyſed land hond wos thys oſwaldis ̄ folke northūberland loued hī wond er well held ther lord· men kyn worthy ynough wold way goodis empyre ſtons anſuerd ayen ſayed truſt god yt owr chyſtys ſhal neu er lake monay put treſour ī heuen vpon certayn day went palaſſe conſtantinopolī ſe marbyll pament cro grauen thought pater benedicte reliquis virtutum titulus et decꝰ atque dolor pelagius wos emprour benedictus v yere ī tyme rome beſeged lūbardies ̄ litell day mauriciꝰ wos emprour tiberiꝰ xxi yere veray criſtī man ̄ ſubdued parſas ̄ armenia ī lat er end day deſcordyd ſent gregorie ītendid haueſlayn appered aman ī rome clothed ī relegiꝰ habit holding naked ſuord ī hand cried citte· wiſe emprour ſhall deſtruyd wich emprour herred corecked ſelf treſpaſe praid god withdraw ſentens lord apered ī ſlepe ſaid thou ſpair ī tyme cum wos louer wricchis ſayd yef heir rewarde wos empror aft er mony day ſhuld haue corecked knyghtis ther extorcion aſked wold pay ther wage ſo fell veryans choſe foca emprour kylled iij ſonnis ¶this tyme ſen auſtyn come englond ordeyned ij archebiſſhoppis tat ſay london yorke ye cummandement ſent gregorie ¶and remembre mony tymes made mencion diuerſe region cuntres oft tyme haue ben turned faith al way faith bood ī diuerſe cauſes englong fraunce perſia iuri thyng rome wos preuelegit ther thee faith petre neu er failith ¶focas wos ēprour maurici maſter ſlew becauſe began yll endid nought dais roman faught ſtrongly ayeneſt perſes roman wer diſcomfited loſt mony prouynce thee laſt ower commen ſlayn eraclyo o vn men ſo wos done anno domini vclxxxiiij gregori fyrſt roman monke pope pelagius xiij yere man called gregorius magnus mony thinges excedid paſſed mē saninianus pope gregorie yere v monethes man ordant ryngyng bellis houres day bot man bacbote ſent gregorie liberalite poer men thought ſe ſent grogorie rebuke thris fourth tyme lie bed thought ſent dedicatit honour neptimꝰ fals goddis wher criſtyn men mony tymes wer ſlayn deuel̄s myght dedicatit worſhip ſenttis heuen man ordend monkis myght vſe office prechīg criſtinyng confeſſion eraclius wos emprour aft er foca xiij yere thrid yere regne coſdras kīg perſes brent ieruſalem worſhipfull place zachary ye patriarke wt mich pepull toke ī captiuite part holy cro wich elena left ther toke wt hī ī cuntre bot xij yere heraclii coſdras wos ſlayn heraclij cro wos brought ayen pepull wer deliu er id whē heraclius wold haue entred ye cite proudly ye yatis ye cite bi pouer god ſchet ther ſelf yere wich ordand man ſhuld take chirche yerd litell el writtyn nota machomitū machomite duke seraſens turkes wos tyme deſauer world fals prophet meſſanger deuell fore goer antocriſt fulfiller hereſy fals men merueleſt dominacion thus begane ¶ther wos certayn famus clarke rome could ſped mater deſired haue ſped reſedit rome ouer ſee procured mony man go emong fals machemite grete man witt clarke promyſed make hī duke cuntre wold gided ¶ther noriſſhed dowfe put corne dowfe eten machomites eire ſo dowfe neuer mete bot ere ¶the certain clarke day called pepull meuede cheſe ſych prince holy goſt wold ſhew forme dowfe anone clarke ſecretly let fly dowfe wich old cuſtom wos wont fell none ſhulder machomite put byll eere pepull ſee anone wos choſen duke pepull whē wos made duke pepull coroſame ſaid wos weray prophet god thē made boke law wos called alcharon bot informacion iij maiſters deuell myniſterid auctorite cunnyng ¶the fyrſt maſter wos iue gret aſtronomier negremē ser ſecūd wos iohn̄ de anthiochia thrid wos ſergius heritike thes iij made vngraciꝰ law ̄ vn happi ſum euer harde beleue tedyus done thei left law put thīg ī ther law wich wordly men weir ꝓne redy ſay glotonye lecchorye rapyn ſuch alſo machomyte ordend man ſhuld haue mony wyfes myght ocupye fynd refuſe twys thries iiij tymes take ayen mony meruelus fals thynges mode law wich wer long reherſe heir bot playn ī boke alchorō eu er wrotte ī boke lord ſpake machomyte prophet ſayng wiſſe ¶thus fals menys diſſaued pepull maiſters made wos ſo delectabull wrotte boke letter gold alſo noreſſhed myghty camell ſecretly preuey place alonli hondis machomyte wos alway fed ther priuely tyed boke law made camales neke put camell forth tyme feldes fore day camell ioyed liberte wos neuer lowſe fore ¶and wold ſuffre man cum toche ̄ ſo ther wos gret fame ſuch camell pepull ran ſe emonge whome wos machomyte ¶but camell ſe fed way anone ran vn taught camell foro tyme fall doun kneis lykke handis ſo fore tho pepull ¶the pepull cried ſayd ther veray enſample wos trew prophet god prayd machomyte opyn holy boke holy handis wich wos ſend heuen euer kepid wich boke ſhewed peple ſhall woyrſhyp god machomyte ayene chyrch rome wt ye pope gedred ged er ſext gen er sinody ī wich wos graunted preſtes greke vſe ther lefull wynys priſtes eſt cauſe gret heet bot tho thee weſt ꝑti menys amytted chaſtite tyme ſent gregori ¶and eu er mā mei adu er tiſe ̄ pond er moch goodnes prince worth quyete ſtate chyrche promocion fayth alſo cōtrari moch male prince hurtith thīg thes ij conſtātines ye fader ſon ordened pax ſhuld yeuen aft er agnus dei ̄ died bliſſed man benedictus ſecund pope leo almoſt iij yere man al thing wos vertuꝰ nam concordid dedis tyme gret peſtelence iuſtinianus ſecund wos emprour chirche wherfor x yere empire taken leo prince patricio ̄ tybirio cutten noſe tong ̄ exiled criſonā ther wos ther gret turbacion chirche ſtrife heritikes ¶and knaw al men verians fal̄lith twix gret lordis arruris multiplied ther man coreckith therfor oft tyme preued chirche aft er fell verians twix leo tibere tibere preualet exiled leonē ̄ cut noſe thrid yere empire ̄ regned iuſtiniā fled ſaraſens bulgars wich reſtored ayen empire kylled leo tibere wich fauored heritikis thē ſame iuſtynian reformid hī ſelf chirche god haad gret repentans bot venged cruelly adu er ſaries ſo wold haue kylled ther innocent child therfor wos ſlayn ſon philipe exiled anno domini viclxxxiiij iohannes fifthe pope aft er benedictus yere wos good man bot deceſſed anone zeno wos pope wos varay holi man wold medill ſeculer materis bewte āgell quiet vertuus meke ſawle verey demure langage religius liffe man wos choſin laſt one accorde chirche layman bot ther wos gret diſtynccion clargi intendid haue choſen perys archbiſſhopp ̄ hoſt lay men wold haue theodo rum preſt bot laſt holy goſt turned pepull holy maij sergius wos pope ix yere man wos vertuus ̄ comendabull liffe ī eleccion gret diſcorde parti clarge choſe theodo rum ꝑti paſcalem bot o lord wold laſt turned man man tranſlatyt body ſent leo alſo fond grett ꝑte holy cro bi miracull criſtyned cadwalidus laſt kyng bretayn commanded agnus dei ſaid ſōg thris maſſe deceſſed bliſſydly▪ nota sent beda worſſhipfull priſt wos tyme aman gret fame englond wich wos take vij yere age benedict abbot gyrwyenſ monaſteri taught aft er colfrido abbot aft er deth benedict xix yere hys age wos made dekyn thebiſſhop yorke xxx yere wos made preſt wich yere began writtē cō tenuyd tyme lyffe monaſtari geuyng laburs writyng forſcriptur exponed lxxviij bokis made wich nombris end engliſſh boke ¶this man wos eu er labour ī prayer ī ſyngyng daly thee chirche lerne teche writ wich thīg mē may iuge bi reſon wos neu er rome yef ſum men ſay went rome myght ſe bokis accorded doctrine chiyrche bot wos certain wos blynd ̄ wēt preche ser uand yt good made hī prech mighty multitude ſtonnys ſayed thei wer men ſermond wos done ſtonnys anſuerd ſaied amen went rome thries ̄ fond writtī iij arris iij effis exponyt hit wos neuer found ī boke autorite ther wos aft er talkyng pepull ſuch writyng yates rome r r r f f f ſuch expoſiciō rigna rome ruent ferro flama fame certan bede wos deſired cum rome writyng ſergij pope vn colfrid abbot bede tranſlatid ye goſpell ſent iohn̄ engleſh tonge deceſſid blyſſedly fame ſayeth lieth deuelyn ſent cuthberto ther beried knawlege dedis englond almoſt conqueſt leo ſecund emprour litell writtyn liberius emprour vij yere wich roſe ayeneſt leo entrid kyngdom kepid priſon long o regned tyme iuſtinian ſecund wich old tyme exiled creſonam opynly ſayd wold recou er empire ayen wherfor pepull cuntre loue liberius wer kyll iuſtinian wherfor fled prince turco rum weddid ſiſter thurgh help brother bulgares recou er id empire kylled liberiū leonem vſurꝑ reame mony tymes almoſt wyped drope noſe wich cut mony tymes ne made enmys kylled leo thrid wos pope sergius ij yere man wos made pope pouer romās put nombre popis yll entred bot yll iohēs ſex greke wos pope wos martir bot wherfor cauſe found hiſtoriis ſaid wos dukys lumbardy thei wer emnys vn chirche myghtely iohēs vij ronan wos pope iij yere bot nothing writtyn iuſtinianꝰ ſecūd wos emꝑour ayen ſonne tibiri vi yere wos wich wos reued empire fore bi leo man wos reſtored ayen toke right faith worchipped pope conſtantin certanly deſtrued creſon place wher wos exiled duelled except child killed come ayene tyme haue kylled innocentis men cuntre made ther captayn certayn mā wos called philip owtlay wich anone went bataill kyllid hys cruelnes ayenes tho child syſynnius pope xx dais gret ſtrife deceſſid bot lytill writtyn conſtantin pope aft er vij yere man verey meke man ſo bliſſid men wos loued went ower ſee iuſtimian emprour ̄ wos reſaued gret honour died bliſſed maij philippe ſecund wos emꝑour yere wich fled ī sciſilya hoſt roman wos heritike cōmanded picturs ſenctis diſtruid wherfor roman keſt way coyn ne wold reſaue monay ymage name writtyn vpon anaſtaſius ſecund kylled philipp emprour iij yere man wos criſtin man leued well bot cauſe put philippi eyn ̄ kylled aft er ward therfor theodoſius faught ayens hym ower come hī ̄ thē wos made preſt leued ſo quyetly anno domini vijcxiiij gregorius ſecund wos pope aft er conſtantyn xvijyere gregorii wos chaſte man nobull man ſcripture tyme popis began deell tēꝑally emprours wer wont ther falſeneſſe ̄ therherici alſo remeue empire fro oo pepull tyme requerid man curſed leo emprour cauſe brent ymages ſentys ſame leo commandid gregori pope ſhuld brine chirches deſtruy ſet nothing ſayng bot commanded contrari manly ſo opynli ſhewed deſtruccion empire roome wos cauſe heriſe certanly faithfull peple ther prelatis wyll drew pope conſtranit emprours leffe ther tyrannyde therheriſe ¶and tyme eſt parte world ſtrongly failed veray faith curſed law fals machomyte theodoſius emprour regned bot yere veray criſtyn man euyn o ſo done vn leo depoſit made preſt leo thrid conſtantin ſon wos emprour xxv yer leo wos myghty depoſit theodoſiū regned wos deſaued bi certayn apoſtata wich bad ſh̄uld take brene ymages ſentys wher fore wos ponyſſhed bothe bataill peſtylence infortunes becauſe wos curſed gregori bode ther iij day therfore pope comyn pepull toke fro weſt parte empire commandyng man ſhuld obay ne ſocour cauſe leued like aritike· ¶holy men ſayd ayeneſt mony bi wos martired exiled laſt myſbeleue died writchedly ¶and man dais bot karolus marcellus holp criſtyn faith faught manly ayen ſareſens drofe bacward ī ſpayn wich ſubduid el entred ī fraunce ¶and karolus ſlew iijcm ſaraſons mo pepull wer ſlayn bot xvm nō man continuall bataill toke lay men treſour chirche whe • ſent euchery biſihop aurilian wos hys prayer ſaw ſame karolum ſaule bodi payned hell angell ſhewed biſſhop man ſayd wos iugement tho toke away goodis thee chirche poer men fortefi biſſhop ſayed preue abbot ſent dionis went ſepulc • ther karolus wos beried opyned chiſt lay ī ther ſe dragon go bot bodi gregory thrid roman pope gregori ſecū de wich conformed worſhippyng ymages ſentis cunſell almoſt biſſhoppis curſed horibly diſpyſers thes ymages emprour wer condicion conſtantinus fifthe wos emprour fader leo xxxv yere curſed man pure heritike ſo ſacrifice deuels purſuid chirche nothyng good writen ſo ſufferans god chirche wos trubelled long tyme ¶about tym wer mony merueles ther wer meruelus erth quakis certaij cite wer ſet mountens wer remeued ̄ borne way hilles feldis ſex myle then ſtod cite wer broken ne hurt land meſopotanyan erth wos brokyn bi ſpace ij myle alſo ther wos mule ſpake ī mannys voce aſh fell heuyn ſee pontico ther wos yſſe gret froſt xxx cubittis thykneſſe ſters fell heuyn ſo myghtely men trowed end world bene comen thes prophetabull vn chirch well word o doctrine gouerned ſpiritualte temparalty nobully wos louer defender poer men man anoynted pippinū kyng fraunce ſend ayenes lūbardis ſhuld compell reſtore chirche paule conſtantine roman ſecund wos pope aft er paule ij yere conſtantine wos lay man ſodenli made preſt o tyrant toke dignite pope gret ſclander chirche pope litell tyme bot faithfull men put put eeyn wos fyfth infamyd pope emong ſo mony hed er ſo holy goſt yt holy apoſtyls ſeet kepid honour holines ¶infenit martirs wer made tyme conſtātin emprour ſuch heritike men trowe ther wos neu er emꝑour ne pagon kylled ſo mony marters tyme chirche wos trubled ſore verey preciuſly bought worſhipyng ymages ſentys gret ſheding blod martyr certanly curſed emprour vn ponyſſhed died cried horabull voiſe ſaid labur mony rebellyng ¶this tyme karolus magnus wos nobull yong man began regne vpon fraunce ſon pippini mother wos called berta stephenus thrid pope iij yere mendid errurs conſtaotine degrated tho ye wich conſtantine ordand gouernall ſynody anno domini vijc lxxxiiij adrianus roman wos pope stephyn xxiiij yere man wos myghtely worſſhippid pepull man grettyr fore honour rich byldyng man ſet ij ſolom ſynodis friſt iijc l fadyrs ſecund rome cl fadyrs beyng preſent charles kyng fraunce granted leberte eleccion pope ordane apoſtils ſeet leo fourth regned emprour grekis v yere leo curſed man bot ſo moch o fader wos couetus man toke away certan croune chirche put vpon hede anone corruppid wyth axis ſo diceſſid curſed wiffe wich regned hir ſon conſtantine wos emprour leo wos meke mā put away mother fro kyngdom ſhe might take heed vn hir woman warke botſhe fenyt rankyr put eeyn afterward hys childireyn alſo regned ayens iij yere laſt ſhe wos haue weddid ̄ whē grekis ꝑſauyd ſhe wold weddid gret karolus thei toke hir ſhethir vp monaſtari toke nichofe rum ther emprour ¶the v vniuſall ſtudy wich old tyme tranſlait athyns vn rome bout thys tyme tranlatyd vn paris bi karolus kyng fraunce nichoferus wos emprour conſtantine wos vere nygoij ̄ exaltid empire grekis bot ꝓfettit tyme eſt impariall wos brought nought roman put vnder karolus magnus ¶ieruſalem bout tyme wos recouerid karolum holy land ſeckit ſariſens wos diſtruied ſtrongly deſtruccion wricchis come michaell wos emprour ij yere verey criſtī mā wos well beloued alſo wos cunnyng ſcience ̄ tho nichoferus hurt deſtreſſid ther goodis bi couetuſnes michaell reſtorid made riche ayene nota karolus magnus friſt ſant wos emprour aft er michaell wos crouned emprour leo pope wich tyme empire wos tranſlatyt fro grekis fraūce germane tranſlacion empire grekys way wer defectieu vn roman grekys ſtrofe eu er bot wos wt venūys wordis thē ſtrength craft bataill thei ſo gret enuy roman nold obey chirche rome certanly popis wold writt vn obey chirche rome wrot ayene ſaid ye haue take kynrad empire thorfor yow obey v take nobull emprour karolous vnd er ſtond man wos yong man wos noynted kyng fraunce stephyn po pe yere deceſſid bliſſed man stephanus fourth wos pope aft er leo iij yere stephanus redemid mony captiue men crouned lodewik emꝑor deceſſid beried rome paſchall wos pope aft er stephyn paſchall yaf gret dylygens relickis ſentis toke vp innumerabull bodis ſentis beried worſhipfully viſion ſent cicill wos commanded eugenius fourth wos pope paſchall verey holy man tho thinges werfor criſt toke heid man wos crounyd marter lay men rome wos beried ſent petre chirche yerde circa annū domini viijcxliiij valintinus wos pope eugeni xl dais litel writtyn gregori fourth wos pope xij yere gregori ſaw mony
