fontanelū wher lotheri wos diſcomfited ther ſuch ſlaughter made ſydis men reſiſt ther adu er ſaries vndirſtode fals criſtyn man ſent vn ſowden ſariſeus ſhuld cum anone toke rome ſent petre chirche wos made ſtabull ther horſes bot lodewik frennſhemen lumbardies infenite multitude diſtruyd greet ſheddyng criſtyn blod sergius ſecund wos pope gregorius ij yere thys man wos called fyrſt o porci engliſh hogyſmothe wherfor man ̄ popis namys archanged bene choſyn iij cauſis friſt criſt changed thee name tho mē ye wich made popis ye ſecūd o moch thei archāged ī name ſo ſhuld thei chāged īꝑfecciō life ye iij leſt ye wich choſī excedīg degre ſhuld hurte name leo wos pope aft er sergius viij yere leo wos holy man alſo prudens ſharpe ſerpent dedis meke dowfe wos broughte forth vertuuſly monaſteri made pope labored repayne chirches agayn wych falſe ſaraſons deſtruyed man wos myghty writer gret precher myghtely labored watche prayer ſo died wos beried lie ſent petris benedictus roman wos pope leo ij yere benedicte name thyng thyng wos bliſſed mā ordand clarkys ſhuld go ordynately honeſtly lodowicus ſon lotharij wos emprour tyme noynted sergio pope regned fadre regned xxi yere allone man ſon heght karolus deuell entred vexed afore fader conſpirid fadres deth tyme mony meruell fell▪ nota iohannes anglicus nacion magnutynne tyme wos pope ſhe wos woman arayed mannys garmentys bot ſhe profetid ſo ī holy ſcripture ther wos fonden none lyke hir ¶then ſhe choſen pope bot afterward ſhe wos child ſhe ſhuld haue gone opynly proceſſion ſhe traueled deceſſid ¶and ſext pope tyme nam holyneſſe wer vecius parſon curſed popis wer wos punyſſhed god ner ſhe wos nombred thee boke popis nicholaus roman wos pope aft er womā ix yere nicholas wos gret holynes yt ther wos mā cōꝑabull hī aft er gret gregori pope whē wos made pope lodewik emꝑour wos preſēt deceſſid verey good man wos beried ī ſent petyrchirche yerde adriā roman wos pope aft er pope nicholas adrian curſed lothariū brother emprour kyng lotharyng adultery· bot come rome excuſe adult er ſayd curſed wronguſly brought wt hī ye nobul mē regiō wer deid wt ī yere kīg died way come cite placenciam anno domini viijclxxiij ¶of kyng alured danois tyme prayd merci myght gone land aluredus thys tyme come danys englond deth eldred regned brother alured dolfynes cald ¶tho went danois ̄ aſſē led went forth ſoche alured tho wos king new made ſouthſex ther fonden wilton litel pepull neu er laſſe faught wt laſt fled then feld went weſtſex ordeyned ſo moch pepull reame alſo ſo tyll departed froo london ſo faſt riden bothe nyght day neu er toke reſt goyng till thei come vn exceſtre token tho toune ther held ¶when kyng alured herd tydyng anone let take hoſtages went then vn exceſtre pouer ¶and danois herd tell cummyng went then vn weſ • ſex come chippenham ther moch harme cuntre robbid folke brought priſon ¶the king alured purſued come vpon ferſly aſſailed ther wer ſlayn bothe hubba hunger brother buerne bocard bataill wos moch folke ſlayn ꝑte ī gree feld left danois moch o kyng come litell companye ¶the kynge haſted moch o myght wend ayene ̄ ye danois fonden hubbais body liyeng deid entered made vpon hit gret logge let call hubeſlow ſo cald vn thiys day place deuenſhire ¶the baroens ſomerſet wilteſhire dorſet herd tell ther king wos deſcomfited ordeined pouer wold yt king alured victorie moch honour danois wer ſo driuen yt ne wiſten whid er turne xv day king purſued wyll glad fayn wer ſpeke pee acord ̄ toke good hoſtage· ſayd nold neuer vpon ne debate day cum ayene wos ſet ̄ ſo wenten forth faſt come ayene ther day wos aſſined danoys brought ther kyng wt ¶the kyng alured anon let baptiſed ther name changid ſo kyng danmarke wos called athelſton xxx felawes name wer changed alſo wer baptiſed right beleue ¶and wos done weſtmynſter kyng alured held kyng athelſton danoys xij day ſoiourne moch ſolempnite yaf gret yeftes aft er yt wer baptiſed ̄ ſo deꝑtid tho wos kyng alured eſe emnys ou er cummyn wer turned right beleue almyghty god ¶how danoys come fraunce gurmond come ayen engloyd deth kyng alured thus befell aft er ward danois northhū berland wer paynyms come gret ſtrength huge hoſt fraunce vnderſtonde yt went fraunce gurmond aufrike cō quered englond yaf vn saxon tho thatt come fraunce ariued kent ̄ ſent northhumbirland ſhuld cum tho ij hoſtis wer comen aſſembled anone went diſtruy ye criſtī pepull englond place place moch ſorow ¶hit befell thꝰ o almyghty god wold hard chance ī englond good kīg alured wos wont abate danois karolꝰ kīg fraunce ¶this tyme empire remeued tranſlatyt deuyded frenſhmen holp chirche wich ther faders hedified fortefied bot diſtruyd ne help roman ayens lombardis wich vexed roman right ſore therfor comyns aſſent wer excludid empire ̄ ye italian gan emprours ī itali almans almany vn till ottanem wich regned place frenſhmen wer conſtrenyd abide ī ther cuntre emprours ther miſcheuus bothe frō land aft er wēt ̄ toke gret prey cumberland edmond regned vij yere lieth glaſtenburi ¶of kyng eldred edmond regned eldred brother avenged edward fader emnys kyll afterward ſeyſed ¶and kyng eldree nobull man good who goodneſſe ſent dū ſtane preched kīg eldred regned xi yere lieth wīcheſt ¶of kyng edwyne eldred regnd edwyne ſon edmond lither man toward god pepull hated folke • called knyghtes moch loued ̄ truſtyd vpon ̄ told go quod nobull baron orgar deuēſhire ſe dought er ſo farr men ſpekith ſoth wyll haue hir vn wife ¶this knyght called edelwold went forth way kyng ſayd come ther lady wos ſaw hir ſo fair thought haue hir hīſelf wife therof ſpakē orgar hir fad er ̄ hir fadre wos old man mo childre hir ſaw edel wold wos fair yong knyght worthi riche wos well beloued kyng thought doughter ſhuld well maried beſet vpon granted hī doughter good lord kyng wold conſent ther ¶then thys edelwold come ayene kyng told ſhe wos fair ynough vpon ſee ſhe wos wond er lothly tho anſuerd thee kīg ſaid toke bot litell charge sir qd edelwold tho ſhe hir fadres heir riche landis ye wold cō ſent grant myght hir haue ſhuld rich ynowghe goodis name qd kyng conſent ther ¶and tho went kyng henri ayen ī englond ̄ maried maude dought er henri emprour almayne ¶of debate yt wos betwē kīg lowis france ̄ kīg hēri ēglōd ̄ kīg henris ij ſonnys wer loſt ī high ſee ī moder chirche ¶and ī yere ye incarnacion ihū criſt mclxxij yere ¶and anone henri new kyng began make vpon henri fadre vpon brether willm thus ¶and ſo vpon day kyng fraunce kynges ſonnes kyng aft er died xxxvi yere regne lieth redīg ¶how criſtyn loſt holy land forſaid kynges tyme thurgh fals criſtyn man bicome ſariſen kīg henri empriſe ſon leued regned gret bataill wos holy land bitwen criſtyn mē ſariſens criſtyn men wer ther kylled thurgh grett treſon erle tirpe wold haue wife quene ieruſalem ſom tyme wos baldewyns wife ſhe forſoke toke hir lord knyght worthi man wos called ſir gnyꝑches wherfor erle tirpe wos wroth wēt anone right soladyne ſoudeyn babilon ̄ bicome man forſoke criſtindom ̄ criſtyn law criſtī men wiſt dedis wened haue gret help wer wont haue ¶and comen bataill fals criſtyn man turned vn ſariſens forſoke nacions ̄ ſo wer criſtyn men ther kylled wt ſariſens ¶and thus wer criſtyn men ſlayn put horibull deth ̄ cite ieruſalē deſtruied holy cro borne away ¶the kyng fraunce gret lordis ye land let cro go vn loly land ¶and amōg went richard kyng henri ſon friſt aft er ye kīg fraūce yt toke ye cro ye erchebiſſhop tour toke viage yt tyme encheſon yt wos let bi man er weys nedis done ¶and whā kīg henri fad er regned xxxvi yere v monethis iiij dais died lieth foundenerard anno domini mclvi adrianus fourth wos pope aft er anaſtaſy v yere pope engliſſhman ye voce comyn pepule ſaeth wos bondman ye abbot ſent albons ī englōd whē deſired made mōke ther wos expulſid hee wēt ou er ſee gaf hī ſtudy ̄ vertu aft er wos made biſſhop albanacens alexandre thrid wos pope xij yere alexander ſtrife xvij yere iiij ſtriuers emprour ſet ayens ou er come curſid ̄ dred yll deth ¶this man alſo accordid frederic emprour emanuell conſtātiōble· kyng brother wered vpon englond ¶but biſſhoppes baron englond withſtod pouer thatt might get toke caſtell wyndoſore caſtelles ¶and forſaied iohn̄ ſaw might ne pouer ayenis baron englond fight anone went ouer ſee vn kyng fraunce ¶and whē kyng richard come priſon wos deliu er ed come englond anone aft er candilmaſſe gret haſt went vn notyngham caſtell notyngham wos yolden tho diſcōfitid brother iohan tho held ¶and aft er hee went vn cite wyncheſtre ther let croun kyng englond ̄ went vnto normandie vpon kyng fraunce ¶and kyng fraunce come withe vc knyghtys toward giſors kyng richard met tho wold caſtyli arbalaſtier ſmote quarell wos enuenyned ̄ kyng drofe ſhaft quarell quarell heed abood ſtill heed began rankill yt might help ſelf ne meue armes ¶and tho wiſt dethes woūde vpō yt might hole man er thing commaūded annone ſharpili men aſſaill caſtell yt caſtell take died ſo manli men ye pepull wer ī ye caſtill wer takē kyng wold ̄ cōmandid men ſhuld brīg ye man ſo hurt ſo woūdid ¶and wen come ye kyng kīg axed hī name ̄ ſaid mi name bartram gurdon wherfor ſaid kīg haſt tow ſlayn· ſith neuer none harme ¶sir ſaid though ye neu er none harme ye yourſelf hond killed fadre brother therfor haue quyte trauell ¶tho ſaid kīg richard died vpon cro bring man ſoule pyne hell yef deth alſo yef ¶tho cōmandid man ſhuld miſdo ¶but ye kynges defēdīg ſom men folowed ̄ p̄ueli kylled ̄ vi erles ̄ baron held ther gret ꝑlamēt ̄ axed ther ye clerge tenth eu er chirche englond cōquere ̄ get ayen normandie angeon loſt wold graūt yt thīg wherfore wonder wroth ¶and yt ſame tyme died hubert prior couēt cantorburi choſen ayens kīgꝭ erchebirſpop maſtyr stephen langton good clerk yt woned court rome ſend pope ther eleccion ̄ pope ꝯfirmid ſacrid viterbi ¶when kīg wiſt tyding wos wond er wroth drofe prior couēt fro cantorbury exiled englond cōmandid yt man er letter yt come frō rome ne cōmandement ſhuld vnd er fenge ne pleted englond ¶when tydīg come pope ſent kīg iohan letter prayed hī wt good good hert yt wold vnd er fenhe stephen erchebiſſh̄op cantorburi chirche ſuffer prior ̄ monkis cū ayen ther duellīg bot ye kyng wold graūte thing ¶how kyng iohn̄ wold nothīg done popis cōmandement wherfor englōd enterdited ſuſpended laſt pope ſent auctorite enioyned biſſhoppis englomd kyng wold vndirfenge prior cantorburi monkis ſhuld done generall interdityng thurgh englone graunted full pouer iiij biſſhoppis pronounce interditing werned ¶the friſt biſſhop willm lōdon biſſhop euſtace ely ̄ iij biſſhop walter wī cheſtre iiij biſſhop giles herford ¶and thes iiij biſſhoppis praied kyng kneling ther kneys ̄ ſore weppīg yt wold popis commandemēt ſhewed popis bulles enterditīg bot prayer myght pray wold conſent ther ¶and whē biſſhoppis ſaw wēt kīg ye morne aft er anūciaon lady pronouced gen er enterditīg thurgh englond ſo chirche doris wer ſhit keis faſtynyng walles ¶and enterditing pronoūced kyng gane wax meſure ̄ anone hand poſſeſſions iiij biſſhoppis clarge thurgh ye land toke ̄ ordened men kepe yt clarkis myght haue ther leuīg wherfore biſſhoppis curſed put ſhuld medle holy chirche goodis ayens owed ¶and kīg wold malace ſees man er thing thes iiij biſſhoppis fore ſaid went ou er ſee come biſſhop cātorburi ̄ told thyng ¶and erchebiſſh̄op ſaid ſhuld gone ayen cā torburi ſhuld cum thider el wold ſend vn certan ꝑſons ſtede ſhuld moch ſelf wer ther ¶and whē biſſhoppis herd turned ayen englōd ̄ come vn cātorburi ¶the tydīg comen ye kīg yt biſſhoppis wer come ayen cantorburi ſelfe might cū theder tyme ſend thider biſſh̄oppis erles ̄ abbotis trete kyng ſh̄uld vnd er fenge erchebiſſh̄op ſtephen ye prior ̄ ye mōkis cantorburi ſhuld neu er tyme thīg take holi chirche ayens awed goodis kyng ſhuld make full amendis goodis taken holy chirche ſhuld haue fraunchis ferforth ſent edwardis tyme confeſſour ¶how stephen langton com englond thurgh popis cōmandemnt went ayen forme accordement thus wos ordened hit apayr endenturs thei put ther ſeales one part comen kynges name put ther ſeales parte endentures iiij biſſhoppis aboue ſaid toke part endenturs yt part endenturs bore ſhew kyng ¶when kyng ſaw forme ̄ vnder ſtode held full well apayed man er thyng ordeyned ſauyng techīg reſtitucion goodis make ayen yt thyng wold accorde ſo ſend word ayen iiij biſſhoppis ſhuld put way poynt reſtitucion ¶but anſuerd thei wold done word tho ſent kyng erchebiſſhop tho iiij erchebiſſhoppis ſhuld cū cātorburi ſpeke ther ſent vn ſaufcondit vnd er plegges ſay iuſtices gilbert peitevyn willm de la brener iohn fitz hugh ther conduit ſaufely ſhuld come ̄ go ayen att ī man er erchebiſſhop stephen come cantorburi ¶and erchebiſſhop comē kīg come chilham wold ney cantorburi yt time ſent bi treſorour biſſhop wyncheſtre yt ſhuld done endenturs clauſe reſtitucion moke goody ¶and erchebiſſhop made oth nold neu er word therof ne yit change biſſhoppis ſpoken ordeyned tho erchebiſſhopp wēt ayen rome wt doyng ¶kīg iohn̄ tho wrother eu er wos let make comyn cry thurgh englond tho holy chirche rentis went ouer ſee thei ſhuld cum ayen englond certan day el ſhuld leſe ther rentis eu er ̄ cōmandid euery ſhereue thurgh englond ſhuld enquere biſſhop abbot prior ony prelat holy chirche fro day aft er ward reſaued cōmaundemēt comen fro pope thei ſhuld take bodi brīg hī yt ſhold take kynges hondis ther landis holy chirche wer yefen ony man bi erchebiſſhop stephen bi prior cantorbury tyme eleccion erchebiſſhop commandid woddes wer erchebiſſhoppis ſh̄uld caſtyn doune vn gronde ̄ ſolde ¶how kyng iohn̄ deſtruyed ordir ciſteaux ī ſame tyme ye iriſhmē began vpon kīg iohn̄ kyng iohn̄ ordeyned hym wend irland let arere huge taxe thurgh englond ſay xxxvm marke thus ſent thurgh englond vn monkis ordir ciſteaux ſhuld help vim marke ſilu er ¶and anſuerd ſaid yt thei durſt nothīg done wt ther chief abbot ciſteaux wherfor kyng iohn̄ come ayen irland ſo moch ſorow care wiſt werfor abide toke ſo moch ranſom eu er houſe ſomme ammounted ixmccc marke clene loſt ̄ deſtruid voided ther houſes ther landis thurgh ēglond ̄ ye abbot wau er ſay dred ſo moch manace ſoke al ye abbey wēt thēs ̄ priuoly ordeyned hī ou er ſee hous ciſteaux tidīg come pope yt kīg ſo moch malice tho toward kīg full wroth ̄ ſent ij legate vn kyng wos called pandolf ̄ yt durāt ſhold warne ye kīg ī popis name yt ſhuld ceſe ꝑſecuciō yt vn holy chirche amend wrong treſpaſe done erchebiſſhop cantorburi priour vn monk cantorburi clarge englond ſhuld reſtore goodis ayen teken ayens ther el ſhuld curſe bi name thing conferme pope toke letter bullis patentz ¶thes ij legatis come englond come kyng northamton ther held parlament full courtaſly ſalued ſaied sir comen fro pope rome pee holy chirche land mend ¶and amoneſt friſt popis halfe ye make full reſtitucion goodis ye haue raueſhed take holy chirche land ye vndirfenge stephen erchebiſſhop cantorburi dignite prior cantorburi monkis ye yeld ayen vn erchebiſſhop landis rentis wt wtholdyng ¶and ſir yit ouer ye ſhall make reſtitucion vn holy chirche wherof ſhall hold well apayed ¶tho anſuerd kyng tochyng priour monkis cantorburi ye haue ſaid done gladly thyng yt ye ordeyn ¶but o tochyng erchebiſſhop ſhull tell myn hert lieth erchebiſſhop let biſſhopprich pope wold pray vpō venture ſhold like ſome biſſhopprich yef englond ̄ vpon condicion wold reſaue vnderfenge ¶and notheles englond erchebiſſhop yef abyde ſhall neuer haue ſo good ſaufcondit ſhall take ¶tho ſaid pandolfe vn kyng ſir holy chirche wos woned neu er diſcharge erchebiſſhop cauſe reſonable euer hath woned chaſtyſe prince god holy chirche wer inobidient ¶what quod kyng manace ye ¶nay ſaid pandolf ye opēle haue told ſtandeth hert ¶and yow telle popis thus ſtandith holy enter dited curſed wronges ye haue done holy chyrche clarge ¶and moche ye duell beth bide malace wricchednes ̄ woll cum ther ne amēdment ye ſhall vnderſtand tyme aft er ward ſentance vpon yeffen holdeth ſtede ſtrength vpon tho haue communed tym whethir erles baron knyghtys ſo eu er aſſoyle ſaufly vn day fro tyme afterward condicion ſom eu er curſe comyn ony word ſentanſe vpon thē openly ſpecially ¶and aſſoill clene erles baron knyghtes men ther homage ſeruis ̄ feautes ſhuld vn done tydyng confirme yef playn pouer byſſhop wyncheſtre ̄ biſthop norwiche ¶and ſame pouer yif ſcotland biſſhoppis rocheſtre saliſburi ¶and wale yeue ſame pouer biſſhoppis ſent dauid ̄ landaf ̄ ſent aſſe· ¶and ou er ſend thurgh criſtī dom biſſhoppis yond ſee done curſſe tho yt helpeth ony cōcell yefeth ony man er nede yt ye haue ꝑte world ¶and aſſoyell alſo actorite pope cōmand alſo wt feght hī emny holy chirche ¶tho anſuerd kyng may ye ¶tho anſuerd pandolf ſayn word god ye ne none heir yt ye haue neu er aft er day may crouned ¶tho ſaid ye kīg bi yt almighti god wiſt yt ye come ī land yt ye brought ſich tyding ſh̄uld haue made ride yere ¶tho anſuerd pādolf full well wēd oure friſt cōmīg yt ye wold haue obedient god ̄ holi chirch haue fulfillid popis commandemēt haue ſhewed vn ̄ ꝓnouncid popis wer charged ther ye haue ſaid ye wiſt cauſe comyng yt ye wold haue made v ride hole yere well ye myght haue ſaid ye wold haue takin hole yere reſpit bi ye popis leue ¶but ſuffre deth ye coude ordeyn ſhall ſpare tell holi popis meſſage wyll yt wer charged ¶how pandolf deliu er ed clarke falſed ̄ cont er feted kynges monay kyng ſelf anone tho commandid kyng ſhereues bailies northamton kynges preſence ſhuld bring forth priſoners myght bene done deth pandolf encheſon kyng wened wold haue gayn ſayed ther dedis cauſe deth thing ſpokin afore ¶when priſoners wer com fore kīg kyng commandid ſom hanged ̄ ſum drawen ſum draw ther eyn ther hede ¶and among ther clarke falſid kyngis monay king commandid ſhuld honged ̄ draw▪ ¶and whē pandolf herd cōmandemēt kīg ſtert vp ſmartely anone axed boke candill ̄ wold haue curſid ̄ ſet vpō ye clarke hand pandolf hī ſelf went ſech cro kīg folowid hī deliu er id hī clarke bi hand yt ſhuld wt hī wolde ¶and thꝰ clerke delyu er id ̄ wēt thēs ¶and pandolf durant felow went kyng iohn̄ come ayen pope rome told kyng iohn̄ wold amended eu er abiden ſo accurſed ¶and notheles pope grantid yere thurgh englond mē myght ſing maſſes coueneble chirchis make goddis body yef ſeke mē ſhuld paſſe world alſo men myght criſtyn child ou er al land ¶and pope wiſt ſaw kyng wold ben vnd er rule holy chirche man er thīg pope tho ſent kyng fraunce remiſion ſinnes yt ſhuld take pouer yt myght ̄ wend ī englond diſtru kyng iohn̄ ¶when tidyng come kyng iohn̄ tho wos ſore anoyed ſore drad leſt ſhuld leſe reame hym ſelf done deth ¶tho ſent pope meſſangers ſaid yt wold bene iuſtyfied cum mendment ī thinges wold make ſatiſfaccion man er men ye popis ordinā ce ¶tho ſent pope ayen engloted pandolf meſſingers come cantorburi tho king abode ye xiij day may kyng made othe ſtand popis ordinance pandolf legate ī man er thīges wich wos curſed ̄ yt ſhuld make full reſtitucion men holi chirche ̄ relegion godis yt taken ayens ther gret lordis englōd ſwore vpon boke ̄ bi ye holydom kīg wold hold oth ſaied wold make hold ſtrength ¶tho put kyng court rome pope tho yaf vp reame englōd irland heires eu er ſh̄uld cum kyng iohn̄ heires ſhuld take tho ij reames pope handis ̄ ſhuld eu er yere pay ferme vn court rome thouſand marke ſilu er ¶and criſt alſo may nothing ſo worthy offer compitent ſatiſfaccion mak god holy chirche wer bodi wt reames englond irland ¶than bi grace god deſire meke v loue meked deth vpon cro thurgh coūſell nobull without yē ſayng pope ̄ eke ward churche vacauntz token thīg eu er laſt confirme ̄ orden yt ſpecial rentis forſaid reame ſauīg ſent petres pen ī thīg mod er chirche rome payng yere mark ſilu er trewli ī man er pointis ayens man er mē pouer thurgh godis helpe ¶how clerkis yt wer outlawed englond come ayenꝭ kyng iohan aſſoiled chartre made enſeled kyng vnderfēg ayen croune pandolfes hand gregori gedirth ged er kynd pepull ther decreid ꝑſons vekerys ſhuld called preſtis ̄ p̄latis man ſh̄uld aſſygne tythis chirche wold o thei fore ſh̄uld paid modir chirche ̄ dampned pluralite beneficis deceſed bliſſid man innocent v wos aft er v monethis litell adrian moneth ̄ la iohannes xxi wos viij monethis ̄ diuſe ſciens famus man bot man er fooill deceſſid anone nicholas thrid wos pope aft er vertuꝰ werkis man curſid emꝑour ꝯſtantinopolon ī ſo moch ꝓmyſed turne fayth ī gen er counſell ̄ wich ſuffrid mich paſſions holy chirche alſo hee curſid kīg aragon expulſed kīg cicill fro kyngdō ꝓfetid ī ordir frere mynors wrot ouer bybell el wos ī yere lord thouſand ccc ̄ xxx ſū men ſays wos brabon yt fad er mod er wer criſtyn pouerty viſet ſcoles iues ſo lerned iues langage el nocholas wos īformid iues ī yong age honoriꝰ fourth wos pope aft er martin ij yere litell writtyn bot tē ꝑate man diſcret nicholaus fourth pope hym iiij yere man wos frere mynor though wos good man ſelf yit mony vnhappy thynges fell tyme chirche mony bataill wos ī cite thurgh occaſion drew tomoch ꝑte ther pope ij yere ſex monethis ¶of kyng edward wos kyng henris ſon kyng henri regned edward ſon worthieſt knyght world honour goddis grace victorie enmys ¶and ſone fadre wos dede come london fair companye prelatis erles baron maner mē moch honour eu er place ſir edward rode london ſtretis wer ¶and wos ſet vn mete kīg alexander ſcotland come done honour reuerence quentize hondreth knyghtis well horſed arayed wer lighted doune ther ſtedis let gone widder wold ̄ myght take toke ther chalenge ¶and afterward come ſir edmond kynd edwardes brother curtas knyght gentill renoune erle cornewaill erle glouceſtre aft er cōe erle penbroke ̄ erle garenne ¶and ech thē ther ſelf lad ther hand hondreth knyghtis gayl • diſgiſed ther armes ¶and wer light ther hors let go whider wold myght cache haue ſtill ony chalenge ¶and thys wos done kyng edward diligence might mende ̄ redreſſe wronges beſt maner myght honour god holy chirche maynten honour mēd noyance comyn pepull ¶how ydeyne yt wos lewelyns dought er wale p̄nce aymer yt wos ye erles brod er moūford wer takē ī ſee friſt yere afterward kyng edward crouned lewelin prince wale ſent fraunce erle moū fort thurgh counſell frendis erle ſhuld wedde dought er erle tho viſed vpon thyng ſent vn lewelyne ſaid wold ſend aft er doughter ¶and ſo ſent aymer brother aft er damiſell lewelyn arayed ſhippis doughter ſir aymer hir fair companye ſhuld gone hir ¶and lewelyn gret wrong couenand ſhuld yef doughter maner man councell conſent kīg edward ¶and ſo befell burgies briſtow come ſee wyne laden met toke might pouer ̄ anōe burgeis ſent kyng ¶and lewelyn herd tydyng wond er wroth ̄ alſo ſorowfull gan vpō kyng edward ̄ moch harme vn engliſſhmen bet doūe kynges caſtelles began faſt diſtroy kīg edwardis landys ¶and whē tiding come vn kyng edward thing went wale ſo moch thurgh goddis grace gret pouer drofe lewelyn vn moch miſcheif fled man er ſtrength ̄ come yeld vn kīg edward yaf lm marke ſilu er haue pee ̄ toke damiſell ̄ heritage ̄ made obligacion kyng edward cum parlament ij tymes yere ¶and ſecund yere kyng edward wos crouned held generall parlamēt weſtmynſtre ̄ ther made ſtatutis defaute law ye ꝯmune aſſent baronage eſtre next ſewyng kyng ſent hys letter vn lewelyn prince wale ſhuld cum hys parlament land holding wale ſtrength letter obligatorye witneſſid ¶tho lewelin ſcorne ̄ diſpite kynges commaundement poer wrath ayen began vpō kyng edward diſtroyed landis ¶and tho kyng edward herd tidynges waxed wond er wroth vn lewelin haſt aſſembled pepull went toward wale werid ſo vpon lewelin prince till brought mych ſorow diſeſe ¶and lewelyn ſaw defence might vaill come ayen yelde kynges grace· cried merci long tyme knelid kynges fote ¶the king pitte cōmandid ariſe mekeneſſe yaf hym wroth ſaid treſpaſſid ayen tyme wold diſtroy eu er ¶dauid wos lewelins brother ſame tyme duellid kyng edward fell man ſotill ̄ enuyous alſo farre caſtyng moch treſon thought ̄ eu er held ſtill wit aſpi kīges ̄ eu er made good ſembland ſemid ſo trew yt man might ꝑſaue falſeneſſe ¶how lewelin thurgh eggyng dauid brother werid ayen vpō kyng edward wos long aft er time kyng edward yef dauid lewelins brother lordſhip frodeſhā made knyght ſo moch honour neu er aft er man wale encheſon hī ¶kyng edward held ꝑlament londō done wale wold chā gid monay tho wos fouyll cut roundid wherfore romyn pepull plenyd wond er ſore kyng let enquere ſuch treſpoces ¶and ccc wer atteynt • ſuch mon er falſenes wherfore ſom wer honged ̄ ſom drawe aft er ward honged ¶and afterward kyng ordeyned ye ſterling half penne ferthyng ſhuld gone thurgh lād commanded man fro day afteerward yaf ne ſeffed hous religion land tenement ſpeciall leue kīg ſhuld ponyſſhed kynges ̄ yift ſhuld nought ¶and wos long lewelin prince wale thurgh ticement dauid brod er ther conſent thought diſherite kyng edward ī moch myght ſo thurgh kingꝭ pee wos broken ¶and whē kyng edward herd anone ſent baron northūberland furreis alſo ſhuld go take ther viage vpōn tratours lewelī dauid ̄ wonder herd tho wynter wale whē cūtres ſomer ¶and lewelin let ordeyn well araye vitolle good caſtell swandon wos therin huge nombre pepull plente vitales ſo kīg edward wyſte wherfor entre ¶and wen kīges mē ꝑſaued alſo ſtrength wale let come ſe barge botes gret plankis mony o myght ordeyn haue gon forſaid caſtell swandō men fote eke horſe ¶but walſhmen ſo moch peple wer ſo ſtrong yt driuen engliſſhmen ayen ſo ther ſo moch bachilars gaſcoyns wer ſowdiours duellyng forſaid iohan veſſie vnd er fong wage wyth wer withold nobull men wer fight brent mony tounes kylled moch pepull walſhmen myght take ¶and tho ſtrength myght made aſſaute vn caſtell swandon get caſtell ¶and dauid prīce brother herd tydyng ordeyned flight ¶and lewelin prince ſaw brother fled ſore abaſſed pouer maynten ¶and ſo lewelin gan fle wened well haue ſcappid morow ſir roger mortemer met x knyghtis ſet round ̄ went ſmoten hede preſentid vn kyng edward ¶and maner prince wale taken hede ſmyten ̄ al heiris diſherited eu er thurgh rightfull dome landis reame ¶how dauid lewelins brother prince wale wos put deth dauid prīces brother wale thurgh prid wened haue bene prince wale brother deth ¶and vpon ſent walſhmen parlament dinbigh ̄ foliſhly made walis ariſe ayens kyng began meue ayens kīg edward ̄ ſorowe diſeſe myght bi pouer ¶when kīg edward herde thyng ordeyned men purſue vpō dauid ferſly defendid till come toune ſent morice ther wos dauid take fled lad kyng ¶and ye kīg commaūdid ſhuld honged ̄ draw ſmyte hede quartir ſend hede londō iiij quartirs ſend iiij chief toūes wale ſhuld take exampull therof ̄ beware ¶and aft er ¶and aft er ſent lordis wale bi letter patent ſh̄ uld cū ꝑlament wer comen kyng ſaid full curteſly lordynges ye welcome behoueth coūcell help wend gaſcoyn amē de treſpaces wos dene wos ther entret pee bitwen kyng aragon prince morrey ¶and kynges liege men erles baron conſentid grauntid therto ¶and tho made kyng edward redy went gaſcoyn let amend treſpaces wos done gaſcoyn debate wos betwen kyng aragon prince morrey ceſid made accordid ¶and whyle good kyng edward quene elienore wife gaſcoyn good erle cornewaill wos made wardeyn englond till kyng edward come ayen· ¶and tho enquerid traitours congetten falſeneſſe ayens eche vnderfenge ther dome aft er deſerued ¶but mene tyme good kyng edward beyond ſe done make amendis ayens trepaſſid ther fals thefe tratour wos called riſap meridoc began make ayens kyng edward wos encheſon sir payne tiptot wrongfully greued diſeſed forſaid riſap meridoc ¶and kyng edward herd ſent bi letter riſap meridoc ſhold begynne make ſhuld pee loue come ayen englond wold vnd er take quarell amēd wos myſdone ¶this forſaid riſap meridoc deſpiſid kynges cō mandemēt ̄ ſparid ſorow yt myght ye kīgꝭ men englond anone aft er wos takyn lad yorke ther wos draw ̄ honged felonye ¶of redreſſing kyng edward made ioſtices clerkis done ther falſenes drofe iues englōd ther vſeri ̄ miſbeleue kyng edward duelled iij yere gaſcoyn wylle come wend ayen englond wen wos cume ayen fonden ſo mony playntes made iuſtices ̄ clerkis done ſo mōy wronges ̄ falſeneſſe wondir wos ¶and wich falſnes sir thomas weylond kīges iuſtice forſwore englōd ye toure lundō falſenes men put vpō wherof wos atteint proued fals ¶and anōe kyng wyll iuſtices ¶tho let enquere aſpi iues deſaued ̄ begiled pepull thurgh ther ſine falſeneſſe vſerie let ordeyn priue parlamēt among lordis ordeynid emōg iues ſhuld void englōd ther miſbeleue alſo ther fals vſeri vntill criſtyn men ¶and ſped make end thīg communite englond yaf vn king xv peny ther goodis meuabull ̄ ſo wer iues driuē englōd ¶and tho went iues fraūce ̄ ther duellid thurgh leue kīg philip tho wos kīg fraūce ¶how king edward wos ſeiſed land ſcotland thurgh ꝯſent ̄ graūt lordis scotland long aleſander kyng scotlōd deid dauid erle huntindone kynges brother scotland axed clymed kyndom scotland brother wos deid encheſō rightfull heir mony gret lordis scotland ſaiden nay wherfore gret debate aroſe bitwen ther frendis moch wold conſent coronacion mene tyme forſaid dauid died ¶and ſo befell yt ſame dauid iij doughtres yt worthely wer maried friſt dought er wos marid bailloll ſecūd brus ye thrid haſtīg· forſaid bailloll ̄ brus chalenged land ſcotland gret debate ſtrife aroſe bitwen iij encheſon ych wold haue bene kyng ¶and lordis ſcotland ſaw debate bitwen iij come kyng edward englōd ̄ ſeiſid land ſcotland chefe lord ¶and kīg wos ſeiſed forſaid lordis ſcotland forſaid bailloll brus haſtynges come kynges court axed kyng wich ſhuld kyng ſcotland ¶and kyng edward wos full gentill ̄ trew let enquere croniclis ſcotland gret lordis ſcotland wich wos eldeſt blod wos foūde bailloll wos eldiſt kyng scotland ſhuld hold kyng englond ̄ feaute homage ¶and aft er thys wos done bailloll went scotland ̄ ther wos croūed kyng ſcotland ¶and ſame tyme vpō ſee gret bitwen ēgliſhmē normās vpō time ye normās arriued dou er ther martired holy man called thomas dou er aft er ward wer norman kylled ther aſcappid thē ¶and ſone aft er kīg edward ſhuld leſe duchie gaſcoyn thurgh kīg philip fraunce thurgh fals caſtyng douſeperis land wherfor ſir edmond wos kīg edward brother yaf vp homage vn kyng fraūce ¶and tyme clerkis englond graūtid kyng edward halfendele holy chirch gooddis helpyng recou er land ayen gaſcoyn ¶and kīg ſent thid er nobull company bachilers ſelf wold haue gone porteſmouth wos let thurgh maddoc wale ſeiſed caſtell swandō hand ̄ encheſō ye kīg turned wale criſtemaſe encheſō yt ye nobull lordis englōd yt wer ſēt ī gaſcoyn cōforth ther lord ye kīg wer take ſir charles fraūce yt ſay ſir iohn̄ bretā ſir robert tiptot▪ ſir raufe tāny ſir hugh bardolf ̄ ſir adam creting ̄ yit aſcenciō madoke take wale yt wos called morgan wer ſent tour londō ̄ ther wer heded ¶how ſir iohn̄ bailloll kīg ſcotlād withſaid homage ſir iohn̄ bailloll kyng ſcotland vnderſtode yt kyng edward wos wered gaſcoyn reame scotland delyu er ed falſely tho ayen oth ſaid homage thurgh procuring folke· ſent vn court rome thurgh fals ſuggeſtion aſſoiled othe ſwore vn kyng englōd ſo wos letter enbulled ¶tho choſen ſcotland douſſpers nymme edward right ¶and tyme come ij cardinales court rome fro pope celeſtine trete accorde bitwen kng fraūce ̄ kyng englond ¶and tho two cardinales ſpeke accorde thomas turbeluill take liouns ̄ made feaute homage warden paris ̄ hī put ij ſonys hoſtage thought go ī englond till aſpie cuntre ̄ tell come englond brokyn kynges priſon fraūce nyght ſaid wold done yt al engliſſhmē ̄ walſh̄men ſh̄old bow king fraūce ̄ thyng bring ende ſwore ̄ vpō couenant dedis wer made betwen thēm ſh̄uld haue yere m· poūdes worth lond bring thing ende ¶this fals tratour toke leue ̄ wēt thēs come englond vn kyng ſaid wos brokyn priſō put ſuch ꝑill loue wherfore kyng coude moch thanke full glad wos commyng ¶and fals tratour fro day aſpied doyng kyng ̄ alſo coūſell kyng loued wel ̄ full priue clerke englond wos kynges houſe fraunce herd treſon falſnes wrot clerke tho wos duellyng edward kyng englond thomas turbeluill done falſe coniectyng councell englōd wos writte haue ſent vn kyng fraūce thurgh foreſaid letter clerke ſent fro fraūce hit wos foūde vpō wherfor wos lad londō honged draw ther treſō ij ſonys yt put fraūce hoſtage wer tho beheded ¶of counqueſt berewyke tho two cardinales wer went ayene fraunce trete pee cambrey kyng ſent thider erlis barouns ſay ſir edmond brother erle lancaſtre leyceſtre ſir henri lacy erle nichol willm veſſy baron baronettis xiiij beſt ̄ wiſeſt englōd ¶and ī ſame tyme king edward toke viage scotland vpō iohn̄ bailloll kyng ſcotland ¶and ſir robert roos berewyke fled fro engliſſhmē went ſcottys kyng edward went toward berewike ̄ beſeged ye toūe ̄ tho yt wer within manly defendid ſet fire brint ij kyng edwardis ſhippis ſaid diſpite reproue ¶weneth kyng edward long ſhankis haue get berewike al vnthankis gas pike done gas dike ¶when kyng edward herd ſcorne anone thurgh myghtynes paſſid ou er dike ̄ aſſailed toūe come yates gat conquerid toūe thurgh gracious pouer kylled xxv thouſand ̄ vijc ſcottys kyng edward loſt man renoune ſaufe ſir richard cornewaill kylled flemmyng reed hall quarell foreſaid richard helme commaūdid yeld put kynges grace ſcottis wold wherfor hall brent caſtyn doune tho wer therin wer brant ¶and king edward loſt mo men viage ſymple eſtate xxvij engliſſhmen wardeyn caſtell yaf vp key aſſaute ¶and ther wos takyn willm douglas sir symond friſell ̄ erle patrike yeld pee bot inghm̄ humſremille robert brus wer kyng edward forſoke kyng edward held ſcottis aft er ward wer takyn put priſon aft er king yaf ther treſpaſſe deliu er id priſon ¶and tho let kyng edward cloſe berwik wally dychis aft er ward robert rous went tindale ſet wuyebrugge fire exham ̄ lamerſtok kyllid robbed folke cuntre ¶and went then vn dumbarre ¶and friſt wedeneſday marche kyng ſent erle garenne sir hugh perci ſir hugh spen ser fair companye beſege caſtell ¶but wos called ſir richard syward traitour fals man ymagyned begile engliſſhnen ſent engliſſhmen diſſaue ſaid wold yelde vn caſtell yf wold graūte viij· dais reſpit myght ſend ̄ tell ſir iohan bailoll wos kyng scotland men faired wer caſtell ſend hī word bot wold remeue ſege engliſſhmen· wold yelde caſtell vn engliſſhmē ¶the meſſinger tho come vn ſir iohan bailoll tho wos kyng scotland wher wos hoſt meſſing er told hī al ye caſe ¶and ſir iohan toke tho hoſt ̄ come morow erly toward caſtell ¶and ſir richard siward ſaw cum wos maſter counſell keꝑ caſtell ̄ ſaid vn engliſſmen qd ſe fare cōpanye well appariled gon ayens ̄ mette aſſaill ¶and ſir hugh spen ser ſaw falſeneſſe treſon ſaid tratour take ̄ proued falſeneſſe ſhall vaill hugh ye ſpē ser cōmādid anone bynde hī ī haſt wēt ayens ther enmys killid ſcottys xxijm ſcottys time man honour ſauf ſir patrik graham yt manli faught ̄ long ̄ laſt kylled tho ſaid engliſſhmen ī reproue ſcottys ¶thes ſcaterand ſcottys hold ſottis wrench vn ware erli mornyng euell tymyng went ye fro dunbare tho caſtell ſaw ſcomfiture yolden vp caſtell vn engliſſhmen boūdē hir body londis caſtellis kīg edward ſo thei wer take ther caſtell iij erles vij baron ̄ xxviij knyghtis xi clerkis vij picardis ̄ wer preſentid kyng edward ſent vn toure londō keped ther ¶how kyng edward gret grace deliu er ed ayeij ſcotis priſon wer chieftens land drew thē frenſſhmen thurgh coūſell willm waleis kyng edward made tho end taken chefetayns ſcotland tho come ſir iohane bailloll yelde vn kyng edward put grace lad london kyng edward comē thid er wer brought kīg axed wold make amendis treſpaſſe loſſe thei done thei put ī merci ¶lordīges qd kīg wyll landis ne goodis wyll ye make oth vpon goddis body trew neu er thys tyme ayenſt bere army ꝯſentid kynges ſwore vpō goddis body ¶that ſay ſir iohan comyn erle ſtrathorne erle carrik alſo iiij biſſhoppis vnd er toke clarge ſo kīg deliu er id yaf ſaufe condithys wend ī ther land long aft er ward ne ariſen ayen kyng edward encheſon wiſt well kyng edwardis folke take gaſcoyne ſayed ſir iohn̄ bailloill kīg ſcotland wiſt well land ſhuld haue ſorow ſhame ther falſeneſſe haſt went ou er ſe landes ther held come neu er ayen wherfor scottys choſin vn ther kīg willm waleis ribaud harlot cumen vp noght ̄ moch harme engliſſhmen ¶and kyng edward thought myght haue deliu er ance pepull wer take gaſcoyn ̄ ī haſt went ou er ſee flaūdres vpon kīg fraunce erle flaundres vnd er fenge moch honour ̄ graūted landis ¶and king fraūce herd tell kynge englond wos ariued flaūdres ̄ come huge pouer hī diſtruye praied trews ij yere ſo engliſſh marchantis ̄ alſo frenſſh might ſaufely go cum bothe ſidis ¶the king edward graūted ſo muſt haue men p̄ſon wer ī gaſcoyn ̄ ye kīg fraūce graūtid anone ̄ ſo wer deliu er id ¶and ī ye ſame tyme ſcottys ſent biſſhop ſent andrew fraūce kīg ſir charles brother ſir charles ſhuld cum pouer ̄ ſcotland wold cum ther pouer ſo ſhuld go englond land diſtruy ſcotland vn comen kent ſcottys traſtid moch vpō frenſſhmē thyng man er graūte ¶and notheles ſcottis began robbe ̄ kill northumberlōd moch harme ¶how willm waleis let ſle ſir hugh creſſingham bataill fonkirke tidyng comen te kȳg edward willm waleis ordeyned ſuch ſtrong pouer alſo scotlond vn wos entendant redy kyll engliſſh men diſtroye land ſore annoyed ſent annone letter erle garren ſir henri ꝑcy ſir willm latomer ſir hugh creſſingham treſorer ſhuld take pouer wend northumberland ̄ ſo forth ſcotland kepe cuntris ¶and william waleis herd hir commyng gan fle engliſhmen folewid drefe till come striuelyn ther held caſtell ¶and walſſhmen eu er day eſcried manaced diſpite myght ye engliſſhmē vpō tyme mornyng wēt caſtell moūtenāce x mile ̄ paſſid ou er brigge willm waleis come ſtrong pouer ̄ drofe bake engliſſhmē ayens tho myght fled yt myght take brigge aſcappid ſir hugh kynges treſorour ther ſlain mony alſo wherfore wos made mich ſorow ¶tho kyng edwar ſped nedis flaūdris wos ayen comen englond haſt toke way ſcotland come thed er aſcenciō tide foūd ſet fire brent ¶but poer pepull ſcotland cō wond er thyke prayd goddis loue wold haue merci pitte ¶wherfor kyng • ho commandid man ſh̄old harme wer yoldin ne man ordir ner houſe religion ne man er chirche let aſpie myght wher myght find ony enmys ¶tho come aſpi vn kyng told wher scottys wer aſſembled bide bataill ¶and ſent mari magdelene day kyng come fonkirke yaf bataill ſcottis bataill wer kylled xxxiij thouſand ſcottys engliſhe men xxviij mo wich worthy knyght ſlayn wos knyght hoſpiteler wos callid freri brian iay ¶for willm wale fled bataill thatt ſame frere brian purſued ferſly hors ran ſtart myere mary vp bely ¶and willm walis turned tho ayene ̄ kylled forſaid brian yt wos moche harme ¶and kyng edward wēt thurgh ſcotlād enquere myght find enmys ī yt land duelled long likyd ther wos none enmye yt durſt abide ¶and ſone aft er ward kīg edward wēt ſouth hamtō wold abyde ſcotland wynt er ſeſon eſemēt pepull come londō let amēd mony miſdedis wer done ayens pee law yt wos flaundres ¶of laſt mariege king edward went thrid tyme scotland aft er ward ordeyned thurgh court rome yt kīg edward ſhuld wedde dame margaret kīg philip ſuſtre fraūce ye erchebiſſhop robert wynchelſe ſpouſed thē gedre thurgh wich mariege ther wos made pe betwen kyng edward englond kyng philip fraunce ¶kyng edward went tho thrid tyme scotland tho within firſt yere enfamined land ſo ther left ne come merci ſauf tho yt wer caſtell eſtreuelin yt wos well vetaled ̄ aſtorid vij yere ¶how caſtell eſtreuelin wos beſeged kyng edward come huge pouer caſtell eſtreuelin beſeged caſtell litell vailed might ſcottis none harme caſtell wos ſo ſtrong well kepid ¶and kyng edward ſaw thought vpō queyntize ̄ let make anone ther ij paire high galews tour ye caſtell ̄ made oth mōy wer ī caſtell wer erle baron wer take ſtrength wold rather yold ſh̄uld honged vpō galewis ¶and tho wer within caſtell heerd come yeld kyngꝭ grace ̄ merci kīg yaf maletalent ¶and ther wer gret lordis ſcotland ſwore kyng edward ſhuld cum london eu er parlament ſhuld ſtond ordynance ¶how troylebaſtonne wos firſt ordeyned kyng edward went then londō wenet haue reſt ̄ pee ī wich wos ocupied xx yere ſay wale gaſcoyn scotlād thught myght recouer treſour ſpendid let enquere thurgh reame tyme yt bene reame men called troillebaſton ordeyned ther iuſtices ̄ man er recou er yed treſour nombre ¶and encheſō wos thought till haue gone ī holy land haue werid vpon goddis enmis encheſō croſſid long tyme ¶and neu er thelas law ordeyned moch good thurgh englond wer myſbode tho treſpaſſid wer well chaſtiſed afterward moch meker ̄ better ̄ thee poer commyns wer reſt ̄ pee ¶and ſame tyme kīg edward priſoned ſon edward encheſō walter langtō biſſhop cheſtre wos kynges treſorar made vpō complayn ſaid forſaid edward thurghe coūſell ̄ ꝓcurment pers ganaſton ſquyer gaſcoī brokyn parkis forſaid biſſhapois ̄ pers coū cellid lad ſame edward ¶and cauſe kyng odward exiled ſon englond eu er ¶of deth willm waleis fals tratour whē kyng edward enmys ou er cummyn wale gaſcoyn scotland diſtroyd traitours ribaud willm wale neu er kīg wold yeld laſt toune ſent dominic ī yere kyng edward regne xxxiij fals tratour wos take ̄ preſentid kyng kyng wold ſe ſent london und er fenge iugement vpon ſent bartholomes eue wos honged draw hede ſmyten hys bowelis take bodi brint ̄ bodi quartired ſent vn iiij beſt tounes ſcotlad hede put vpō ſpere ſet vpon london brigge exampull ſcottis ſhuld haue mynd amys ayens ther leige lord eftſones ¶how ſcottis come kyng edward amēd ther treſpaſſe done ayens mihelmaſſe tho next commyng kyng edward helde parlament weſtmynſtre thider come ſcots ſay biſſhop ſent andrewes robert brus erle carik simōd ye friſell iohū ye erle athell thei wer accordid kīg bounde oth ſwore aft er ward miſbore ayens kyng edward ſhuld diſherited eu er ¶and whan ther pee thus made toke ther leue priueli wēt home vn ther cuntre ¶how robert brus chalenged ſcotland aft er robert brus erle carik ſent letter erles baron scotland ſhulde come scone morow concepcion lady hegh nedes land lordis come day aſſined ¶and ſame day ſir robert brus ſaid fair lordis full well ye know ꝑſon duelled right reame ſcotland o ye wate well rightfull heir ſith ſir iohan bailoll wos kyng v hath forſaken ̄ left land ¶and though ſo kyng edward englond wrongfull pouer hath made aſſent ayens wyll ye wyll graunt may kyng ſcotland ſhall kepe ayens kyng edward englond ayens man er men yt word abbot scon aroſe vp ſaid reſon helpe ̄ land ta kepe defend tho ſaid preſens wold yef thouſand pound maynten land ̄ graūted land hī ther pouer help defied kyng edward englond ̄ ſaid robert brus▪ ſh̄uld kīg englond ¶how ſir iohn̄ comyn yen ſaid crounyng ſir robert brus lordynges ſaid ſir iohn̄ comyn thenketh vpon truth oth ye made vn kyng edward englond touchyng ſelf breke myne oth man ſo went company tyme wherfore robert brus tho conſentit wer wonder wroth tho manaced ſir iohn̄ comyn ¶tho ordeyned councell domfris wich come forſaid ſir iahan comyn duelled ij myle domfris ther yt woned ſodiorne bide ¶how ſir iohn̄ traitourſ • kylled robert brus wiſt grete lordis ſcotland wer commyn scone ſauf ſir iohn̄ comyn ſodiorned tho nygh scone ſent aft er ſpecialli ſir iohan comyn ſhuld cum ſpeke vpon come ̄ ſpeke gray freris damfres thurſday aft er candilmaſday ſir iohn̄ grauntid wend ¶and herd maſſe toke ſoppe ̄ drank aft er ward beſtrod palfray rode way ſo come domfres robert brus ſaw cum wī daw chambre tho made ioye ynough come ayens coled nec made hī goode ſemblant ¶and erles baron ſcotlād wer preſent ther ¶robert bruſe ſpake ſaid sirres ſaid ye wot well encheſon commyng wherfore ye graunte might kyng scotland right heir land· lordis wer ther ſaid vois ſhuld crouned kyng ſcotland wold helpe maynten ayens maner men liue wer nede die ¶the gentill knyght tho iohan comyn anſwerid ſaid certis neu er ne haue moch help vaill boton oth haue made vn kyng edward englond ſhall hold whil lefe laſt worde went companie ̄ wold haue wened vpon palfrie robert brus purſued drawen ſword bare thurgh bodi ſir iohan comyn fell doune vn erthe whenne rogier wos ſir iohn̄ comyns brether ſaw falſeneſſe ſtarit ſir robert brus ſmote hym wyth knyfe falſe tratour wos armyd vndir ſo ſtroke myght done harme an̄d ſo moch help come bout ſir robert brus ſo rogier comyn ther kylled hew peſes ¶and robert brus turned ayen ther ſir iohon comyn nobull baron lay wounded pyned towarde deth ſides high auter chirche gray freris ſaid vn ſir iohan comyn traytour thou ſhall deid neu er let myne vauncement ſhoke ſwerde high auter ſmote hede brayn fell doune vpon grounde blod ſtert high vpon walles yit vn day blod ſeyn ther water may waſhe way ̄ ſo died nobull knyght holy chirche tratour robert brus ſaw man wold let coronacion commaunded pouer ſhuld cum vn crounyng ſant iohanes toūe scotland ¶and ſo befell vpon lady day annuncion biſſhop glaſton biſſhop ſente andrewes crouned ther kyng robert brus ſent iohanes toune made kīg ¶and anone aft er drofe engliſſhmen cut ſcotland fled come plened vn kyng edward robert brus driuen land diſherited ¶how kyng edward dubbed weſtmynſtre xxiiij ſcore knyghttis kīg edward hered myſcheef ſwore yt ſhuld bene venged therof ſaid tratours scotland ſh̄uld bene honged draw ſhuld neuer raunſomed ¶and kyng edward thought vpō falſeneſſe ſcottis done ſent bachelars englond thei ſhuld cum londō witſontide· dubbed weſtmynſtre xxiiij ſcore knyghtis ¶th • ordeyned nobull kīg edward wend ſcotland vpon robert brus ſent hī ī ſcotland ſir aymer valaūce erle penbruke ̄ ſir henri percy baron wt afair cōpanye purſued ſcotis brend toūes ̄ caſtels ̄ aft er ward come kīg hī ſelf wt erles baron fair companye ¶how robert brus wos diſcomfited bataill ̄ symond friſell ſlayn friday next aſſumcion lady kyng edward met robert brus beſide ſent iohanes toune ſcotland componye wich companye kyng edward kylled vij thouſand ¶when robert brus ſawe miſchief gan fle hid man might fīd ſir symond friſell purſued ſore ſo turned ayene ̄ bode bataill wos worthi knyght ̄ bold body ye engliſſhmē purſued eu er ſore eu er ſide kylled ſtede ſir symond friſell rode vpon toke lad vn hoſt ¶and ſir symond began flater ſpeke fair ſaid lordis ſhall yef iiij m▪ marke ſilu er myn horſe myne harnes myne armure becum beggar ¶tho anſuered theobaude peuenes wos kinges archier ſo god helpe nought thou ſpeketh gold englond wold let go wt ꝯmaundement kīg edward ¶and tho wos vn king edward kyng wold ſe commaūded lede way haue dome london ¶and lady eue na •• te wos honged drow dnd hede ſmyten honged ayē chynes yren vpon galowes hede ſet vpō london brigge vpō ſpere ayenſt criſtemaſſe body wos brenned encheſon men keped body nyght ſaw ſo mony deuels rampaand gret yren crokys rennyng vpon galowes orabuli turmented wer brought kyng kyng ſent vn pope rome ſhuld done wt ¶how iohn erle atheles wos taken ̄ put deth bataill fled ſir iohan erle atheles went chirche ther hid drede myght haue ther refute encheſan chirche wos enterdited thurgh generall ſentens ſame chirche wos taken ¶and ſir iohan went well haue ſcapped deth encheſon clamed kynrad kyng edward king nold longer trayed traitours ſent hī london ī haſt ther wos honged ̄ hede ſmyten ̄ body brend aſſis prayer ye quene margaret encheſō yt clamed kīg edwar kynred drawyng wos foryeue ¶how iohn̄ yt wos willm waleis brod er wos put deth greteſt maſters scotland wer thus done euell deth ſhendid ther falſeneſſe iohan wos willm waleis brother wos take done vn deth ſir iohn̄ erle atheles wos ¶how robert brus fled ſcotland norway ſame tyme wos robert brus moch hated among pepull scotland ſo wyſt wos beſt done hide hī wēt ī norway thee kyng ſpouſed ſuſtre ̄ ther held ſocour haue ¶and robert brus might foūde ſcotland ſo kȳg edward tho let crie pee thurgh lād lawes wer vſid miniſtres ſerued thurgh land ¶how kyng edward died kyng edward abated enmys turned ayene ſouthward maladie toke burgh vpſand marche scotland wiſt well deth full nigh called hī ſir henri laci erle nicholl ſir guy erle werwik ſir aymer valēce erle penbroke ſir robert clifford barone ̄ prayd vpō faith owed ſhuld make edward carnariuan kyng englond raathe o myght ſhuld nat ſuffre pers ganaſton cum ayen englōd make ſon riot ̄ graūted wt good ¶and kīg toke ſacrement holy chirche good criſte man ſh̄uld died ī veray repētance whē bene kīg xxxv yere died wos buried weſtmīſtre wt moch ſolempnite vpō who ſoule god haue mercy ¶of merlin ꝓphecies wer declarid kyng edward wos kyng henri ſon kyng edward ꝓphecied merlin called dragon ſecund vi kynges ſhuld regne englond ſaid ſh̄uld medeled wyth merci alſo ſtrength ſterneſſe ſhuld kepe englond cold hete ſhuld open mouth toward wale ſhuld ſet fote wyke ſhuld cloſen wt walles ſhuld moch harme ſede ¶and ſaid ſoth good kyng edward medled merci ̄ ferſeneſſe wt merci ayens enmys wale ̄ aft er scotland ferſeneſſe whē put deth ther falſeneſſe tratori deſeruied ¶and well keped englond colde hete ſith keped maner enmys ronne vpon hym done wronge ¶and well opyned mouth toward wale ̄ made quake thurgh hidour mouth whē cōquerid thurgh dynt ſwerde· prince leuelin dauid brother ri morgan wer put deth ther falſenes ther foly ¶and ſet fote wike conquered berewyke wich conqueſt wer ſlayn xxv thouſand vij hondreth take wer brend reed hall ¶and walles let make ſhall noyous vn ſede mē ſhal aft er ſee lifee sir edward camarauan ſon ¶and yit ſaid merlin ſhuld make riueris ren ī blod brayn ſemed well weris ther maſtrie ¶and yit merlin ſaid ther ſh̄uld cum pepull north weſt regne forſaid dragon ſhuld lad yll grehound ſhuld dragō croune king afterward ſhuld fle ouer ſee drede dragon cummyng ayen ̄ wos proued ſir iohan bailloll kyng edward made kyng scotland falſely aroſe ayens fled vn landes fraunce neu er come ayen scotland drede kīg edward ¶and yit ſaid merlin pepull ſhuld lede forſaid grehond ſhuld fad er le vn till c er tan tyme ̄ ſaid ſoth pepull ſcotlād gretly wer diſeſed ſiith yt ſir iohn̄ bailloll ther kīg fled frō ſcotland ¶and yit ſaid merlin yt ſon ſhulde become tyme reed ony blode tokenyng gret mortalite pepull yt well knaw ye ſcottis wer ſlayn ¶and ſith ſaid merlin
