anone breke brugge wos made tre ¶and whan ſir thomas lancaſtre herde ſir andrew herkela brought ſuch pouer ſore drad ſent ſir andrew herkela wt ſpake· ſaid man er ¶sir andrew quod ye mow well vnd er ſtond lord kyng lad miſgou er ned moch fals councell thurgh ſir hugh spenſer fadre ſir hugh ſon ſir iohn̄ erle arundell thurgh maſter robert baldoke fals piled clerke kynges court duelling wherfore pray yow ye wold cum v pouer ye haue ordened help diſtro venym england tratours bene therin yeue vn yow beſt parte v erledoms haue holdeth make vn oth wil neuer done thyng councell ſo ye ſhall bene eft well v eu er wos robert holand ¶tho anſuerd ſir andrew herkela ſaid ſir thomas wolde done ne conſent ther maner thing ye might yeffe without commaūdement lore kyng ſhuld holden tratour eu er ¶and nobull erle thomas lancaſtre ſaw wold conſent vn man er thing ſir androw ſaid ye conſent diſtroye venym reame conſent one worde ſir androw tell yere gone ye ſhall take hold traitor ony yow hold v wors deth ye ſhall die eu er knyght englond vnd er ſtand well ye neu er thyng ſorer ye ſhall repente goth ̄ dothe good liketh wyll put mercy god ¶and ſo went fals traytour tirant fals ſworin maij thurgh noble erle thomas lancaſtre vnd er fenge armes chiualri thurgh hī wos made knyght ¶tho myght men ſee archeris drawe one ſide knyghtes alſo foughten tho gedre wonder ſore alſo among ſir humfrey de boughon erle herford worthy knyght renoune thurgh criſtyndome ſtode fought enmys vpon bruge nobull lord ſtode faught vpon brugge thefe ribaude ſkulked vnder brugge ferſly ſpere ſmote nobull knyght foūdement ſo bouell comen bout fete ther ¶alas ſorow ther ſlayn flour ſolace comforth alſo curteſie ¶and ſir roger clifford nobull knyght ſtode eu er faught well worthely defendid nobull baron laſt ſore wounded hede ſir willm sullay ſir roger bernefeld wer ſlayn bataill ¶when ſir androw herkela ſaw ſir thomas men lancaſtre laſſed ſlaked anone compani comen vn gentill knyght ſir thomas lancaſtre ſaid vn high yelde tratoure yeld ¶the gentill erle anſuerid tho ſaid nay lordis trators none neuer v yeld lyues laſt leu er haue ſlain treuth yeld v vn yow ¶and ſir androw ayen gard vpon ſir thomas componi yollyng wode wolfe ̄ ſaied yelde tratours takē yeld ſaid high vois beth war ſires none yow ſo hardy vpon lyfe limme myſdone thomas bodi lancaſtre ¶and word good erle thomas wēt ī chapell ſaid kneling vpon knee ̄ turned viſage towardes croſſe ſaid almyghty god yelde holli put vn thy merci vileyns ribaudes leped boute eu er ſyde tirantis wode turmē tour diſpolid armurie clothed robe rey ſquyers liueira forth lad vn yorke wat er ¶tho myght men ſe moch ſorow ̄ care thee gentill knyghtis fled eu er ſide ̄ ribaudis ̄ vileyns egreli diſcried gried high yeld yow tratours yeld ¶and wer yolden wer robbed bounde thefues ala ſhame diſpite gentill ordir knyghthod ther bataill land tho law holy chirche tho reuerance bene brodell hous bataill fadre ayens ſone vncle ayens nepheu ſo moch vnkyn denes neu er ſeyn englond wos tyme among folke one nacion ¶for kynrad pitte hungri wolfe hath ſhepe wos wonder ¶for gret lordis englond wer one nacion wer medled nacions ſay ſome bretans ſome saxōs ſom danys ſome pehites ſom frenſſhemen ſome norman ſome spanyardis ſome roman ſome henaudes ſome flemmyng diu er ſe nacions nacions accordid kind blod englond ſo gret lordis bene onli weddid engliſh pepull ſhuld pee haue bene reſt amonges owt enuy ¶and bataill roger clifford take ſir iohn̄ monbray ſir willm tuchit ſir willm fitz willm ̄ mōy worthy knyghtys ther wer take yt bataill ſir hugh dandell next day aft er wos taken ̄ put ī priſon ſhuld haue done deth ſpouſed kyngꝭ nece erle gilbertis ſuſtre gloceſtre ¶and anōe aft er wos ſir bartholomew badelſmere taken ſtowe paarke maner biſſhoppis lyncolne yt wos nepheu ̄ mony baron ̄ baner • ttz wherfore wos made moch ſorow ¶how thomas lancaſtre wos heded poun • fret v baron honged drawen ther ſhall tell yow nobull erle thomas lancaſtre wos taken brought yorke mōy cite wer full glad vpon cried high vois ſir traitour ye er welcome bliſſid god ſhall ye haue reward long tyme ye haue deſerued caſt vpon mony ſnowe balles mony reproues bot gentill erle ſuffred ̄ ſaid nothir word ne ¶and ſame tyme king herd ſame ſcomfiture wos full glad ̄ haſt come poūtfret ſir hugh ſpen ser ſir hugh ſon ſir iohn̄ erle arundell ̄ ſir edmond wodeſtoke kynges brother erle kent ſir aymer valaunce erle penbroke maſter robert baldoke fals piled clarke priue duellid kynges courte come thed er wt kyng kyng entred ī caſtell ¶and ſir andrew herkela fals tirant thurgh kynges commaundement toke gentill erle thomas poūtfret ̄ ther priſoned caſtell new made ſtode ayen abbey kyng edward ¶and ſir hugh ſpen ser fad er ſon caſt ̄ thought man er good erle thomas lancaſtre ſh̄uld dede ony iugement hys perys ¶wherfore ordened thurgh kyngꝭ iuſtices yt kīg ſhold put vpon pointes treſon ¶and ſo befell yt led barre kīgis iuſtis barehed thef fair hall caſtell yt made ther mōy fair feſt rich poer ¶and thes wer iuſtiſes ſir hugh ſpen ser father aymer valaūce erle peenbroke ſir edmōd wodeſtoke erle kent ſir iohn̄ bretan erle richemond ſir robert malemethrop iuſtice ſir roberte coulpid maner ¶thomas friſt owr lord kyng court excludeth maner anſuere ¶thomas lord kyng putteth vpon yow ye haue land riden banner diſplayed ayens pe tratoure worde gentill erle thomas wt high vois ſaid nay lordis forſoth bi ſent thomas neu er traytour ¶the iuſtice ſaid ayen tho ¶thomas lord kyng puteth vpon ye haue robbed folk mordred pepull thefe ¶thomas alſo kyng put vpon diſcomfited pepull folkd reame wherfor ye went fled wodde outlawe ¶and alſo ye taken outlawe ¶and thomas traitour ye ſhall hanged reſon kīg hath yef iewes loue quene iſabell ¶and thomas reſon wold alſo ye ſhuld hanged kīg hath yef iewes cauſe loue linage ¶but thomas o moch ye wer take fleyng ̄ outlaw king wyll hede ſhall ſmyte ye haue well de ser ued anone doth prece anone bring iugement ¶the gentill knyght thomas herd thes wordis high vois cried ſore wepyng ſaid ala ſent thomas fair fader ala ſhall dede thus ¶graunte bliſſidfoll god anſuer vailled nothyng curſed gaſcoyns put hither thedder cried high vois kyng arthur moſt dredfull well knawen thyn open traitorie euell dethe ſhalt thow die thow haſt well diſeruyed ¶and tho ſet vpen hede ſcorn hold chapelet wos rent wos worth half penne ¶and ſet vpon leue white palfra full vn ſemeli eke bare hold bridell horribul noiſe droue caſtell toward deth caſt vpon mony balles ſnowe ī diſſpite ¶and traitoris lad caſtell tho ſaied pytouſe wordis handes held vp hight toward heuen kyng heuen yef v merci erthely kyng hath v forſakyn frere prechour wenten caſtell till com place endid lyfe vn ſhrofe life ¶and gentill erle held frere wond er faſt clothis ſaid fair fadre abide v till dede fleſh quaketh drede deth ¶and ſoth ſay gentill erle ſet vpon knee turned toward eſt ribaud called higone moſton ſet hand vpon gentill erle ſaied deſpite sir traytour turne toward ſcottes thy ſoule dede vnderfenge turned toward northe ¶the nobull erle thomas anſuered tho myld vois ſaid fair lordis ſhall done woide frere went ſore wepyng anone ribaude went ſmote hede xi kal auerell yere grece mccc xxi ¶alas eu er ſuch gētill blod ſhall done deth cauſe reſon ¶and tratorſly wos kyng coūcellid whē thurgh fals counſell ye ſpē ſers ſuffred ſir thomas vncles ſon put ſuch deth ſo bene heded ayens man er reſon gret pitte alſo ſuch nobull kyng ſh̄uld deſceiued myſgou er ned thurgh counſell fallis ſpenſeres wich tho maīteneyd thorow loſelrie ayens honour eke ꝓfite aft er ward ther fell gret vengeaunce englond encheſon foreſaid thomas deth ¶when gentill erle life paſſid priour monkis pountfret getten body ſir thom̄s kīg beried high aut er right ſide • ¶that ſame day gentill knyght dede ther honged draw ſame quarell pountfret ſir willm tuchet ſir willm fitz willm ſir warreyn yſell ſir hēri brad borne ſir william cheynye baron all· iohane page eſquyre ¶and ſone aft er yorke draw honged ſir rogeri clifford sir iohan mambray baron ſir goſelin dauill knyght ¶and briſtow drawe honged ſir henri wemyngton ſir henri mounfort baron gloceſtre wer draw honged sir iohan geffard ſir willm elmebrugge baron ¶and london wer honged drow ſir henri tyes baron wynchelſe ſir thomas colepepir knyght windeſore ſir fraunces waldenham baron cantorburi wos draw ̄ honged ſir bertholome badeleſmere ſir bartholomewe aſſhebourneham baron kerdyfe ī wale ſir willm flemmīg baron ¶how kyng edward wēt ſcotland hondreth thouſand men armes ̄ might ſpede kyng edward englond brought flour chiualrie vn ther deth thurgh councell conſent ſir hugh ſpenſer fadre ſir hugh ſon become wode lyon ¶and ſo eu er spenſers wold haue done ſo well kyng loued might done wt thyng liked wherfor kyng yaf vn ſir hugh ſpenſer fadre erledom wyncheſtre vn ſir andrewe herkela erdom cardoill preiudice harmyng croune ¶and kyng edward tho thurgh ꝯſell ſpenſers diſherited bene ayens quarell thomas lancaſtre mony oder wer diſherited alſo encheſon ſtat ſpenſers couetted haue ther landes ſo wold deſire wrong ayens reſon ¶tho made kyng robert baldok fals piled clerke chauncelar englond thurgh caunſell forſaid ſpen ser fals ribaud couetiſe ̄ ſo coūceled kyng moch kyng let take warde goodis lordis put wrongfully deth hond well token goodis wer holy chirche goodis wythout let bene put treſorie london let call forfaittis bi ther councell kyng wrought eu er dyſherite goodis owghten ¶and thurgh ther counſell let rere talliage goodis englond ¶wherfor richeſt kyng eu er wos englond willm baſterd normā die conquerid englond▪ ¶and yit thurgh councell ſemed ynough bot made yit eu er toune englond find man army vpon ther coſtages gone vpon ſcottis wer enmys wherfore kyng wēt ſcotland hondreth thauſand mē armes witſontide yere lord ihū criſt mccc xxij ¶but ſcottis went hid moūtayns ̄ woddis taried engliſhmen fro day day kīg myght maner thyng find playn feld ¶wherfor mony engliſhmē yt litell vitayles died ther hunger wond er faſt ſodenly goyng comyng namly tho bene ayens thomas lancaſtre robbed men vpon landis ¶when kyng edward ſaw vitayles failed wos tho wonderfore diſcomforted encheſon alſo men died myght ſpeed enmys laſt come ayen englond ¶and anone come iames douglas alſo thomas randulph hoge hoſt englond northumberland engliſhmen wer driuē englōd come robbed cūtre kylled pepull alſo brend toune wos called northallerton ̄ mony toūes yorke ¶and kīg herd tidyng let ſompne man er men might trauell ſo engliſhmen mett ſcottis abbey beigheland xv day aft er mihelmaſſe ſame yere aboueſaid engliſhmen wer ther diſcomfited ¶and yt ſcomfiture wos toke ſir iohan bretan erle rochemond helde cuntre erldom lancaſtre ¶and paied huge raunſome wos let go aft er wente fraūce come neu er afterward ayen ¶how ſir andrewe herkela take ̄ put vn deth wos erle cardoill tyme ſir andrew herkela new made erle cardoill cauſe taken good erle thomas lancaſtre ordeyned thurgh kynges ꝯmandement englond bring pouer might help ayenſt ſcottis abbey beigheland ¶and fals tratour gadred pepull myght ſhuld haue come kyng vn abbey beigheland ¶the fals tratour lad cuntre thurgh copeland thurgh erledom lancaſtre went thurgh cuntre robbed ̄ killed folke myght ¶and forther fals tratour taken gret ſoume gold ſilu er ſir iames douglas ayens kyng englond bene helpyng holdyng ſcottis thurgh who treſon kyng englond wos diſcomfited beigheland come thed er ¶wherfor kyng wos toward wond er wroth let priueli enquere cuntre wos· ¶and ſo men enquerid aſpied ſo laſt trewth foūd ſought atteynt take fals tratour ye good erle thoms lancaſtre told wer put vn deth takyng burbrugge ¶and ſaid yere wer done ſhuld take hold tratour ¶and ſo wos holy man ſaid wherfor kyng ſent preueli ſir anthoyn lucy knight cuntre cardoill ſhuld take ſir andrew harkela put vn deth ¶and bring thys thyng vn end kyng ſent comiſſion ſame andrew take cardoill ̄ led vn barre maner erle worthely arrayed ̄ ſwerde gurt aboute hī hoſed ̄ ſpored ¶tho ſpak ſir anthoyn maner ſir andrew ꝙ king put vpon moch thou haſt bene orped thy dedis ded moch honour made erle cardoill thou traytour thi lord kyng ladeſt pepull cuntre ſhuld haue holpe bataill beiland thou ladeſt way cuntre copeland thurgh erledom lancaſtre wherfor lord kyng diſcomfited ther ſcottis thurgh thy treſon falſeneſſe thou hadeſt comen tymes bataill treſō thou diddeſt gret ſoume gold ſilu er thou vnderfenge iames douglas ſcot kynges enmye ¶and lord kyng ordir knyghod thou vnderfeng thyn honoor worſhip vpon thy body al brought nought thi eſtate vndone knyghttes lawer degre mow aft er war wich lord hath vaūced hugli diu er ſe cuntreis englond yt may take exſample ye ther lord aft er ward trewly ser ue ¶tho commanded knaue anone hewe ſpors heles aft er let brake ſwerd ou er hede wich kyng yaf kepe ̄ defēd land ther made erle cardoill ¶and aft er let vnclothed furred tabard ̄ hode furred cote gurdel wos ſir antonye ſaid vn andrew quod art thow knyght bot knaue ̄ thi treſon kyng thow ſhalt bene honged drawe ̄ thyn hede ſmyten ̄ thi bowelels taken thy body ̄ brent thy body quartired thyn deſent london ther ſhall ſtond vpō londō brigge iiij quarter ſhall ſent iiij toūes englond may war ̄ chaſtiſed bi ¶and antonye ſaid ſo done maner thyng laſt day october yere grace mccc xxij yere ¶and ſone turned blod pepull ſaw durid morne till xi cloke day ¶of myracles god wrought ſent thomas lancaſtre wherfore kyng let cloſe chirche doris priore pountfret yt mā ſhuld cum therin body offren ſone aft er good erle thomas lancaſtre martired ther preſt long tyme blind dremed ſlepyng ſhuld gone vn hill ther yt good erle thomas lancaſtre wos done vn deth ſhold haue ſight ayen ſo dremed iij nyghtis fewyng ¶and preſt let lede ſame hill com place martirid full deuoutly made ther praiers ̄ prayed god ̄ ſent thomas myght haue ſight ayen o praiers laid right hand vpō ſame place yt good man martired ̄ drope dry blod ſmale ſand cleued hand ther ſtriked eeyn anone thurgh might god ſent thomas lancaſtre ſight ayen thanked tho almyghty god ſent thomas ¶and whē miracle wos knowen among men pepull come thider eu er ſide knelid made ther praiers toumbe priorie pountfret praied holy merter ſocour help god herd ther prayer ¶alſo ther wos yong child drenched well toune poūtfret wos dede iij dais ̄ iij nyghtis men come ̄ laid deid child vpō ſent thomas tombe holy marter childe aroſe deth liue mony man ſaw ¶and alſo moch pepull wer owt ther mynd god hath ſent ther mynd ayen thurgh u er tu holy martir ¶and alſo god hath yeuen ther alſo crippils ther goyng ̄ crokid ther handis ther fete blind alſo ther ſight· ̄ mony ſeke folke ther helth diu er ſe malady loue good martir ¶alſo ther wos rich mā coundom gaſcoyn ̄ ſuch maladie right ſide roted fell away frō hī yt men myght ſe liu er hert ſo ſtonke vnneth men might cū ny hī wherfor frēdis wer hī wōd er ſori bot laſt god wold praid ſent thomas lancaſtre yt wold prai almyghty god priſoner ̄ behight go pountfret done ther pilgrimage thoht yt mertir ſent thomas cō annoynted ouer ſike body ¶and ther good man awoke wos hole fleſhe wos reſtorid ayen wos roted fallen away ¶for wich miracle good man frēdis loued god ſent thomas eu er mere ¶and good man come ī englōd ̄ toke wt hī iiij felowes come poūtfret vn yt holy mart er ̄ ther pilgrimage ̄ good man yt ſeke come thed er naked ſafe priue clothis ¶and whē done turned home ayen ī ther cūtre told miracle wher ſo eu er come ¶and alſo ij mē haue heled ther mormale thurgh helpe yt holy mart er though yt euell holdē incurabull ¶ whē ye ſpen ser herd yt god ſuch miracle holi mā nold leue ī man er wiſe▪ bot ſaid opēli yt grete hereſi ſuch vertu hī beleue ¶and ſir hugh ye ſpen ser ſon ſaw doyng anōe ſent meſſang er frō pountfret ther duellid ye kīg edward tho wos grauen scipton cauſe kīg ſhold vndo pilgrimage ¶and o ribaud meſſīger went toward kīg done meſſage come bi hill ther good mart er deth ̄ ſame place made ordure went toward kīg ſtrong flix come vpō come yorke tho ſhedde bowel foūdement ¶and ſir hugh ſpen ser herd tydīg ſomedele drad ̄ thought vn pilgrimage myght ony man er way ¶and anōe kīg went ſaid ſhuld gret ſkland er thurgh criſtīdom deth thomas lancaſtre ſuffred peple ther pilgrimage pountfret ̄ ſo coūcelled kīg cōmaūded cloſſe chirche dores pountfret wich chirche holi marter ſent thomas entered thus ayen fraūchiſes holy chirche ſo that· iiij yere aft er might pilgrime cū vn yt holy body ¶and encheſon monkis ſuffred men cū honour holy body ſent thomas martir thurgh cō cell ſir hugh ſpenſer ſon thurgh coūcell alſo maſt er robert baldoke fals piled clarke wos kīges chauncelar kyng conſentid ſhuld ſet ther wage let make wardeyns ou er ther good long time thurgh cōmā dement forſaid ſir hugh ſpen ser xiiij gaſcoynes well armed kept hill ther good man ſent thomas done vn deth ſo pilgrame might cum way ¶full well went haue take criſtis myght ̄ pouer gret boo miracle ſhewed marter sent thomas thurgh criſtyndom ¶and ſame tyme ye kyng made robert baldok fals piled clarke thurgh praier ſir hugh ſpen ser ſon chaūcelar englond ¶and ſame tyme caſtell walynford holdē ayens kyng thurgh priſoners wer within caſtell ſent thomas quarell lancaſtre ¶wherfor pepull c • ntre come toke caſtell vpon priſoners ¶wherfore sir iohn̄ goldington knyght ſir edmond beche priſoners ̄ ſquyer called roger walton· wer take ſent vn kyng pountfret ther werdone priſon forſaid roger ſent vn yorke ̄ ther draw honged ¶and anone aft er ſir roger mortimer wygmore brake tour london man er ¶the forſaid reg herd ſh̄uld draw ̄ honged londō morow ſent laurence day ̄ day held fair feſt tour londō ther wos ſir stephen ſegraue conſtable tour mōy gret men ¶and ſhuld ſope forſaid stephen ſent offiſers tour come ſopid ſhuld take ther leue ſquyer called stephen full priue wt forſaid rog er thurgh coūſell yaf ſuch drinke leſt ſlept ij dais ij nyghtis ī meyn tyme ſcappid away wat er yt ſay bi thamſe wēt ou er ſee held fraunce ¶wherfor kīg wos ſore annoyed tho put thee ſame stephen cōſtablerie ¶how quene iſabell went fraunce treten pee bytwen hir lord kyng englond king fraunce hir brother kyng went tho vn london ther thurgh cōcell ſir hugh ſpen ser fad er ̄ ſon maſter robert baldoke fals piled clarke chanceler let ſeiſe tho quenes landes ī handis ̄ alſo landis wer ſir edward ſon wer ſo put hir wage ayenſt man er reſō yt wos thurgh falſeneſſe ye ſpēſers ¶and whē kīg fraūce yt wos quene iſabelles brod er herd falſenes ſore annoyed ayens kīg englond ̄ fals coūcelers ¶wherfor ſent lett er kīg edward vnd er ſeal yt ſhuld cū ī fraūce c er ten day done homage ther ſomened hī ̄ elles ſhold leſe gaſcoyn ¶and ſo ordeyned englond thurgh kīg coūcell yt quene iſabell ſhold wend fraūce tret pee bitwen hir lord hir brother oliu er yngham ſhuld wēd gaſcoyn haue vij thouſand men ̄ mo armes ſeneſhall ̄ wardeyne gaſcoyn ſo wos orddyned yt quene iſabel wēt ou er ſe come fraūce wt hir went ſir aymer valāce erle pēbrok yt wos ther mordred ſodēli īpue ſege bot yt wos thurgh godis vēgeaunce wos ye iuſtices yt ꝯſentid ſent thomas deth lācaſtre ̄ wold neu er aft er repēte hī yt wikkid dede ̄ yt tim ſir oliu er ynghā went ou er ī gaſcoī moch harme ye kīg fraunca tho gat ayen kyng edward loſt moch ther ¶how kyng edward ſent ſir edward ſon eldeſt fraunce quene iſabell quart yere duelled ī fraū ce bot ſir edward hir eldeſt ſon axed leue tho wende fraunce ſpeke mother iſabell quene ¶and fader kyng graūted good ſaid go fair ſone goddis bliſſing myne thīke cū ayen haſtely thou may ¶and went ou er ſee ̄ come fraūce ¶and king fraūce vncle vnderfenge moch honour ſaid vn fair ſon ye welcō cauſe fad er come done homage duchie gnyhene aunceſtres wer wont yeue yt lordſhip hold heritage man er aūceſtres fore wher fore called duke gnyhenne ¶how kīg exiled quene iſabel edward heldeſt ſon kyng edward englond herd tell kyng fraunce yeue duchie gnyhen vn ſir edwarde ſon conſent ̄ ̄ ſone vnderfonge duchie become wonder wroth ̄ ſent ſone letter wyfe alſo ſhuld cum ayen englond haſt myght quene iſabell ſir edward hir ſone wer wōder ſore adrad kynges manace wroth principally falſenes ſpenſers father ̄ eke ſon commaundement wold cum ¶wherfore kyng edward wos full ſore annoyed ̄ let make crie londō quene iſabell edward hir eldeſt ſone come englond ſhuld bene holde enmys reame eke croun englōd ¶and thei nol̄d cum englond bot wer exiled moder hir ſon ¶when quene iſabell herd tidinges ſhe wos ſore adrad ſh̄ent thurgh fals congettyng ſpencers ¶and wēt knyghtys wer exiled englond ſent thomas cauſe lancaſtre yt ſay ſir rog er wigmore ſir willm truſſell ſir iohn̄ cromewell ̄ mōy od er good knyghtys ¶wherfor thei toke ther coūcell ̄ ordeyned amōges make mariege bitwen ye duke gnyhē ye kīgys ſon englōd ̄ erles dought er henaud yt nobul knyght name doughty ī time ¶and yt thīg myght brought ſtode trowyng wt help god help recou er ther heritage englōd wer wer put thurgh fals congettynges ſpen ser ¶how kyng edwar thurgh coūcell ſpen ser ſent douzeꝑs fraūce yt ſh̄uld help yt quene iſabell hir ſon ſir edward wer exiled fraūce kyng edward ̄ ſpen ser herd quene iſabell ſir edward hir ſon alied erle henaud wer exiled owt englond encheſon thomas lancaſtre wer ſo ſori thei wiſt done ¶wherfor ſir hugh ſpen ser ſon ſaid vn ſir hugh fadre man er wyſe ¶fadre curſed tim coūcell eu er ye conſentid quene iſabell ſhuld go vn fraunce trete accord bitwen kyng englond hir brother kyng fraūce councell tyme forſoth wit failed ¶for drede ſore leſt thurgh hir hir ſon ſhall ſh̄ent bot yf take better councell ¶now fair ſirres vnd er ſtond meruelus felonie falſhed th̄e ſpen ser ymagened caſt priuely let fill v barellis ferrors ſylu er tho ſoume amounted v thouſand pound ſent tho barrel ou er ſe priuely alien wos called arnold spayn brocour london ſhuld gone • uſepers fraunce ſhuld procuren ſpeke kyng fraunce quene iſabell hir ſon edward wer driuen exiled fraunce ¶and among thynges wer brought deth priuely myght ¶but almighty god wold ſo arnold wos high ſee wos take ſe land re met high ſee toke lad ther lord erle henaud ̄ moch ioye made taking ̄ laſt arnold priueli ſtole away fro then come london ¶and takīg od er thīges erle henaud ſaid quene iſabell dame maketh meri good chere ye richer ye wened haue bene take thes v barell full ſilu er wer ſent douzeꝑs fraūce kyll yow ſon edward thinketh haſteli wend englond taketh ye ſir iohan henaud brother vc mē armes mony thē fraūce ī whome ye haue grett truſt done ſcorne ¶and almyghti god graunte grace enmys ou er cum ¶the quene iſabell ſent tho thurgh henaud flaūdres hir ſaudiowrs ordeyned hir eu er day wend englond ayen ſo ſhe hir cō panye ſir edmond wodſtoke erle kent ſir edwardis brother englond ¶how kyng edward let kepe coſtes ſee ̄ let trie priſe men armes fote men thurgh englond kyng edward herd tell quene iſibell edward hir ſon wold cum englond gret pouer alien wer outlawed owt englond hir rebelneſſe ſore adrad put doūe leſe kyngdom ¶wherfor ordeyned kepe caſtels ī wale well englond vitales ther apparile let kepe riu er e alſo ſee coſtes wherof v porte toke kepe alſo ſee ¶and feſt decolaciō ſent iohn̄ bapteſt citizenis london ſent kyng porcheſtre hondreth men armes ¶and alſo commaū ded bi letter ordeyned yt eu er hondreth wapentake englond triours well men armmes o men fote ̄ ſhold bene put xx ſome ̄ hondreth ſome cōmāded tho men wer redy outeſe crie wer made purſue take alien come englond benomme land put owt kyngdom· ¶and ou er let crie thurgh patent eu er faire eu er marketh englond quene iſabell ſir edward eldeſt ſon erle kent wer take ſaufely keped wt man er harme vn doyng man er pepull come anone ſmyten ther hedis man er ranſome takyng ¶and man might bringe ſir roger hede mortimer wygmore ſhuld haue hondreth poūde monay trauell ¶and forthermore ordend patent cōmaūded make fire vpon eu er hyll beſide riu er e law cuntres make hie beekenes tymbbre ſo wer alien come vn land nyght men ſhuld tend bekenes contre might warned cum mete ther enmys tyme died ſir roger mortimer vncle tour london ¶how quene iſabell ſir edward duke gnyhene ſon com lond herewich quene iſabell ſir edward hir ſone duke gnyhenne ſir edward wodſtoke erle kent ſir iohan erles brother henaud ther company drad thee manace kyng ne traitours truſtid goddis grace ̄ com vn herewich ſauthfolke xxiiij day septembre yere grace mcccxxvi quene ̄ ſir edward hir ſon ſent lettres maire ̄ cōmmalte londō requiring ſhuld helpyng quarell ̄ cauſa yt begonne ſay diſtroy tratours ream bot none anſuer ſent ayen wherfore quene ſyr edward hir ſon ſentē patent lett er vnd er ther ſeales tenour wich lett er foloweth man er ¶iſabell thee grace god quene englond lady irland countes pountyf edward eldeſt ſon kyng englond duke gnyhen erle cheſtre pauntif mouſtroill ye maire cominalte cite london ſendeth gretyng moch haue tyme ſent yow lett er cū land good aray ī good man er honour profet holy chirche right dere lord kīg reame oure myght pouer kepe maynten good folkis forſaid reame ar holden done ¶and vpon pray ye wold helpīg v ī moch ye may ī quarell comune profet forſaid reame haue tyme none anſuer forſaid lettres ne know partie ¶wherfor ſend ayen pray charge ye bere ſo ayens v haue cauſe greue bot ye bene vn v helpyng wayes ye may may knowe wyte ye well certayn tho yt comen v reame thynke done thyng thyng ſhall commune ꝓfet reame bot onli diſtroy hugh ſpen ser enmy ̄ enmy te ream ye well knowith ¶wherfor pray charge faith ye owe lord kīg v vpon ye ſhull mow forfet agayn v ſaid hugh ſpen ser enmy come pouer ye haſteli ben takyn ſaufli keped vn till haue ordeyned wyll ye leue man er wyſe ye deſire honor profit v ream ¶vnd er ſtondyn ye well ye doo prayer commandemēt holdē vn alſo ye ſhall get worſhip profet yf ye ſend v haſtely anſuer ayen baldok vi day october ¶which letter erly dawyng day ſent denis wos takked vpon new croſſe chepe mony copy ſame letter wer tacked vpō wyndowes doris vpon place cite london men paſſing way myght ſee rede ¶and ſame tyme kyng edward london tour mete ¶and ameſſinger come hall ſaid quene iſabell wos comen land herewich hath brought hir companie ſir iohn̄ henaud ̄ men armes without nombre ¶and word ſir hugh ſpenſer fadre ſpake thus vn kyng ſaid moſt worſhipfull lord king englond make good chere c er tanly ben̄ ¶the kyng ſaw word comfortable yit full ſorowfull ̄ penſife ī hert ¶and kīg fully eten bot ther come hall meſſinger ſaid yt quene iſabell ariued herewich beſide yepſwyche ſouthfolke ¶sir hugh ſpen ser fadre ſpake meſſinger ſaid tell ſoth good faith meſſinger fair frende ſhe come wt gret ſtrength ¶now ſertis ſir ſoth ſay ſhe ne hath hir componye vij houndreth men armes ¶and wt word ſir hugh ſpen ser fad er cried high vois ̄ ſaid ala ala bene betrayed c er ti ſo litil pouer ſhe neu er comen land folke lond wer vn hir conſent ¶and therfor aft er mete token ther coū cell went toward wale arere walſhmen ayenſt quene iſabell edward hir ſone fight ſo wer purpoſed eu er ychone ¶how maſter walt er stapilton biſſhop exceſtre kynges treſorer wos heded london ſame tyme kyng edward wos ſore adrad leſt men london wold yeld vn quene iſabel hir ſon edward ¶wherfor ſet maſt er walt ſtapiltō treſorer wardeyn keper cite londō wt maire ¶and ſo come gyldehall london axid keyes yates cite thurgh vertu ſtrength cōmiſſion wold haue kepyng cite comuners anſuered ſaid yt wold kepe cite honor kyng edward iſabell quene duke kynges ſon ony biſſhop wos tho ſore annoyed ſwore othes ſhuld abie anone kyng edward wer comen wale ¶and communers anone cite toke biſſhop ̄ lad myddes ye chepe ther ſmyten hede ſet hede right hand ¶and heded ij ſquyers held biſſh̄op called willm waile biſſhopis nepheu ¶and called iohan padyngton alſo toke burgeis london wos called iohn̄ marchall wos ſir hugh ſpen ser aſpie fader ſmoten hede alſo ¶and ī ſame tyme biſſhoop ī londō fair tour ī makīg ī cloſe vpō riu er thameſe yt wos tempull barre failed ſtone make ther end wher cōmaūded men go chirche frere carmes ther toke ſtone make ther touer moch ſand ̄ mort old robous wos left ¶and diſpite yt biſſhop done vn holy chirche ij ſquyers wer beried ſand o though bene houndes ¶and ther lay xi wekis till quene iſabell ſent hir lettres comuners praid yt wold ſuffre ̄ graūte yt biſſhop myght take place beried exceſtre owne chirche ¶and ſo ij ſquyers wer beried ſent clementis chirch tempull barre ̄ wos wōd er though biſſhop died euell deth ¶for couetous mā ̄ wt hī merci euell coūcelled kīg ¶and ſone aftar arnold ſpayn taken aſſentant haue lad vm pound ſiluer ī v bareles ferriers vn ye douzeꝑs fraunce help haſt quene iſabell hir deth edward hir ſon alſo arnold wos put deth owt cite london ¶how kyng edward ſir hugh ſpenſer erle arundell wer taken kyng edward ſent maſter walter stapilton treſorer london kepe cite vn ayen quene iſabell wyfe ayens edward ſone anone hī ſelf toke ſir hugh ſpenſer ſon ſir iohan erle arundell maſter robert baldoke chancelar fals piled preſt token ther way toward briſtow ¶and ther kyng abode litell tyme made ſir hugh ſpen ser fad er coneſtable keꝑ caſtell ¶and kyng thatt ſpen ser went ſhip ̄ ſailed toward wale toke leue ſtiward ne none kingꝭ houſold ̄ went ou er ī wale arere walſhmen ayen dame iſabell quene thee duke hir ſon erle kent ̄ ſir iohan henaud thei went ̄ purſued aft er ther pouer encreſid eu er day laſt kyng taken vpon hill wale ſir hugh thee ſpen ser ſon ſide ſame hill fals pilede clarke maſter robert baldoke ther faſt beſides ̄ wer brought ayen englond almighti god wold ¶and kyng ſelf put ſauf kepyng caſtell kemlworth hī kept ſir hēri yt ſent thomas brod er lancaſtre ¶and ſir hugh fad er come put ī quenes grace ſir edward hir ſun duke gnyhenne ¶but ſir hugh thee ſpen ser aft er tyme taken nold neu er ete man er mete ne drinke man er drinke frō wiſt haue mercy ſauf dede ¶and quene hir counſell tho ordeyned ſhuld haue deth londō bot ſo febull hys moch faſtyng yt ny dede therfor wos ordend yt ſhuld haue iugemet herford ̄ place toure hood wos take hede alſo robert baldoke wos fals piled clarkd kynges chauncelare men ſet vpon ther hedis chappelettis ſharpe netteles two ſquyers blew ther eres ij gret bugle horne vpō tho ij priſoners men might ther blowyng horne myle • ¶and symond ridyng kyngꝭ marchall bare ther armes vpō ſpere reu er ſed ī tokē yt ſh̄uld vndone eu er ¶and vpō morew ſir hugh ſpen ser ſone dampned deth wos draw honged ̄ heded ̄ bowel takin body brent thatt quartired ̄ iiij quarter wer ſent iiij tounes englond hede ſent london brigge ¶and simond encheſon diſpiſed quene iſabell draw honged ſtage made myddeſt forſaid ſir hugh galewes ¶and ſame day litell then wos ſir iohn̄ arū dell beheded encheſon wos ſir hugh ſpen ser councelers ¶and anōe aft er wos ſir hugh ſpen ser fad er honged draw heded briſtow ̄ aft er honged ayen bi armes wt ij ſtrong rope iiij· day aft er hewen peces houndes eten encheſon kyng yeffen erledom wyncheſtre hede wos ſent thider ̄ put vpō ſpere ¶and fals baldoke wos ſent londō ̄ ther died ī priſon amonges thefes men hī reuerens wold done vn hound ̄ ſo died traitours englond bliſſed almyghty god ¶and wos wōder thurgh ther councell good erle thomas lancaſtre wos deth held thomas lancaſtre thurgh traitours wer vndone ther heires diſherred ¶hw kīg edward put doūe dignite take frō anone done quene iſabel edward hir ſone grett lordis englond one aſſent ſent kīg edward caſtell kenilworth ther kepyng vnder ward ſir iohan hachī wos biſſhop ely ̄ ſir iohan percy baroun encheſon ſhuld ordeyn parlament certain place england rodreſſe ̄ amend ſtate reame ¶and kyng edward anſuerd ſaid lordis quod ye ſee full well lo haueth ſeal yef yow pouer ordeyn parlament wher yt ye ¶and toke ther leue come ayen baron englond ¶and kīges patent thyng ſhewed lordis ¶and tho ordeyned parlamēt ſhuld weſtmynſtre vtas ſent hillarie ¶and gret lordis englond let ordeyn ther ayens yt tyme parlament ſhuld ¶and wich day parlament wos kīg wold cum ther man er thyng ſet ſelf aſſigned ¶and notheles baron ſent vn tyme ſuore godis ſoule nold cū ther fote wherfore wos ordeyned gret lordis englōd yt ſhuld longer kyng depoſid ſaid wold croune edward ſone elder king yt wos ye duke gnyhenne ſent tydyng vn kyng ther yt ward vnder ſir iohan erle garen ſir iohan bothun biſſhopp ely ſir henri percy barone ſir willm truſſell knyght wos erle ſir thomas lancaſter yeld vp ther homage vn englond ¶and ſir willm truſſell ſaid thes wordis sir edward encheſon ye haue traied pepull englond haue vndone mony gret lordis englond outen cauſe ye ſhall depoſid ye withſtond thanked god ¶and alſo encheſon ye wold cū ꝑlamēt ye ordeyned weſtmynſtre lett er patent contend tret lege men kyng ſh̄uld ¶and therfore thurgh comuns aſſent ̄ lordis englond tell vn yow thes wordis ye ſhall vnder ſtond ſir baron englond aſſent ye kyng englond vtterly haue put yow rialte eu er ¶and biſſhop ely ſaid tho kyng ¶sir edward heri yeld vp feaute homage erchebiſſhoppis biſſhoppis englond clerge ¶tho ſaid ſir iohan erle garenne ſir edward yeld vp vn yow feaute homage ̄ erles englond ¶and ſir hēri percy yaf vp alſo ther homage baron englond ¶and tho ſaid ſir willm truſſell yeld vp vn ſir myne homage alſo knyghtes englond holden ſeriauntre man er thyng ¶so day aft er ward ye ſhall clamed kyng nother kyng holde ¶but frō thys tyme afterward ye ſhall bene holden ſinguler man pepull ſo went then london ther lordis englond abode ſir edward abade priſonne good kepīg wos day conu er ſion ſent paule thee xx yere regne ¶of ꝓphecie merlin declarid kīg edward ſone kyng edward friſt kyng edward ꝓphecied merlin ſaid ther ſhuld cum goot carre ſhuld haue horn ſilu er berd white ſnow▪ doppe ſh̄uld cum noſethriles ſhuld betoken moch harme hounger dethe pepull ̄ gret loſſe land begynnyng regne ſhuld haūted moch lechorie ¶and ſaid ſoth ala tyme kyng edward kyng edward ſon bonre carnariuan wale ſoth horne ſylu er berd white o ſnow made prince walis moche yaf hī riot ̄ folie ¶and ſoth ſaid merlin prophecie ther ſhulde cum noſe doppe tyme gret honger among poer pepull ſtrong deth among riche died ſtrange land moch ſorow ̄ ī ſcotland aft er ward loſt ſcotland gaſcoyn while ſelf wos kīg ther wos moch lechori haūted ¶and alſo merlin told ſaid goot ſh̄uld ſeche flour lyfe deth ſaid ſoth ſpouſed iſabell kynges ſuſtre fraunce ¶and tyme merlin ſaid thei ſhuld made brigges folke vpō diches ſe well ſeyn banokkeſ borne ſcotland whan diſcomfited ther ſcottis ¶and merlin told alſo ſtones ſhuld fall caſtels mony tounes ſhuld made playn ¶and ſaid ſoth whan kyng edward wos diſcomfited ſcotland come tho ſouthward ſcottis beſeged tho caſtels moch harme brend tounes vn herd erthe ¶and aft er ward merlin told egle ſhuld cum cornwaill ſhold haue fetherris gold pride ſhuld haue peir ſhuld deſpiſe lordis blod aft er ſhuld die thurgh bere gauſich propheci full wel know found ſoth ¶for egle vnderſtond ſir pers ganaſton tho wos erle cornewaill wonder proud man diſpiſed baronage englōd aft er ward heded gauſich thurgh erle lancaſtre thurgh erle werwik ¶and merlin told ī tyme ſholde ſeme bere ſhuld brenne bataill ſh̄old vpon arme ſee feld araied like ſh̄eld wher ſhuld die mony whit hedis ¶and ſaid ſoth bi brennīg bere betokened gret dred thurgh cuttyng ſwerdis bataill miton ther come ſcottis maner ſheld man er wynge ſlew vpō ſwale men religion preſtis ̄ ſeculers wherfore scottis called bataill diſpite engliſhmē white bataill ¶and aft er merlī ſaid yt ye forſaid bere ſh̄uld goot moch harme ſhuld vpon ſouthweſt alſo vpon blod ſaid alſo goot ſhuld leſe mich dele land till tyme ſhame ſhuld ou er cum ſhuld cloth lyon ſkyn ̄ ſhuld wyn ayen loſt thurgh pepull ſh̄uld cum northweſt ſhold make bene adrad venge vpon enmys thurgh councell ij owles friſt ſh̄old ꝑell vndone ¶and tho two owles ſhuld wend ou er ſee ſtrange land ther ſhuld duell vn till c er tan time ̄ aft er ſh̄ uld cum ī englōd ayen ¶and tho two owles ſhuld moch harme vn mōy ̄ yt ſhold cōcell goot meue ayens foreſaid bere ¶and ye got owles ſhold cū arme ſee borton vp trent ̄ ſhuld wend ou er ̄ yt drede ye bere ſhold fle wt swan ī cōpanye buri toward north thurgh vnkind outpul̄ter swan ſhall ſlayn ſorow bere ſhuld ſlayn full ny owne neſt ſh̄old ſtond vpō poūtfret vpon ſonne ſhall ſhed bemes mony folke ſhall ſeke vertu ſaid ſoth good erle thomas lancaſtre borne northweſt ̄ coſin kīg vncle ſon ¶and law made kyng leſe moch land wich purcheſed wilfulli till laſt kyng ther toke ſhame ſelf filled wyth cruelte ¶and gat ayen yt loſt moch thurgh folke let aſſemble northweſt yt made adrad venged baron thurgh coūcell ſir hugh ſpen ser fadre ſir hugh ſon fore wer owt lawed englond ther wikkednes ¶bot afterward cume ayen engloed ſir hugh ſpen ser fadre fraunce ſo moch cōceled kyng ſhuld vpon thomas lancaſtre ¶so kyng ſpenſers erle arundell ther pouer met thomas lancaſtre burton vpon trent ther diſcomfited ſir humfry erle herford wos companye ¶and aft er fled forſaid thomas humfrey ther company burbruge ſir andrew erkela called vnkind outpulter ¶and alſo ſir symondward erle yorke come mete thomas lancaſtre huge companye ther diſcomfited ̄ ſcomfiture erle herford wos ſlayn vpō bruge couherdly ſpere foundement erle thomas wos take lad vn paūtfret tho heded beſide caſtell aft er ward mony men ſought miracle god ¶and tyme merlī ſaid ſorow harme ſhuld die pepull land wherfore mony landis ſhuld vpō bolder ¶and ſaid ſoth encheſon baron wer done deth ſent thomas quarell lancaſtre pepull mony landis become bold meue vpō kyng ther blod wos turned mōy nacions ¶and aft er ward merlin told ̄ ſaid forſaid owles ſhuld moch harme vn floor life deth ſhuld bring hir moch diſeſe ſo yt ſhe ſh̄uld wēd ou er ſe ī fraū ce make pee ye flour deliſe ̄ ther ſhuld bide till tyme hir ſede ſhuld cum ſech hir tho ſh̄uld biden bothe till tyme ſhuld cloth grace ̄ tho two owles ſhe ſhold ſeke ̄ put vn pytuus deth ꝓphecie wos well know full ſoth ¶for ſir hugh ſpen ser fadre ſir hugh ſone moch ſorow perſecucion vn quene iſabell thurgh procurment hir lord kyng ¶so ordeyned amonges ſhe put vn hir wage ſay xx ſh̄ylling day ¶wherfor kyng fraūce hir brother ſore annoyed ſent englond letter vn kyng edward ſhold come vn hys ꝑlament paris fraunce kyng edward ſore adrade cum ther wened haue bene areſted till made amendis treſpaſe ſir hugh ſpenſer fadre ſone done harme done vn thee quene iſabell ſuſtre ¶wherfor thurgh hir ordeynaunce ̄ conſent ſpen ser quene iſabell went ou er ſe ī fraūce make accorde bitwen kyng edward kīg fraūce hir brother ¶and ther duel̄led ſhe fraūce till edward hir eldeſt ſon come hir ſech ̄ ſo duelled ther till yt aliance made bitwen gentill erle henaud wt ther help might deſtroi ̄ ou er cū venym ̄ falſenes ſpenſers yt ſir edward ſhuld ſpouſe dame philip worſſhipfull lady ̄ erles dought er henaud ¶wherfor quene iſabell ̄ ſir edward hir ſon ſir edward wodſtoke kynges brother englond ſir iohn̄ henaud ̄ ſir roger mortimer wigmore ſir thomas rocelin ſir iohn̄ crōwell ſir willm truſſell mony liaunce gētill erle thomas lancaſtre wer exiled englond quaril wer diſherited ther landis ordeyned gret pouer ariued herewich ſouthfolke ¶and ſone aft er purſued ſpen ser till wer takyn put vn ſpitouſe deth ſaid ther company • alſo gret falſenes yt thei kīg edward pepull ¶and merlin ſaid alſo goot ſh̄uld put īto gret diſeſe gret anguyſh ̄ gret ſorow ſh̄uld lede lyfe ¶and ſaid ſoth aftir tyme kyng edward wos take put ward till ſpenſers wer put vn deth ¶and alſo encheſon wold cum vn ꝑlament london ordened aſſigned himſelf baronage alſo wold gou er ne rule pepull ne ream king ſhold done ¶wherfore ſum baron englond come ̄ yeld vp ther hamages vn ream day ꝯu er ſion ſent paule yere regne xx ̄ put rialte eu er eu er leued lyfe afterward moch ſorow anguyſſh lodewicus fourth wos emprour aft er henri iiij yere lodewic wos duke banare diſpiſed coronacion pope wherfore pope depoſit moch labour mony ꝑell aft er trubled gretly vnite holy chirch ̄ wos choſin ayens frederik duke auſtrich ou er come duke boid rebelion end ̄ gret parell ſoule laſt karolus wos choſin ayens wich p̄uayled ſodenly lodewik fell doūe horſe ̄ deceſſed iohan maundevill doctor feſike knyght borne wos englond bout tyme ̄ made meruelus pilgrimage went almoſt bowt world wrot dedis iij langages deceſid wos buried ſent albons benedictus xxij wos pope aft er iohn̄ vij yere man wos monke youth wos good conu er ſacion doctor diuinite wē wos made pope reformed ordir ſent benet thyng yt neceſſari wos hard man graūt benefice leſt graūted vnconyng man made decretall wich began benedictus deus donis ſuis wos veray reame graūtid chartre ſtedfaſt pee yt wold axe ¶and ſir iohn̄ henaud ̄ cōpanye toke ther leue ye kīg ̄ lordis reame turned home ther cōtre ayen eche full rich yeftes eu er ych mā wos value eſtate ¶and tho wos englond ī pee ̄ ī reſt ̄ gret loue bitwene kīg lordis comynly engliſh men ſaid amōges deuell dede treſour kīg fadre treſour ſpen ser fadre ſon erle arundell ̄ maſter robert baldok yt wos kinges chancelar deꝑtid quene iſabellis ordenaunce sir roger mortimer wigmore ſo kyng nothyng ther hir ̄ hir deliu er ance ne ther landis aft er ward ye ſhall ¶how kīg edward wēt ſtanthop mete lancaſtre brother ¶and ſo erle lancaſtre ̄ leiceſtre ̄ eke ſtiward englond brother wos tyme ſir edward wos kīg edwardis fadre made ſorow end becauſe myght ſpeke wyfe ne wt ſone wherfor wos ī moch miſchief though wer ſo wos lad ̄ ruled fals councell yit wos kyng edwardis ſo ne called edward long ſchankis ̄ come worthieſt blode world ¶and whome wos woned yeue gret yeftes ̄ large wer moſt p̄ue wt kīg ſon ̄ wer enmys bi nyght bi day ̄ procurid make debate cōtake bytwen hī ſon ̄ iſabell wife bot frere prechours hī wer good frēdis eu er caſt bi nyght ̄ bi day myght bring hī priſō ¶and amōg ther cōpany yt freris priueli brought ther wos frere called dunhened ̄ ordeyned gadred gret cōpanye folke kepe yt nede frer wos take put ī caſtel poūfret ther died priſon ¶and ſir henri erle lancaſtre kinges fadre ī keping thurgh cōmandemēt kīg deliu er ed edward kīges fad er bi endētur ſir thomas berkeley ſo ſir iohn̄ mautreus ̄ led caſtell kemlworth caſtyll berkeley kept ther ſaufly ¶and eſtren next coronaciō kīg ordyned huge hoſt fight ayens ſcottis ſir iohn̄ ye erles brother heenaud frō yond ſe come help kyng edwarde brought hī vij houdreth men armes ariued dou er leue go forth till come yorke ther yt thee kyng abode ¶and ſcottis come thed er kyng make pee accorde· accordement laſted bitwein tham bot litell tyme ¶and tyme engliſſhmen wer clothed cote ̄ hodes hod witles gay cote gracelas make englond thriftles ī trinite day next began ꝯtake cite yorke bitwen engliſſhmen henaudires debate wer kylled erledom nycholl mordred lxxx wer buried vnder ſtone ſent parke ſtanhope turned ayen ſcotland tyme ſcottis aſſembled ther pouer comen englond kylled robbed thatt myght take alſo brennet diſtroid north cuntre thurgh till come vn parke ſtanhope wyredall ther scottis held buſchement ¶but kyng herd thurgh certayn aſpies wher scottis wer anone right hoſt beſeged within forſaid parke ſo ſcottit wiſt wher gone vn ther harmis abiden parke xv day ̄ vitales failed eu er ſide ſo wer gretli appaired ther body ¶and ſith brut come fyrſt bretan vn tym wos ther neu er ſeyn ſo fair hoſt engliſſhmen lyens men fote wich ordeyned fight ſcottis thurgh eggyng ſir henri erle lancaſtre ſir iohan henaude wold haue gone ou er wat er haue foughten ſcottis ¶but ſir roger mortimer cō ſentid ther priuely takyn mede ſcottis thē help myght wend away ayen ther cuntre ¶and ſame mortimer councelled ſo moch thomas brotherton erle marſhall kyng edwardis vncle ferſaid thomas ſhuld aſſembull tyme vn ſcottis aſſentid wiſt doyng bitwene ſcottis forſaid mortimer ¶and encheſon marſhall englond ꝑteyned eu er vauntward ſent haſteli erle lancaſtre ſir iohan henaud ſhuld fight scottis preiudice harmyng fee ſhuld ſtond ther perrill ¶and forſaid erle marſhall al araied tratourſly kīg edward diſſaued ̄ merueluſly ̄ boldly ſcottis iamys douglas cc men armes riden thurgh aut hoſt gyng edward ſame nyght ſcottis wer aſcaped toward ther cuntre aboue ſaid till com kynges ¶wherfor ēpror made crie rome ordeyned od er pope yt hight nycholas yt wos frere mynor yt ayens right holy chirch ¶wherfor wos curſed pouer od er pope ſone wos leid encheſō ſuche meruellis wer ſeyn ſtond lady wife come thing ny ye wold hir ſtrangle kyll alſo ye wold lord ſon ſame ¶tho anſuered ſimple chere ala ala ī priſon god hit wote thought neu er wold wer dede ſo wold god wer wer ſorow wos go bedde kīg went vn bed ̄ lay ſlept faſt king lay ſlept ye tratourys fals ſworne ayens ther homage ther feaute come priueli kynges chambre ̄ ther company laid huge tabull vpō wombe men preſſed ſir hēri erle lancaſtre put ī hidīg dred quene ſhe loued wonder moch prayed vn kyng ſame thomas myght exiled englond ¶and nobull erle ſir henri lancaſtre oft tymys herd comune clamor engliſhmē diſeſe wer done englōd alſo diuerſe wronges wer done among comune pepull wich kyng bare blame wrong bot full yong tender age thought good man done way ſlake ſklandre kynges parſon myght maner wiſe alſo men londō made ther othe maynten ſame quarell ¶and ther cauſe wos kyng ſhuld hold houſe meny kyng ought done haue riallti yt quene iſabell ſhuld deliu er hir hand kynges hād man er lordſhippis rentis tounes caſtels apꝑtened vn croune englond quenes hir medle none thyng ¶and alſo ſir rog er mortimer ſhuld duell vpon landis wich landis holpe diſherited moch pepull ſo comune pepull wer diſtroyd thurgh wrongfull takyng ¶and alſo enquere ̄ thee king betraied falſly diſceyued stanhop thurgh whois councell scottis went way nyght thee kyng ¶and alſo ̄ thurgh who coūcell ordenaunce made kynges coronacion put doune ſai kyng amendement helpyng reame honour ſhuld gou er ned ruled xij greteſt ̄ wiſeſt lordis reame ̄ ſh̄uld thyng ben graunted ne done ſaid wich couenantis maliciuſli wer put doūe fro kīg werfor moni harmes ſhames reꝓues haue falle kyng ream vnderſtond moch edward ſum tyme kyng englon ordeyned aſſent cominalte playn ꝑlamēt vnd er warde ̄ gou er naunce henri erle mordred who deth aroſe ſclandre thurgh criſtendō done ¶and alſo treſour ſir edward carnariuan left ī mōy place englond wale wer waſted borne away without kyng edward ſon deſtruccion folke alſo thurgh who councell kyng yaf vp kīgdō ſcotland wich reame kynges anceſtres full ſore trauaill ſo mony nobull man ther right ̄ deliu er ed vn dauid wos robert brus ſon right right reame world wiſt ¶and alſo bi chartres remembrance yt ye right scotland wer take treſorie taken vn ſcottis ye kynges enmys diſherityng hys ſucceſſours gret harme vn liege ̄ gret reproue vn engliſſhmen eu er ¶alſo wherfor dame iohana tour kynges ſuſtre edward wos diſꝑaged marid vn dauid yt wos robert brus ſon yt traitour enmye vn englond ̄ thurgh who councell ſhe wos take enmys handis englond ¶and meyn good erle henri lancaſtre companie toke councell thes pointes aboue ſaid myght amendid vn worſſhip kīg ̄ ꝓfet ̄ ꝓfite alſo liege ¶and quene iſabell thurgh coniecting ſotelti alſo mortimer let ordeyn parlament saliſberi ¶and yt ſame ꝑlamēt mortimer made erle march ayenſt baron englōd preiudice kyng ̄ croune ̄ ſir iohn̄ eltham kyngꝭ brother gurt ſwerd cornwaill tho wos called erle cornewaill eu er quene iſabell ſo moch pracurid ayens hir ſon kyng ſhe ward forſaid ſir edward ̄ landis· ¶and ꝑlament erle lancaſtre wold cum ordeyned al pouer ayens quene iſabell mortimer men londō ordened v hondreth men armes ¶whē quene iſabell wyſt doyng ſhe ſwore god bi name full angrely euell tyme thought vpō tho pointes ¶tho ſent quene iſabell mortimer aft er ther retene ̄ kynges retenue ſo ordeyned amonge theem huge hoſt councelled kyng ſo yt vpō nyght riden xxiij myle toward bedford • erle lancaſtre wos ꝯpani thought haue hī deſtroied yt nyght ſhe rode bi ſide king hir ſon knyght armed dred deth ¶and done kyng vnd er ſtond yt erle henri lancaſtre companie wold haue diſtroid kyng coūcell euer wherfor kīg wos ſomdele towardis hī heuy annyed ¶whan erle marſhall erle kent kīges brod er herd tyding riden ſo ī meſſage bitwen king graūted pee erle henri lancaſtre c er tan raū ſone xim pound yt wos neu er paied aft er ward ¶and thes wer lordis held ſir henri lancaſtre ſir henri beamōt ſir fouke fitzwaren ſir thomas rocelyn ſir willm truſſell ſir thomas wyther hondreth knyggtis mo yt wer concentid tho wer exiled thurgh coūcell quene iſabell ̄ mortimer mortimer weited haue ther landis myght thurgh ony maner ꝯiecting couetous ̄ moch ̄ wos gret pitte ¶how kyng edward went ou er ſee homage vn kyng fraūce duchie gnyhen wos long aft er kyng fraunce thurgh cō cell douſepe ſent kyng edward englond ſhuld cume paris done homage reſon wold duchie gnyhen ¶and ſo thurgh counſell lordis englond kyng edward went ou er ſee aſcencion tide come vn paris thrid yere regne homage vn kyng fraūce kyng vnd er fenge homage made hī moch ioye worſſhip ¶but kīg edward made homage haſteli ſent englōd thurgh quene iſabell moder ̄ anone haſtely come ayen englond vpon witſonday takyng leue kīg fraūce wherfore wos wond er wroth ¶how ſir roger mortimer bare proudly ̄ ſo hie ſhall ye ſir roger mortimer wygmore diſſired couyted high ſtate ſo yt kyng graunted called erle marche thurgh lordſhip ¶and become ſo proud ſo hauteyne wold leſe forſake name anceſtres euer ¶and encheſon let call erle marche none comuns englond durſt call bi name name called ſo thurgh kyngꝭ crie men ſhuld call erle marche ¶and mortimer bare ſo hauteyne ̄ ſo proud wond er wit alſo diſgiſed hī wt wond er rich clothes man er reſon ſhapping wering wher engliſſhmen gret wond er ̄ whot maner myght contreue find ſuch man er pride ſaid amō ge comenli prid ſh̄old long endure ¶and ſame tyme ſir geffrey mortimer yong yt mortimer ſon let call kyng folie ſo befell aft er ward dede wos ſo full pride ̄ writchedneſſe held roū de tabull wale men thid er come contrefete doīg ̄ man er kyng arthur tabull bot openli failed nobull kyng arthur wos moſt worthy lord renoune yt world tyme yit come neu er none ſuch aft er al nobull knyghtis criſtendome dede armes aſayed duellid kyng arthur ̄ held ther lord ſoferen ¶and wos well ſayn ꝯquered bataill roman wos called froll ̄ get reame fraūce kylled handis ¶and alſo faught geant wos called dinabus kylled raueſſhed fair eleyn wos kyng hocles nece kyng litell bretan ¶and aft er ward kylled bataill emprour rome wos called lucie aſſembled ayens king arthur fight ſo moch pepull romās phethis ſariſens yt man coud nōbre ̄ diſcomfited ſtori telleth ¶and ye ſame tyme cōmune loo ſprong englōd thurgh coniecting ordinaūce freres prechours ſir edward carnariuan wos kyng edward fadre geeſt telleth ſaid liue caſtell corf wherfor cōmyns moſt englond wer ſorow ī dred wherfor wer ſo wiſt traitourſly mortimer done mordrid ¶how edmōd wodſtok yt wos erle kent kinges brother edward carnariuan heded wyncheſtre vpō tyme befell ſo ſir edmond wodſtoke erle kent ſpake vn pope iohan xxij auinion ſaid almyght good oft tymes done thomas loue lancaſtre mony gret miraclls mony men woman wer thurgh diu er ſe malady undone vn world thurgh praier wer brought vn ther hel̄th ¶and ſo ſir edmond praied pope herteli wold graūte grace yt forſaid thomas myght tranſlatid pope ſaid nay ſhuld tranſlatid vn tyme wer bett er c er tefied clargie englond ſeyn ther obedēce thyng god done loue thomas lancaſtre ſuggeſtion forſaid edmōd erle kent vn made ¶and whan edmond ſaw myght ſpede purpoſe tochyng tranſlacion praied coūcell toching ſir edward carnariuan brod er ſaid long gone wos kyng englond thīg might beſt done toching deliu er ance ſith comune fame thurgh englōd liue hole ̄ ſauf ¶whan pope herd hī tell ſir edward liue cōmaūded erle vpō beniſon ſh̄uld help wt pouer yt myght yt wer deliu er ed priſun ſ • ue body ī man er yt might bring thīg end aſſoyled hī cōpani pena culpa tho holp deliu er ance ¶tho toke edmōd wodſtoke leue pope come ayen ī englōd whā ſir edmond wos comē ſū frere precheurs come ̄ ſaid yt ſir edward brod er yit wos liue ī caſtell corf vnder kepīg sir thomas gurnay ¶tho ſped forſaid edmōd faſt o might till come caſtell corf ̄ queynted hī ̄ ſpak ſo fair wt iohn̄ dauerell yt ꝯſtable ſame caſtell yaf rich yeftes haue acqueyntance knaw coūcell ¶and thus befell forſaid ſir edmōd praied ſpecially tell priuely lord brother ſir edward leued wer dede wer liue praied ons haue ſight ¶and ſir iohan dauerill high herted man full curage ̄ anſuerid ſhortely vn ſir edmond ſad ſir edward brother helth vnder kepyng durſt ſhew vn man ſith defended kynges half edward edwardis ſon carnariuan alſo thurgh commaundement quene iſabell kynges modre ̄ ſir rog er mortimer ſh̄uld ſhew body vn maner man world ſauf vn vpon leſyng life limme ̄ diſherityng heiris eu er ¶but fals traitour falſly lied ward wos take then lad vn caſtell berkeley thurgh ſir thomas gurnay thurgh ꝯmaūdemēt mortimer til wos dede ſaid ſir edmōd wodſtoke wiſt nothyng edward brod er dede wher vpon toke lettre vn kīg edward brod er worthi lord ¶and vnderfeng letter hight meſſage man er faill ſir edmōd toke leue forſaid iohn̄ wēt ī ꝯtre lordſhip ī kent ther ¶and anone ſame iohn̄ wiſt yt ſir edmond wos gone ī kent lordſhip anone went ī haſt myght fro caſtell corf comen vn ſir roger mortimer toke letter ſir edmōd wodſtoke erle kent takē cloſed ̄ enſeled ſeale ¶and wē ſir rog er mortimer vnd er feng letter vncloſid ̄ ſaw cōteyned therī ̄ began rede wherof begynnyng wos ¶worſhippes reu er en brother legeaunce ſubieccion sir knyght worſſhipfull dere brod er pleſe pray hertely yt ye good cōforth ſhall ſo ordeyn ye ſhall cum priſon deliu er ed diſeſe ye vnd er ſtondeth gret lordſhip haue aſſentant almoſt ye gret lordis englond ther apparaill ſai wt armure wt treſour nombre maynten yor quarell ſo ferforth ye ſhall kyng ayen ye wer haue ſuorne vpon boke ̄ well prelatis erles baron ¶when ſir roger mortimer ſaw vnd er ſtode myght thee ſtrength lettre anone hert wroth gan boll euel hert bare toward ſir edmond wodſtoke erle kent haſt myght went vn dame iſabell quene wos kīges mod er ̄ ſhewed hir ſir edwardes lettre purpoſe coniected ordeynde put doune kyng edward wyndeſore hir ſon rialte kyngdom ¶now certis ſir rog er qd ſhe hath ſir edmond done ſo fadre ſoule quod ſhe bene therof auenged god graunte life ſhorte tyme ¶and quene iſabell went vn ye kyng edward hir ſon ther thee ꝑlament wyncheſtre haue mende wronges treſpaces doon among pepull reame ¶and tho toke ſhe ſhewed letter ſir edmond wodſtoke erle kent made enſeled ſeale bad vpon hir benyſon ſh̄uld venged vpon edmond vpon dedely enmye ¶tho quene ſo wroth toward ſir edmond erle kent ceſſid neu er pray vn hir ſon till ſent haſt ¶and vpon kyng ſent lettres aft er ſir edmond wodſtoke ſhuld cum ſpeke wyncheſtre man er thyng left ¶and whan ſir edmond ſaw kyng ſent aft er lettres enſelid haſted myght till come vn wyncheſtre wen quene wiſt ser edward wos cumyn wyncheſtre tho anone ſhe praied ſo faſt went vn kyng edward hir ſon good erle wos reſtid anone lad vn barre robert hamond wos coroner kynges houſe hold aſſocied vn ſir roger mortimer ̄ tho ſpake foreſaid robert ſaid ¶sir edmond erle kent ye ſhall vnd er ſtond done v witt principally vn liege lord kyn edward englond myghty god ſaue kepe ye dedely enmye tratour ̄ alſo comune enmye vn reame ye haue ben bout mony day make priue deliu er aunce ſir edward ſum tyme kyng englond brother wich put doune rialte comun aſſent lordis englond peſyng lord kyng eſtate alſo reame ¶tho anſuerid good man ̄ ſaid forſoth ſir vnd er ſtondeth well neu er traitour kyng ne ream god world ̄ therfore kinges leue ſh̄all p̄ue defend man aught ¶tho ſaid mortimer ſir edmōd ſo ferforth know may well gaynſaid yt ī preſens ſhal well proued fals mortimer ſame lettre ſir edmond taken vn ſir iohan dauerill caſtell corf take kyng edward brother ſir edmond wiſt ne ſuppoſed thyng ſir iohn̄ dauerell bene ſo fals deliu er letter ſuch wiſe vn mortimer thought man er thing yt letter thā mortimer ſaid ſir edmōd ſhewed lett er ſeled axed yt knew yt letter ſeal ¶this ſir edmond loked ther ̄ viſed long tyme printe ſeal might ſe lett er wos therī wiſt well ſeal thought ſome letter yt bore gret charge thought thing od er lett er ſaid openly hering ye forſoth ſeall forſake ¶lo quod mortimer ſires ye hereth ſaid knowleches hī yt lett er ſeal ye ſhall conteyued ther ¶and mortimer opened letter folden afore gedre red openli word word hering ¶and whē lett er red ſaid lo ſires ye haue herid written ̄ yt hath knowlecheth letter ſeal ̄ may go ther fro ¶and cried yaf dome ſhuld honged draw hede ſmyten man er trator heiris diſherited eu er ſo lad forth put priſon ¶and wos done quene wiſt wos dampned way law life limme heires diſherited eu er thurgh opyn knowle chyng playn court ¶wherfore thought wer good forſaid ſir edmond wer haſteli kylled wittīg kyng el kyng lyghtly wold yef deth ſhuld turne moch ſorow ſo o wos enpeched ¶and anone quene thurgh councell mortimer ony councell ſent haſt balifs wyncheſter ſhuld ſmyte ſir edmond hede wodſtoke erle kent maner bydyng reſpite vp payn lyfe lyme ſhuld haue none execucion cauſe tarieng withſtonding iugemēt tho tokē balifs ſir edmond priſō lad beſide caſtell wyncheſtre ther made gong fermer ſmyte hede none durſt done ſo died ther ala ſai x day october iij yere kyng edwardis regne whan kyng wiſt ther wos wond er ſori ̄ let entier frere mynors wyncheſtre ¶of deth ſir roger mortimer erle march ſo befell tyme ſir roger mortimer erle marche ſo proud ſe hauteyn helde lord reame pere tho become ſo couetous yt folowed dame iſabell quenes court wos kyng edwardis modre beſet penyworthis wt offics quenes houſold ſame man er kynges officer ſo made takyng tochyng vitalles alſo cariagis becauſe ſpenſis gadre treſur ſo nombre yt myght ¶tho made hym wond er priue quene iſabell ̄ ſo moch lorſhip ̄ reteneu ſo yt al gret lordis englond wer adrad wherfore ye kyng cōcell towardis hī wer agreued ̄ ordeyned among vndo hī thurgh pure reſō law cauſe yt king edward yt kyngꝭ fadre traitourſly thurgh mordred caſtell berkeley bofore ſaid planly ī ye ſame part boke deth ¶and ſū wer ye kynges cōcell loued ye martimer told priuete kīg ̄ coūcell wer frō day day hī ſhend vndon wherfor mortimer ſore annoyed ̄ angri ye deuell ayens yt wer kīges coūcell ſaid wold thā bene avenged ſo euer toke ¶it long aft er ward kynd edward ̄ dame phelip wife ̄ dame iſabell kyngꝭ modre ſir rog er mortimer ne went vn notyngham ther ſodiorne ſo befell quene iſabell thurgh councell mortimer toke hir key yatis caſtell notingham ſo man mygh cum nother ne nyght thurgh commaundement mortimer ne kyng ne none councell ¶and • fell ſo mortimer deuell wroth bolled alſo wrath ayens kyngꝭ men edward ̄ principally ayeneſt accuſed kyng ye deth ſir edward fadre ¶and p̄uely coūcell take bitwen quene iſabell ̄ mortimer biſſh̄op lyncoln ſir symond beford ſir hugh trumpyngton od er priue ther coū cell vndone accuſed mortimer vn kyng fadres deth treſon felonie ¶wherfore al tho wer kynges councell whan wyſtē thee mortimer caſtyng priuely come kīg edward ̄ ſaid yt mortimer wold deſtroy cauſe yt accuſed kīg edwardis deth fadre praid yt wold maynten ī ther right ¶and thes lordis purſue quarell ſir william mountagu ſir humfrey de bo • hun ſir william brother ſir rauf stafford ſir robert hereford ſir willm clinton ſir iohn̄ neuil hornby mōy othre ther conſēt al̄l thes ſworen vpon boke maȳten quaril moch myght ¶and befell ſo aft er ſir william mō tagu ne none kīges frendis muſt nat herbrugged caſtel mortimer· went toke ther herbrughe diu er ſe place toune notyngham ¶and tho ſore adrad leſt mortimer ſhuld deſtroy ī haſt thei come vn kyng edward ser william mountagu tho yt wos caſtell priueli told ne none companie ſhuld take mortimer coūcell help will̄m eland ꝯſtabul ſame caſtel c er te ꝙ kīg loue wel therfore councel yt ye go forſaid ꝯſtabull commaund name fiend help take mortimer thing left vpon parill life limme ¶tho ſaid mountaygu ſir lord groūt mercy ¶tho went forth forſaid montaygu come cūſtabull caſtell ̄ told ye kyngꝭ ¶and anſurid ̄ ſaid ye kynges ſhuld done moch myght yt wold ſpare fore man er deth ſo ſwore made oth ¶tho ſaid ſir willm mountagu coneſtabull ī hering helpyng vn ſame quarell ¶now c er ti dere frend v behoueth worch quentyſe take mortimer ſith ye keꝑ caſtell haueth keyes ward ſir quod conſtabull ye vnd er ſtond gate caſtell ben lokked lockis dame iſabell ſend hider nyght ſhe hath key therof lieth vnder leueſell bed vn morow ſo ye may cū caſtell bi ye yates man er wiſe ¶but knowe aley ſtretcheth ward vnder erth ye forſaid caſtell goth weſt wich aley dame iſabell quene ne none hir men ne mortimer ne none companie knoweth ¶and ſo ſhall lede thurgh aley ſo ye ſhall cum thee caſtell aſpieng oni mā yt ben emnys ¶and thee ſame nyght ſir willm moū tagu ye lordis quarel ſame ꝯſtabul alſo wēt horſe ̄ made ſemblāt wer wend mortimer ſight ¶but anone ye mortimer herd tydyng wēt yt wold haue gon ou er ſee dred hī anone companie token councell amonges let ther paſſage ſent lettres anone thee porte ſo none ye gret lordis ſhuld wēd home ther cūtre bot areſtid ̄ take ¶and amōg od er thingꝭ willm eland coneſtable ye foreſaid caſtel priueli lad ſir william mountagu compain foreſaid way vnd er erth ſo til̄ com ī ye caſtell went vp toure mortimer ¶but ſir hugh trumpyngton aſcried hidouſly ſaid traitours nought ye comen vn caſtell ye ſhall die yit euell deth eu er ychon anone mountagu companie vp mace ſmote ſame hugh vpō heed brayn breſt fel ground ſo dede euell deth ¶tho toke mortimer armed toures dore hard noyſe dred quene iſabell ſaw mortimer taken ſhe made moch ſorow hert thes wordes vn ſaid ¶now fair ſires pray ye ne harme body worthy knyght welbeloued frend dere coſyn ¶tho went then come brought mortimer preſentid vn kyng edward commaunded bring ſauf ward anone yt wer conſent vn mortimer doyng herd tell taken went hid priuely nyght went toune eche ſide heuy hert mornyng leued vpon ther landis well myght ¶and ſo ſame yere mortimer take retene ix ſcore knyghtis ſquyers ſergiauntys armes fote men ¶and tho mortimer lad london ſir symōd beford lad take coneſtabull toure kepe ¶but aft er ward wos mortimer liif examined weſtmynſtre kīg al gret lordis englōd ꝑill yt might fall reame enquere alſo wich aſſentyng ſir edwardis deth kīges fad er alſo thurgh ſcottis aſcappid ſtanhope ſcotland kyng edward ¶and alſo chartre ragman deliu er ed vn ſcottis wherin homag feautes ſcotland conteyned yt ſcottis ſhuld done eu er engliſh̄ kīg reame ſcotland wherfore abſēs dampned draw honged treſon myſchief come vn ſent andrewes euen ye yere incarnaciō lord ihū criſt mccc xxx ¶how kyng edward get ayen vn grociouſly homage feautes scotlād wher put thurgh fals coūcell iſabell modre ſir roger mortimer new made erle marche ye haue hard lordis ſir iohan bailloll time pee choſen kyng scotland encheſon come eldeſt doughter erle dauid hontīgton thas wos kyng alexandre brether scotland died heir body begoten iohan made feaute homage kyng edward henris ſon iij land • ſcotland aft er ward withſaid homage thurgh councell ſcottis yere lord mcc lxxiiij ̄ ſent vn ye pope thurgh fals ſuggeſtion yt made oth vn forſaid kyng edward ou er aſtate ̄ wich othe pope aſſoilled thurgh bulſis hī ſent ¶and none kīg edward wiſt ther ordeyned anōe baron come vn berewike ̄ ꝯquerid toūe wich cōqueſt ther ſloyn xxvm ̄ vijc bailloll kīg ſcotland cō yeld hī good kīg edward ̄ kīg aft er ward deliu er ed hī tour londō gret lordis scotlād tho taken berewik yaf ſauf condithis gone ſcotland ¶and ſcottis ſith thurgh ther falſeneſſe wered vpon good kyng edward ¶and ſir iohan bailloll kīg ſcotland ſaw went ou er ſee vn dunpier leued ther vpō landis well myght till ſcottis wold amend thermiſdedis treſpace ̄ lad ſir edward ſon wherfore scot • diſpite called ſir iohan turnlabard beca • wold offende ne treſpace ayens good kyng edward englond ¶and ſo ſoke reame scotland ſet thar litell price ¶and ſir iohn̄ long tyme duelled fraunce till died ther ſir edward ſon vnderfeng heritage homage vn kyng fraunce landis dunpier ſo fell aft er ward edward yt wos iohn̄ bailloll ſon hī ſquyer englōd wos borne yorkſhire called iohn̄ barnabi edward bailloll loued moch wos ny full priue ¶and ſo iohn̄ barnaby debate frenſh man toune dunpier ̄ ſo killed wēt wai haſt myght caſtell haue ſocour help lord ¶and anōe come ye officer toūe take iohan barnaby felon ſir edward lord holp hym ̄ reſcued ̄ nyght made hī wēd caſtell ſo went way come ī englōd harme ¶and kyng fraūce ſaw ſir edward reſcued felon become wond er wroth ayens ſir edward anōe let areſtid toke hand landis ¶tho duelled ſir edwar priſon vn tyme ſir henri beaumont come fraunce wich henri ſum tyme erle angos ſcotland thurgh wife wos put forſaid erldom whē accordemēt bitwen englond scotland thurhh quene iſabell ſir rog er mortimer ther copani mariage ſhe made bitwen dauid wos robert brus ſon dame iohana atte toure kyng edwardis ſuſtre englōd well vnd er ſtode yt end ſh̄uld cum right wer thurgh ſir edward bailloll right heir reame scotland ¶and kyng fraūce lowys loued moch ſir henri full priue thought make deliueraunce ſir edward baillolls body migh man er wyſe ¶tho praied kyng yt wold graunte grace ſir edward baillolls body vn next ꝑlament myght lyue rentis meyn tym myght ſtand iuged bi peri parlamēt ¶and kyng graūtid praier made forſaid edward deliu er ed priſon man er aboue ſaid anone wos priſō ſir henri toke forth lad englond made duell priuely maner ſandhall vp onſe yorkeſhire lady veſcy ſo ordeined ther houge retenaunce pepul engliſſhmen ̄ alſo alien conquere ayen heritage ¶and ſo yaf moch ſilu er vn ſowdiours ̄ alien help hī ¶and behight help myght failed hī moſt nede ¶and tyme donald erle morrif herd tell ſir edward bailloll wos priuely cum englond come made gret ioye comīg ayen ſaid vn ̄ behight gret lordis englond ſhuld entendant ſh̄uld hold hyng right heir ſcotland homage feaute ¶tho come ſir henri beaumont kyng edward englond ̄ praied way charite wold graūt grace vn ſir edward bailloll myght ſaufl̄y gone bi land sandhall vn ſcotlond cōquere right heritage ſcotland ¶the kyng anſuerid ſaid ſuffre ye bailloll wend thurgh land ſcotland pepull wold ſay ſhuld aſſentyng vn compani ¶now ſir pray yow ye wold yef leue tak wt hī ſoudiours engliſhmen myght ſaufly lede thurgh yowr land vn ſcotland ¶and ſir vpon couenaūt ſo befal god forbide diſcomfited batell thurgh scottis alſo lordis holden wt bailloll bene eu er rentis haue englond ¶and ther kyng vpon thys couenaunt graunted ther bone tochyng tho wer ſame quarell wich clamed haue landis rentis ream englond ¶and thes wer name lordis purſued mater ſay ſir edward bailloll chalenged reame scotland ſir henri beammont erle angos ſir dauid stroboly erle atheles ſir geffrey monbray walt er comyn ̄ mony od er yt wer put ther heritage scotland whan pee wos made bitwen englond ſcotland ſaid ¶and ye ſhall vnd er ſtond yt thes lordis toke wt v hondreth men armes ij thouſand archer fote men ̄ tho wēt ī ſhip rauenſpore ſayled ſe till yt come vn ſcotland come land kynkehorne xij myle frō ſent iohanes toune anone ſent ther ſhippis ayen ſh̄uld hurte ne empayrid nether yt man ſh̄uld go ī ſhippis ayen though yt nede bot bidē ꝑrillis fle ſtād rather ſuffre deth flee maynten ther trew quarell ¶when erle fiffe fers man ſterne herd yt bailloll comyn take land ſcotland come ī haſt kynghorn xij thouſand ſcottis deſtroy hī ſh̄uld cum land ¶but ſir edward bailloll compani ther deſcomfited ye wich diſcomfiture ſir aleſand er ſeton wos ther kyllid mony od er ¶the erle fiffe tho ſore full yll ſhamed ſo litell compani diſcomfited ̄ ſhamly put al compani yt lyue flee ¶tho come ſir edward bailloll ̄ token cuntre till com vn abbey dunfermilyn ther found vitallis folke ̄ among thyngꝭ fond ī chambre bout v hondreth gret ſtauis fine oke long pykis yren ſtele toke deliu er ed moſt ſtrongeſt men compani ¶and anone went fro then logged ī felde ij myle ſent iohanes toune burgies toune herd erle fiffe diſcōfited thurgh bailloll wer ſore adr • br • ken ther brugges hed made ou er water erne ſo bailloll myght gone ou er wherfore loged hī ther nyght litell hede toke reſt ſaid vn pepull ¶now dere lordis ye know full well logged bitwen enmys may v hampre ther bote deth wherfore abide ſtill nyght leue ſhall turne v moch ſorow harme pouer ſcotland may eu er day wax encrece may ſo done bot litell pepull ayenſt ¶wherfor pray loue almyghty god make v bold hardy yt may mighteli take ſcottis nyght boldely vpon let v purſue night ̄ traueled thurgh v ſe oure heidines od er ſcottis yt ſe ſo traueled wery ſorer adrad v fight ferſely ſhall fight ̄ purſue ſo thurgh grece god almyghty world ſhall ſpeke doughtyneſſe chiualrie ¶and ſires vnd er ſtondeth wel yt ye companye yt comen ſir edward bailloll graūted wel vn councell werther right glad anone purſued vpon ſcottis becomen wonder wery ¶and bailloll companie ſore folowed ̄ moch harme ̄ ſorow thurgh ther aſſaut ſo might febull help litell pepull ¶but tho ſaid ſcottis amonges befall ſo litell pepull bailloll hath wynge done v ſo moch trauell ſorow ¶now certes ſemeth v wyrketh bi grace wond er gracious quarell c er te ſhall dede may cum hī v yeld ſith fadre ſet v price ¶and among thinges bail̄loll pepull paſſed wat er erne ſo ſir roger swynerton ſon wos fers angri went forth ſaw pepull armes ful well araied forth went vn faught kyled take mony wold abide ¶and nothles aſſaute wend bene gret hoſt ſcotland ¶and whē come morow gadred gedre reſtid ye yt engliſſhmē reſted thē nobull baron thomas veſcy nobull baron ſtafford prikked ther hors vp doūe hilles kepe eſtres cūtre pricked vp doūe ſaw gret oſt good aray ordeyned ther wynges wt helmys ̄ ſheldis ſhynyng cōīg vpon ¶and ther come tho two lordis ayen vn baillollis folke ̄ ſaid loue god almyghty bene good cō forth ye ſhal haue bataill anone right ¶and tho ſpak ſir fouk ſon gareyne baron gret renowne dede armes ¶sirris lordinges vnd er ſtōd ſay haue ſeyn mony diu er ſe wīges well amōg ſariſēs ̄ iues amōg ſcottis yit ſaw neu er fourth ꝑte wynge fight ther far ye abide enmys ynow fight ayēs good hert good fight wt c er ti bene full ayens compani ¶and therfore loue god take v good hert ̄ let v bene bold thynke neu er wife ne childre bot onli conquere enmys ī bataill ¶and thurgh help lord god ſhall ou er cum ¶and yt come hoſt ſcottis towardis full ſerely ayens ſir edward bailloll ī iij batai • le well araied armure ¶and wond er ferſly come toward bailluls compani whan ſir donald erle marcill yt ſcottis ſaw ſaid vn robert brus ſon robert brus thes wordis ¶sir robert ꝙ full ſore forthynketh hart yt thes pepull yt bailloll hath brought ſhuld die wt dynt ſcottis ſwerdis ſith criſtyn men well ben ¶and therfor thynke wer gret charite ſend vn yeld vn mercy raunſon thurgh grevos ranſon moch haue taken land done ill ¶now certes quod ſir robert brus haue well ꝑſaued yt thou art enmy traytour vn ſcotland ſith yt thou ꝯſent ſaue dedeli enmys yt hath done v moch ſorow ̄ ſhame ſemeth well ye bene ther aſſent ¶now c er te robert quod ſir donald falſly ye lie ther cōpani ne ther ꝯſent haſtely ye ſhall ſee fight rather ꝯpani ¶and c er ti ſir robert ſaid ſhall ī maugri thy hede aſſaill thou ¶and wt yt pricked ther ſtedis ferſly vpō caſkemore ̄ ther wyng folewed renge tho come met bailloll cōpani hongyng bough ī ſtrat paſſage ̄ ſo faſt haſted vn ye engliſſhmen ſo yt thouſandis fell groūd ech ou er ī hepe hors man ¶the bailloll men myghtely ſtode ayens faſt killed ſcottis groūd ̄ mony ſore woūded ſo lōg till yt ſtod vpō ̄ foyned ther ſuerdis ſperis thurgh • body ̄ ſo ſore traualed vpō thē till yt thei become wond er weri wiſt ſcottis wer left liue fled away ſaue ſelf ī ye beſt man er myght ¶and tho purſued ſir edward bailloll men killed till nyght fro thēs thei went ſent iohanes toūe ̄ toke held ther vitailed ſelf ther foūden inough wherwith make meri ¶tho made bailloll men yt wer wōdid go ſhip wend ī englōd hele ther woūdes ¶and ī yt time ther flemīg ī ſee ſtrong thefe robber wos caled crabbe ¶and flemmyng driuen flaūdres wikkednes therfore come ī ſcotland hold scottis moch harme vn thee engliſſh̄men myght ¶and crabbe met bailloll men ſe wer wounded bataill wer ſent ayen englond hele ther wound • crabbe yaf vn gret aſſaute wold haue killed euerychon bot engliſhmen defendid well manly diſcomfited crab companie ¶and tho gan fle ſcotland come toward ſent iohanes toune fond gret cōpany ſcottis wer comen ayen gedre diſcomfiture gaſkemore wich beſeged bailloll men ſame toune ſent iohn̄ anone told ſcottis wos diſcō fited engliſſhmen wer woūdid gaſkemore wēt toward englōd hele ther woūdes ſaid ſcottis ſhuld haue pouer ne myght ne grace yen edward bailloll encheſon ſcomfited empired chiualri scotland handfull men accompt yen scottis wer ſlayn wherfor coūcelled remeue ſege ſent iohanes toune kepe beſt maner yt thei coude might ¶the ſcottis vnd er ſtod yt crab ſaid ſothe forſoke ye ſege wēt then night ̄ helpe ſelf ī beſt man er yt thei might ¶when thing wos know thurgh ſcotland lordis ̄ knyghtis wer diſcomfited gaſkemore ſcotland thurgh ſir edward bailloll ¶ye ſhall vnd er ſtond lordes lady gentils scotland com wō der faſt ſent iohanes toune yel̄d vn baillol homage feaute ther landis yelde pee reſaued frely ¶and fro thēs wēt abbey scone ther crouned kyng ſcotland aft er let crie pee thurgh land ¶and ſame tyme befell kyng edward held ꝑlament among liege new caſtell vp tyne amēd treſpaces wronges done land ̄ ſir edward bailloll kyng ſcotland come thid er feaute homage reame ſcotland ¶and maner kyng edward englond gadred ayen homage feautes ſcotland wher put thurgh councell aſſent dame iſabell modre ſir roger mortimer erle marche tho toke bailloll kyng ſcotland leue kyng edward englond went then land sotland ſet bot litell counceled holpen quarell wherfore went fro went leued ther landes rentis ſcotland ¶and ſo befell afterward long kyng scotland ne remeued come toune anand ̄ ther token duelling thidder come company knyghtes ſtrong men worthy yeld vn kyng bere ſo fair dede countinaunce ſo yt truſtid moch vpō ¶and anone traytours ſaw truſt moch vpon them▪ ordeyned amonges l compani wold haue kyled ther lord kyng ¶but thurgh grace almighty god brakē thurgh walle hole chambre o god wold aſcappid theyr trecherie men wer kylled aſcappid moch dred vn toune cardoil ther held ſore anoyed befell lady eue concepcion· ¶tho ſent kyng edward bailloll kyng edward englond falſely tratoursly litell tyme put ſhame ſorow thurgh liege men vpon truſtid wōd er moch praid loue god yt wold maynten ̄ help ayens enmys ¶the kyng englond gret pitte behight helpe ſocour ̄ ſent word ſhuld hold pee ſtill forſaid cite cardoill till gadred pouer ¶tho ordeyned kyng edward englond coūcell london let gadre men diu er ſe ſhires englond whan wos redi went toward thee toune berewill vpon twede thid er come vn kīg edward bailloll scotland pouer beſeged toune made toune fair toune pauilons • iked ſo dred thee ſcottis made mony aſſaute gonnys engynes toune wherwith diſtroid mony fair houſes chirches alſo wer bet doune vn erth gret ſtones ſpituuſly come gonnys engynes notheles ſcottis kept well toūe tho two kynges might come therī long tyme ¶and notheles kīges abyde ther ſo lōg till tho toune failed vitales alſo wer ſo wery wakyng wiſt done ¶and ye ſhall vnderſtād thas tho ſcottis wer toune berewik thurgh commune coūcell ther aſſent let crie vpon walles toune might haue pee engliſhmen ther praied kyng grace merci praied trewes viij day vpō couenaunt wer reſcued ſide toune toward ſcotland ſcottis viij day wold yeld vn kyng toune alſo ¶and hold couenant proferid ye kyng xij hoſtages toune berewik ¶when hoſtages wer deliu er ed vn kyng anone tho toūe ſend vn ſcottis told ther ſorow miſchief ¶and thee ſcottis come tho priuely ou er wat er twed bought abbey ſir willm dyket wos tho ſtiward ſcotland mony yt come put ther gret ꝑill ſelf yt tyme ther life come ou er brugge wos broken ſtones away mony ther cōpani wer ther drenched forſaid willm went ou er companie come bi ſhippis englond kylled ī barge hul xvi men went toune berrewik water ſide ¶wherfore ſcottis held tho toune reſcued aſked ther hoſtages ayen kyng englond ¶and thee kyng ſent word ayen axed hoſtages wrong ſith come toune englond ſide couenant bitwen toune ſhuld reſcued half scotland ¶and anone kyng edward tho cōmaunded yeld toune wold haue hoſtage ¶and ſcottis ſaid toune reſcuyd wel ynowgh ther wold hold ¶when kyng edward ſaw ſcottis brek ther couenaunt made wos wond er wroth anone let take ſir thomas fitzwillm ſir alexand er ſeton wardeyn berewik wich thomas wos perſon dunbar let take fyrſt fore hoſtages encheſon ſir alexander fadre wos keꝑ toūe ¶and tho commaunded eu er day ij hoſtages toune till wer done deth yeld toune ¶and ſo ſhuld teche breke ther couenauntes ¶and tho toune herd thes thingꝭ becomen wond er ſori ſent kyng englōd wold graunte viij dais reſpet ſo bitwē tho hondreth men armes xx· men armes myght ſtrength gone bytwen toune berewyk vital toune muſt holde reſcued ¶and ſo wer xxi xxij wer ſlayn tho hundreth beforeſaid toune ſhuld holden reſcued couenaunt holden ſent xij forſaid toune hoſtage ¶the kyng englond graunted ther praier token hoſtages ſent margaretis eue yere grace mccc xxxij ſcottis com ferſely iiij wengis well raid ī army mete kīg edward englōd ̄ edward kīg ſcotland wt ther pouer com faſt ſharpely ayens euenſong tyme ̄ ye ſame tyme wos flode berewik ī wat er twed yt man myght wend ou er hors fote wat er wos betwen ij kyngꝭ reame englond yt tyme abidē ſcortis ī yt othir ſide encheſon yt engliſſhmen ſh̄old haue ben drenched ſlayn ¶this wos ye aray scottis yt
