ihū criſt mcccxxxij ¶and doyng laſtid engliſh page toke pilfry scottis yt wer killed eu er man myght take ony chalengyng man ¶and ſo gracious victori kyng turnyd ayen vn ſame ſege berewik whan beſegid ſaw ̄ herd kīg edward ſped yolden hī toune caſtell morn aft er ſent margaretis day ¶and kyng ordeyned ſir edward bailloll wyth nobull worthy men kepers gou er ners scotland abſence ſelf turned ayen come englond aft er victori moch ioye worſhip ¶and ye next yere ſewyng ſay yere incarnacion lord ihū criſt thouſand ccc ̄ xxxiij kyng edward vij· went ayen ſcotland wint er tyme wich viage caſtill kilbrigge ſcotland men wt hī com recou er yd ayens scottis luſt ¶and ſame yere ſir edward bailloll kyng scotland held parlament ſcotlād moni nobull lordes englōd wer yt ſame parlament encheſon ther landes ̄ alſo lordſhippis reame ſcotland ̄ helden ſame bailloll ¶and viij yere regne feſt ſent iohan baptiſt ſir edwarde bailloll veray trew kyng ſcotland heritage right lyne made homage feaute vn kīg edward englond reame scotland new caſtell vpon tyne preſence mony man worthy lordis alſo comunes reame englond alſo ſcotland none ſame yere kyng edward englond reſaued duke bretan homage erldom ̄ lordſhip richemond ¶and ſo folowyng ix yere rene mihelmaſſe kyng edward rode ſcotland ther faſt ſent iohanes toune almoſt wynter tyme ſo held criſtemaſſe caſtell rokeſburgh ¶and ſame yere thurgh englond ſent clementis tyde wynter ther aroſen ſuch ſpringyng welling vp watres alſo ſlodis ſee alſo freſh reu er y ſpringꝭ yt ſee bankes walles ̄ coſtes brekē vp yt mē beſtis ̄ houſes ī mōy place namly ī low cūtres violētli ̄ ſodēly wer drenchid ¶and frutis driuē away ye erth thurgh ꝯtinuance ̄ habūdaūce wat er ſee eu er aft er warde wer turned ī ſaltenes ſowrnes ſauour x yer kīg edward regne kīg edward entred ye ſcottis ſe aft er midſomer mōy ſcottis yaf bataill ̄ ou er cō mōe treted boued vn pe thurgh doughtyneſſe· ¶and mihelmaſſe thā next foloyng wos erle morif take edenburgh brough ī englōd ̄ put ī priſon ¶and ī monethes iune iulij next foloyng ī xi yere regne wos ſeyn ̄ aperid ī firmament bemed ſterre wych clarkys calle ſtella comata yt ſterre thynges longyng ther men ̄ goodis kīg edward fonde redy vn made beheighten ſeurte good feith truſt kīg haſted englond ayen left ther quene ſtyll behynd braban ¶than xiiij yere regne whan lordis ream fallen parlament wer called aſſembled gedre ſame parlament holden london feſt ſent helarie ¶the kynges nedes wer put forth promoted touching kīgdō fraunce nedis ſped kyng axed fifth ꝑte meuable ſorow ¶in ſame tyme thee kyng thurgh councell trew liege coūcell lord ther wer preſent toke kyng fraunces name toke ̄ medled kynges armes fraunce quartled wt armes englond commaundid forth coyen gold falen vnprofitabully u er harmfull neu er lat er ſcapyng al ꝑrels ſee god wold come tour london nyght ¶and ſame yere kyng held criſtēmaſſe men̄es ſent word ſcottis meſſingers wos redy wold fight wt bot ſcottis wold abide fled ou er scottis ſee hid thē wel̄ thei myght ¶and ī xvij yere regne feſt conuerſion ſent paule kyng edward wen bene ſcotland ſaw ſcottis wer fled tho come ayen englonde ¶and litell lent turnement dunſtabull wich turnement come al yong bachelary chiualrie englond mony erles lordis wich turnement kyng edward ſelf ther preſent ¶and next yere folewyng ī xviij yere regne ꝑlament holden weſtmynſtre auynzeme paſke kyng edward thrid made edward hys friſt ſon prince wale ¶and xix yere regne anone aft er ianiu fore lent ſame kyng edward let make full nobul iuſtes gret feſtis place birth windeſore ther wos neu er nōe ſuch ſeyn ther fore wich feſt rialte wer ij kynges ij quenes prince wale duk cornewaill x erles ix coūteſſes baron mony burgeis wich myght lightly wyndeſore witſon weke eu er yerly ¶and time engliſhmē ſo moch haunted ̄ cleued wodneſſe ̄ foly ſtrangers frō tyme comyng henaudres xviij yere paſſed▪ ordeyned changid eu er yere diu er ſe ſhappis ̄ diſgiſing clothing long large wide clothis deſtitut diſert al old honeſte good vſage ¶and tyme ſhort clothis ſtrayt waſted dagged kyt eu er ſide ſlatered botoned ſleues ̄ tapitis ſurcotes hodis ou er long ou er moch hangyng ſoth ſhall ſay wer like tormentouris deuels ther clothing ſhoyng ̄ aray men ¶and woman nyſely yit paſſid men aray ̄ coriouſloker wer ſo ſtrait clothid let hang fox tailles ſewed neth within ther clothis hele hide ther arſes wich diſgyſynges pride ꝑauentur aft er ward brought forth cauſed mony myſhappis ̄ myſchief reame englond ¶the xx yere kyng edward went ou er britan gaſcoyn who companie went erle warwyk erle suffolke erle hūtyngton erle arundel ̄ mony lordis comune pepull gret multitude gret nauye cc xl ſhippis anone midſomer venge mony wronges harmes done thurgh councell gret lordis reame englond called ̄ gadred geder perlament weſtmynſter fore eſter ordeyned paſſe ou er ſee ayen diſeſe deſtrobull rebelles fraūce ¶and nauye wos come gedre made redy paris brugge fond broken two dayes let make ayen morn aft er thee aſſumcioō lady kyng edward paſſed ou er wat er ſeyn goyng toward creſcy diſtroyed way tounes pepull duelling ther feſt ſent ¶wherfor ſaid commune among pepull nrē beal ſoy retreyt ſay fair draweth ¶than kyng edward engliſſhmen thanked god almyghti ſuch victori aft er ther gret labour taken thyng nedefull ther ſuſtinance edward word wold yef playn bataill iij day aft er euenſong tyme durſt cum fro ſeege ̄ abide ¶and kyng edward herd ony lōg tarieng long viſement accepte gladly day houre bataill yt philip aſſigned ¶and kyng fraū ce herd next nyght aft er ſet tentis fire ̄ remeued ̄ went away then cowardly ¶than wer ī toune caſtell beſeged ſeyng none help ne ſocour kyng fraunce ne men ¶and alſo ther vitales within wer ſpendit waſted forfaut vitales refriſhing eten hors houndes cattes myce kepe ther trewth long myght ¶and ſaw wos found among laſt thei thyng among ete ne lyue ne ſocour ne reſcueng frenſhmen ſide wiſt well moſt nedis die defaut el̄s yeld toune anone tho thei wenten token downe baners armes fraunce eueri ſide wer hongen wenten walles forſaid toune diuerſe place naked ou er wer borne ſauf onli ther ſhertis ther priue clothes held ther ſwerdis naked ye point donward thi • hondis puten rope halter ther nekkis yelden vp key toun caſtill kyng edward englond gret fere dred hert er xxiiij yere kīg edwardis regne wit vnd er ſtond treſon wos begun calais ̄ ordeyned ſell toune gret ſomme florens vn kīg philip fraūce thurgh falſeneſſe ̄ ordynaūce knyght wos called ſir falſeneſſe opē ly high men myght ¶and ſhall ye wer deceyued comen priue poſtterne ouer litell brugge tre wer comen ſotaly priuely brigge wos draw vp kept none comen myght go ne mo cū ¶and anone englyſhmen went priue hole wyndous ouer walles toune caſtell went faughte mā ly frenſhmen wer better wich wer occupied ſel̄f ther ſide king toune hauyng ſcarſly xxx men armes drew ſwerd loud vois cried vp high ſent edward ſent george ¶and folke herd comen rennyng yaf ther ther enmys ſo gret aſſaut ther wer mo two hondrith men armes mony mo ſlayn mony fleden away ſo grace god almyghty victorie fell vn engliſhmen kyng toke hym geffry finder trechorie alſo mony frenſh priſoners ̄ come ayen englond ¶and ſame yere yere afore thee yere next ſo gret peſtilence men eſt weſt namli thurgh botch tho mihelmaſſe vn auguſt next folewyng almoſt hole yere ¶and thes day wos deth without ſorow weddyngis frenſhip wilfull penaunce derth without ſcarcite fleyng without refute ſocour mony fled place place cauſe peſtilence wer enfeckid myght aſcap deth ꝓphet iſae ſaieth fleith fro face dred ſhall fall diche windeth diche ſhall hold ̄ tied grenne whē peſtilence wos ceſed god wold vnnethes tenth parte regne ſent iohannes day harueſt ī ſee faſt winchelſe king edwarde gret bataill men ſpayn wher ther ſhippis nauye lay chaned gedre muſt fight drēched ¶and ſo worthy men armes ̄ ſee coſtes faſt wynchelſe romeny wer gadred ged er nauye ſhippis redy engliſſhmen met manly ̄ ſtifly wt ther enmys comyng ferſly ayens ¶and whē ſpanys veſſailles nauy wer cloſed ī ther mē might ſe ſtrōg bataill ſides lōg ī ye wich bataill wos faught wer ſpitouſly hurt aft er batail ther wer xxiij ſhippis thers take ̄ ſo engliſhmen better next yere folowyng regne yt ſay xxvi yere ye kīg thugh coūcell let orden ̄ make hys new monay yt ſay ye peny grot value iiij pen half grot ij pen bot wos le weight old ſterlīg wos v ſhillyng poūde ¶and xxvij yere regne wos gret derth vitailles wich called thee dere ſomer ¶and xxviij yere regne ī ye ꝑlament holden weſtmīſtre aft er eſter ſir henri erle lancaſtre wos made duke lancaſtre ī yere wos ſo gret drought frō moneth marche mōeth iuyll ther fell rayn erthe wherfore frutis ſedis herbes moſt ꝑtie wer loſt defaute ¶wherof ther come ſo gret diſeſe men beſtes derthe vitales englond ſo land eu er afore bene plenteous nede tyme feke vitalis refreſſſyng occupied bi diuerſe kynges fraunce hand haue hold kyng edward heires ſucceſſours eu er frely peſabully good quiet vpō thys couenaunt kyng englond ſhuld leue releſen right claym claymed kyngdom fraunce titell toke ther vpō wich ſpeche couenauntis wos ſent court rome ſides kynges forſaid couenaūt ſh̄uld enbulled bot god ordeyned better kīges worſſhip englōd· thurgh fraud diſcert frenſhmen pariſſhid drenchid wich stiward worthi gret men denmarke wer take priſoners kyng englond councell priſoned wich lordis danois aft er ward come ſoughten bout haue ther goodis loſt thay wele apaied ne ther bane ¶and tyme pers kyng spayn kyngꝭ yt ſay kyng naune kyng malogre beyng menes wē ten bitwen praied coūcell help ſir edward prince thurgh who coūcel vnderſtond ther article deſire wos ¶and wer founden priued aft er ward kyng nede wold gladly eu er man hys pouer ſtate help len ¶and wer publiſſhid ſhewed ꝑlament mony playntes defautis diu er ſe officer reame namly af lord latimer naunce ayens profet ye reames alſo comynalte axed deſirid ſhold meued put away ther ſtedis wiſe men worthy wer trewe ̄ well aſſayed proued good gou er naunce ſhuld put ther ſtedis ¶so among ther wos kyng edward yaf richard burdeux heir wos prince edwardis ſon wyndeſor ordir knyghthod made knyght wich kyng edward whan regned li yere xi kal̄ iune died shene buried worſhipfulli weſtmynſtre whois ſoule god haue merci amen ¶this kyng edward forſothe paſſing goodneſſe full grecious among worthy men world paſſid ſhone vertu grace yef fro god boue prediceſſours wer nobull men worthy wos well herted mā hardy drad neu er miſh • ppis ne harmes ne euell fortun might fall nobull weri fortunat land ſe batailles aſſembles wt paſſing glorie ioye victorie meke benyngne homeli ſobre ſoft maner men well auiſed temꝑall wordly nedes wiſe ī coūcell diſcret meke ſpeke wt ī dedis ̄ man er gētill wel taught hauīg pitte yt wer ī diſeſe plentious yeueng benefaites almoſe biſi ̄ curious ī bylddyng duke lancaſtre wer accerded ged er thurgh ther councell man er kīg ſpaī ſhuld wedde dukis doughter lancaſtre right heir ſpayn ſh̄uld yef vn duke lancaſtre gold ſelu er wer caſt gret wegges ̄ mōy iewelles mony viij charietes myght carie ¶and eu er yere life duke lancaſtre duch • ſ wyf xm marke gold wich gold auenture charge ſpayn ſhuld au • ̄ture bring yerly vn bayon dukis aſſignes ſurite made ¶and alſo duke maried od er doughters vn kyng portingale ſame tyme whan done thus come home ayen englond good lady wyfe alſo mony worthy man vpon flix died ¶and xv yere kyng richardis regne hee held criſtēmaſe ī man er wodſtoke erle penbroke yong lord tendre age wold lerne iuſt knyght called ſir iohn̄ ſent iohn̄ riden gedre parke wodſtoke ther worthi erle penbroke ſlayn othir knyghtis ſpere keſt whan coupled thus good erle made ther end ther kyng ̄ quene made moch ſorow dethe ¶and xvi yere kyng richardis regne iohn̄ hende beyng tyme maire london iohan walworth henri • anner beyng ſhereues london ſame time baker man bare baſket horſbred fletſtret toward hoſtre ther come yong man biſſhoppis saliſberi wos called romayn toke hors lofe baſkit baker ̄ aſkid ſo romayn turned ayen brak bakerhede neghbours come wold haue reſted romayn brake fled lordis place ꝯſtabull wold haue biſſhoppis men ſhet faſt yates keped place man might entre moch pepull gadred thidder ſaid wold haue hī elles wold brenne vp place wer therī ¶and come maire ſheriues moch pepull ceſſed malice comunes ̄ made eu er man go hom ther houſes kepe pee ¶and romayns lord ther biſſhop saliſburi maſter iohan waltham yt tyme wos treſorer englond went ſir thomas arundell erchebiſſhop yorke chanceler englōd ̄ ther biſhop made cō plaint vn chanceler vpō ye pepull cite london ¶and thes ij biſſhoppis gret malace vēgeaūce cō vn kyng wyndeſore ̄ made gret complaīte vpō maire ̄ ſheriues anon cite aft er ward wer kīg coūcell ̄ caſt vn cite greuous hert wond er gret malice ¶and anōe ſodēli kīg ſent aft er maire londō ij· ſheriues ̄ thei come vn caſtell wyndeſore kyng rebukid maire ſh̄eriues full foule offence done ayens officer chambur londō wherfor depoſit put mare bothe ſheriues ̄ wos done xiiij day afore feſte ſent iohan bapteſt ¶and kyng called knyght wos called ſir edward dalingrigge ̄ made hī wardeyn gaunour cite ̄ chambur londō ̄ ou er peple therī ¶and ſo kepid office iiij wekis cauſe yt wos ſo gentill tendir citiſens londō wherfor kyng depoſit made ſir baudwyn radyngton knyght yt wos courtrouller kng houſold wardeyn ̄ gou er nour hys chambre pepull therin cheſe ij worthy men cite ſhiriues gaune kepe kyngee lawes cite· called gilbert mawefeld thomas newenton ſhereues maire ij ſhereues alderman worthy craftes lō went fote vn tour ther come conſtable tour yaf maire ſheriues ther oth ̄ charge ſhuld haue take eſcheker weſtmynſtre kingꝭ court iuſtices baron eſcheker went home ayen ¶and kyng councell gret malace deſpite cite londō remeued courtis weſtmynſtre vn cite yorke ſay chaunceler eſcheker kyngꝭ bench comune place· ther held thes courtes law fro midſomer ſay feſt ſent iohn̄ baptiſt vn feſt criſtemaſe next ſuyng kyng councell ſaw ſo ꝓfitabull ther wos londō anōe remeued ayen vn londō ſo weſtminſtre gret eſe offics vaūtage kyng comunes reame ¶and pepull londō ſaw ̄ knew thes courtes wer come ayen ¶and kyng pepull alſo ye maire ̄ ald er men thee chief comunes cite let gad er gret ſomme gold comunes cite ordeyned made gret rialte ayens comyng londō haue hys grace good lordſhip alſo ther liberty fraūchies graūtid vn ayen wer wont haue afore tyme ¶and thoru gret inſtance ̄ prayr quene othhir lordis lady kyng graūtid grace wos ſhene ī ſutherei ¶and thā kyng ij dais aft er com londō maire cite ſhereues ald er mē worthy mē cite aft er ward ridden ayens good aray vn heth ſide man er ſhene ſubmyttyng hūb • ly mekely man er obeiſſaunce vn ought ¶and thus brought kyng ̄ quene londō kyng come yate thee brugge londō ther preſented mylke white ſtedeſadiled brideled trapped cloth gold rede ꝑtied gedre quene palfrey white ſame aray trappid white rede condites london ranne wyne white rede maner pepull drinke wold ¶and bitwen ſent poules croſſe cheppe ther made ſtage riall ſtandīg vpon high ̄ therin wer mony angel diu er ſe melody ̄ ſonge ¶and angell come doune frō ſtage high viſe ſet croūe gold pight rich perle precious ſtonys vpō kyngꝭ hede othir vpō quenes hede ſo citiſens brought thee kyng quene vn weſt mynſtre ī ther palais morne mayre ſhereues alderman london come vn kīg palays weſtminſtre preſentid ij baſīs ſiluer ouer gilted full coyned gold ſoum xx hondreth pound prayng high merci grace lordſhip ſpeciall grace myght haue good loue wt liberty fraūcheſes like wiſe wer wond haue fore tymes ̄ lettres patentis chartri confermed ¶and ye quene othir worthy lordis lady fell knee beſought kyng grace cōferme ¶than kyng toke vp quene ̄ graūted hir hir aſkīg ̄ thankid kyng ye quene went home ayen ¶and xvi yere kyng richardis regne certayn lordis ſcotlond come englond get worſhip foot armes thes wer ꝑſons erle marre chalēgid erle marchall englond iuſt c er tayn pointes horſbake ſh̄arp ſperis ̄ riden ged er ij worthi knyghtis lordis certayn courſes full chalenge ſcottis erle mado coſt hors man ij ribbes broken wt fall ſo borne ſmygthefeld hom vn yn litell tyme aft er wos caried homward ī litter yorke ther died ſir willm darell knyght tho baner ſcotland made chalenge sir pers courtayn knyght kyngꝭ banerer englond c er taī courſes yit hors bake ſame feld ̄ riden c er tayn curſeſ ̄ aſſayd myght haue better yaf ou er wold chalenge ſir pers courtayn knyght kynges baner englond turned hors rode home vn yn ¶and one cokkeborne ſquier ſcotland chalenged ſir nicholl hawbarke knyght c er tayn courſes yet ſharp ſperis horſbake ̄ riden v courſes geder ̄ eu er courſe ſcot wos caſten doune hors man thus engliſh lordis thankid god feld ¶and ī xvij yere kyng richardes regne died good gracious quene anne wos wife kyng richard man er ſhene ſhire furre vpō witſonday wos ſhe brought londō ſo weſtmynſtre ther • o ſhe beried worthely entered beſide ſent edwardis ſhrine who ſoule almyghty god haue pitte merci amen ¶how kyng richard ſpouſed dame iſabell kyngꝭ dought er fraunce ī toune calais brought hir englōd let hir croūed quene ī abbey ſent petres weſtmynſtre xx· yere kyng richardis regne went ou er ſee vn calais dukis erles lordis baron mony worthy ſquiers gret aray comune pepull ye reame ī good aray lōged ſuch kīg ̄ p̄nce nobley ꝑſon hī reu er ence ̄ ob ser uaūce ought done ther liege lord ſo mighti kīg ̄ emꝑour ī abide reſaue ther worthy gracious lady yt ſhuld wyfe yong creature xix yere age dame iſabell kingꝭ doughter fraunce mony othir worthy lordis gret name baron knyghtis moch pepull comen vn toune grauenyng ij dukis fraunce yt duke burgoyn othir duke barre yt wold ferther leſſe plegges ¶and thā kyng richard deliu er ed ij plegges go ſauf cum ſauf two worthi vncles duke glouceſtre duke yorke ¶and thes two went ou er wat er grauenyng abeden ther plegges vn time mariage feſt done thes ij dukis fraunce wer comen ayen vn grauenyng water ¶and thes ij worthy dukis comen ou er wat er grauenyng ſo calays wt worſſhipfull lady dame iſabell wos kynges dought er fraū ce hir come mony worthy lord eke lady knyghtes ſquiers beſt aray myght ther met menay calais wich welcomed hir hir meny wt beſt honor reuerence myght ſo brought hir ī toune calais ¶and ther ſhe wos reſaued ſolempnite worſhip myght done vn ſuch lady brought hir vn kyng kyng toke hir ̄ welcomed hir hir fair companie made ther ſolempnite myght done ¶and kyng coūncell aſkit frenſh lordis whethir al couenaūtes forwardes compoſicion wer ordeyned made party ſhuld trewly keped hold bitwen ¶and ſaid ye ther ſwore toke ther charge vpō boke made ther oth well ̄ trewly hold man er pointes couenaūtis contradiccion delay ony man er wiſe ¶and thā wos ſhe brought vn ſent nicholas chirche calais ̄ ther ſhe wos worthely weddid moſt ſolempnite ony kyng quene myght erchebiſſhoppis biſſhoppis ̄ miniſters holi chirch wer brought home vn caſtell ſet mete ¶and wer ſerued maner delicaſie riall metis drinkes plenteuouſli maner ſtraungeis othir creature warned feſt bot wer welcum ther wer gret halle tentis ſet vpon grene caſtil receyue maner pepull eu er office redy ſerue thus worthy mariage wos ſolemply done endid rialte ¶than thes ij duke fraunce ther pepull token ther leue kyng quene went ayen vn grauenyng water ther ye frenſh lordis ſay ij dukis ther menye come ouer wat er grauenyng ther met eu er ichō toke leue othir ſo deꝑted lordis comen ayen vn calais frenſh lordis wenten ou er water ſo home fraunce ayen· ¶and anone aft er kyng made redy quene lordis lady ther peple come ou er thee ſee englond ſo vn london maire ſheriues ald er men ond worthy commune ridden ayens vn blak heth kent ̄ ther met thee kyng quene wolcomed good aray eu er man clothyng craft ̄ ther minſtrelles ¶and ſo brought vn ſent gregoris barre ſouthwarke ther token ther leue kyng quene ridden kenyngton pepull londō turned home ayen ¶and turnyng ayen londō brigge ther ſo gret p̄ſe peple hors ̄ fote therwer dede brigge xi· ꝑſons mē woman ̄ child who ſoules almighty god haue pited merci amen ¶and aft er ward quene wos broght vn tour londoō ̄ ther ſhe nyght morow erle arundell erle warwik anone kyng euell excitacion ̄ euell councell malice late ī euenyng ſame dai aboue ſaid made redy ſtrength rode eſtſex vn toūe chelmeſford ſo come plaſſhe ſodenly ther ſir commaundement englond ¶and tyme erle marchall wos capitayn cali anone commaūdemēt kyng fals councell commaunded capitayn put deth ¶and anōe c er tayn yomen good duke kepyng toke thir councell ſhuld put vn deth ¶and ther oppoyntment ſhuld cum vpō wer ī bedde ſlepe fether bedde anōe bond hand fote charged lie ſtill whan done thus token two ſmale towellis made ij rid knottis ̄ caſt towellis nee thei toke fethir bede lay vndir ̄ caſt aboue hī drew ther towellis eche wei ſum lay vpon fethir bede vpō vn tyme wos dede cauſe ſhuld make nonoyſe thus ſtrangled worthy duke vn deth who ſaule god high pitte haue merci amen ¶and kyng reſtid worthy duke vncle ̄ ſent calais come ayen vn londō haſt wonder gret pepull o ſone wos comen ſent erle arundell good erle warwike ¶and anone come areſtid ſelf ſir iohn̄ cobham ſir iohn̄ cheyn knyghtis areſtid ſame man er till made ꝑlament anone werput hold erle arundell went large vn ꝑlamēt time fonde ſufficient ſureti abide law anſuer maner pointes kyng councell wold put vp ¶and xxi yere kyng richardis regne ordeyned ꝑlament weſtmynſtre wich wos called gret parlament ꝑlament wos made iugge iij worthy lordis othir mo liſt tyme ¶and iuggement kyng let make haſt alōg houſe ̄ large tymbre wich wos called hall couerid wt tyles ou er oppī ſides endis yt man er men myght ſee thurgh ther dome holden vpon thes forſaid lordis iuggement yef forſaid parlament ¶and cum vn ꝑlament kīg ſent writtis eu er lord barō knight eu er ſquier eu er ſhire thurgh englōd eu er lord gadre ̄ bring retenew ſhort time ̄ beſt aray myght gete mayntenyng ī ſtrengthīg kīg ayens yt wer enmys ̄ yt wer done ī haſt come ī payn deth ¶and kīg ſelf ſent cheſterſhire chiuetās cuntre gadred brought gret huge multitude pepull knightis ſquiers ̄ principalli yemen cheſterſhire wich yomen archiers kyng toke hys courte ̄ yaf bowge court ̄ good wage keꝑs body nyght ̄ day aboue al othir ꝑſons ̄ moſt loued beſt truſt wich ſone afterward turned kīg gret loſſe ̄ ſhame hyndring ̄ vtterly vndoyng deſtruciō ye ſhall tyme come ſir henri derby gret menye men armes archiers erle rutlād come ſtronge pouer pepull men armes archiers ¶and erle kent brought gret pouer men armes ̄ archiers erle marchall come ſame man er lorde spē ser ſame man er ye erle northumberland ſir henri percy ſon ſir thomas percy erlis brod er thes worthy lordis brought fair menye ̄ ſtrong pouer ech mā beſt aray ̄ duk lancaſtre duke yorke comē ſame man er men armes archiers folowyng kyng ¶and ſir willyam ſtrop treſorer englond come ſame man er thus aray come worthy mē land vn kyng ̄ thes pepull com londō ī day ſo moch yt euery ſtret lane ī londō ī ſubarbes full logged x xij myle londō eu er way thees pepull brought kyng weſtmynſtre went homi ayen ther loggyng hors man ̄ mōday xij day september ꝑlamēt began weſtmīſtre wich callid gret ꝑlament ¶and friday next aft er erle arundel̄ wos brought ꝑlament among lordis wos ſent matheues day apoſtill euangeliſt ther wos iugged vn deth hall yt wos made ī palays weſtmynſtre wos iugement ſhuld go fote handis bound behynde thee place wos iuggid ſo forth thurgh cite londō vn toure hill hede ſmyten ſo dede ſame place vi thee gret lordis yt ſat iuggement ridden vn place ther wos vn thee deth ſo ſee execucion wer aftar ther dome ¶and bi kynges commaundement went fote men armis archiers gret multitude cheſtre ſhire men ſtrengthyng thee lordis brought erle deth dred leſt thee erle ſhuld reſeued takin frō whan com london thus paſſed forth thurgh cite vnto deth ther • e toke full paciencli who ſoul god haue mercy amen ¶and come freris auſtyns toke vp body hede good erle ̄ bare home vn ther place beried ther quere morow wos ſir richard erle werwike brought parlamēt ther erle arundell wos iugged yaf erle werwike ſame iugement forſaid erle lordis compaſſion cauſe age releſed perpetuall priſon put thee ile man ¶and mōday next lord cobhan kēt ̄ ſir iohn̄ cheyn knyghtie wer brought parlament ī ſame ¶and ſame yere died ſir iohan gaunte kinges vncle duke lancaſtre biſſhoppis yn holborne wos brought frō thēs ſent paules ther kyng made held enterement well ̄ worthely hys lordis chirch ſent paules ī londō ther wos beried beſide dame blaunch wife wos dought er heir good henri yt wos duke lancaſtre ¶and ī ſame yere ther fell diſcenciō bitwen duke herford duke norfolk ī ſo moche waged bataill ̄ caſten doune ther gloues wer taken vp enſeled bataill ioyned day ſet place aſſigned wher ſhuld couentre theder come kyng lordis day wos ſet feld thees two worthi lordis comen feld well cleen armed well arayed ther wapen redy done ther bataill redy place fight vtteraunce ¶but kyng bad ceſe toke thee quarell hand ¶and forth right ther preſent exiled duke herford terme x yere duke norfolke eu er ¶and ſir thomas arundell erchebiſſhopp cantorbury wos exiled ſame tyme eu er ̄ depeſit ſee malice kyng anone thes iij worthy lordis wer commaunded defendid kynges reame anone gat ſhippis diu er ſe hauens went ouer ſee diuerſe landis eche way ¶and duke norfolke wēt venice ther died who ſoule god haue merci amen ¶and kyng richard made clarke ſir rogier walden ercheaiſſhop cantorburi ¶and xxij yere kyng richardis regned fals councell ymaginacion couetous men wer wer made ordeyned blanke chartres made enſeled maner rich mē thurgh reame ſo moch compelled diuerſe pepull ſet ther ſeall ther wos done gret couetiſe wherfore good hertis reame wer clene turned away kyng eu er ¶and vttirly deſtrucciō end ſo high excellent prince ̄ king thurgh couetous fals coūcell falſely betrayd ala pitte yt ſuch kīg myght ſe ¶and thā king richaid ſet kīgdome riall land englond ferme vn iiij ꝑſons ye wich wer thes sir willm ſtrop erle wyl̄teſhire ̄ treſorer englond ſir iohn̄ buſſh henri grene ſir iohn̄ bagot knyghtis wich turnid miſchief ̄ deth litill tyme ye ſhall aft er ward find writtyn ¶and thā king richard made gret ordynaūce wēt ou er ſe irland ̄ moni gret lordis gret hoſtis ſtrength ther king men armes archiers moch gret ſtuf right good ordynaūce longed vn ¶and paſſed ou er ſe ordand ̄ made ſir edmōd langley vncle duke yorke liuetenaūt englond abſent gou er nance ̄ coūcell ōf thes iiij knyghtis take englōd ferme kyng thā paſſed ſe come irland ther wos well ̄ worthely reſeyued ¶and thees rebelles ben called wild iriſhmē cō doūe kyng ̄ yeld bothe body goodis ſuore vn liege men ther ther homage ̄ feaute ̄ good ſeruice thus conquered moſt partie irland ī litell time ¶and kyng richard thus irland ſir henri bolingbroke erle derby kīg made duke herford wich duke kyng exiled owt land comen ayen englond chalenge thee dukedom lancaſtre right ̄ trew heritage come doune fraunce land vn calays ¶and ther met sir thomas arundell wos erchebiſſhopp cantorburi wos exiled englond ̄ com erle arundell ſon heir wiche wos ward kepīg ſir ion ſhelley knyght ſum tyme wt erle huntīgdone duke exceſtre thee wich wos tho thee caſtell reigate southſex ther ſtole away come calais ther wos kepid well worthely till thees othir two lordis wercomen calais worthy duke erchebiſſhop cantorburi arundell ſhippid hauen calais drew ther courſe northward ariued yorke ſhire rauenſporne faſt wydelyngtō ther come entred thee land two lordis ther manye ¶and moche pepull reame yt herd commyng knewen wher wos anane drew vn welcomed theſe lordis ſo coraged maner thyng paſſed forth land gadred moch pepull ¶and whan kyng richard herd wiſt thees ij lordis wer cumen ayen englond wer londid ¶than kyng left ordynaūce irland come englondward haſt yt myght come thee caſtell flint ther abode take councell myght com none ¶and ſir thomas percy erle worceſtre yt kīges stiwarde wyſt knew anone come hall amōges pepull brake thee yerde riall kynges houſold anone euery man wos diſꝑ bled euery man went way ſoke ther maſtir ſouerayne lord ̄ left alloyn ¶and thus wos kīg richard brought doune deſtroid ſtoden ſelf allone without comforth ſocour ani good councell man ala pite riall kyng ¶and anone come tidynges yt ſir henri bolīgbroke wos vp wt wonder ſtrong pouer pepull ſquiers englond riſen vp thee ſhires ſtrēgthīg hī ayen thee kyng richard thus ſone wos come thee good archiers fraunce come paris duke burgoyn ¶and ther reſaued welcomed thes engliſhmen lordis meny ¶and wos done wit duke orliaū ce comen ſemtclowe faſt paris gret nombur men army arbalaſters thidd er went engliſhmen fought gat brigge ſemtclow ther ſlew moch pepull frenſhmē· arminakis thee remenaunt fled wold longer abide ¶and engliſhmen come ayen vn paris ther token thir leue duke come home ayen englond ſaufte duke yaf gret yeftes anone folowyng duke orliaūce ſent embaſſatours ī englōd kīg henri iiij beſechyng hī help ſocour ayens dedly enmy ye duke burgoyn ¶and kīg made thomas ſon duke clarence othir ſone iohan duke bedford ̄ othir ſone humfrey duke glouceſtre ſir thamas beauford erle dorſet duke awemarle made duk yorke tha kīg ordeyned ſon ſir thomas duke clarence ſir thom̄s beauford erle dorſet ſir iohn̄ cornwill many othir lordis knyghtis ſquyers men armes archiers go ouer ſee fraunce helpyng ſtrengthyng duke orliaūce ¶and thes worthy lordis ther retenue ſhippid hamptō ſailed ou er ī normādie ̄ landid hogges ther met lord hambe ther landyng wt vijm men armes frenſhmen iij▪ ſergauntis armes wt wer put flight takē vijc men armes ̄ iiij hondreth hors wt tho wer ſlain ī feld ¶and ſo riden forch thurgh fraūce toke caſtellis ̄ toūes ̄ ſlew moch pepull frenſhmen yt withſtode thē ̄ toke mony priſon er riden ſo paſſed forth till come burdeux ̄ ther reſtid ſet cū tre pee reſtid till vyntage wer redy ſaill thā duke menye come home englond ſaufte thā ked god ¶and ſame yere wos kynges coyn changed thurgh englond kyng councell ſay nobull half nobull ferthyng gold ¶and xiiij yere kyng henris regne iiij let moke galeys hoped haue paſſed gret ſee ſo forth ieruſalē ther haue endid liffe god viſeted ſo ſone wt infirmites gret ſikeneſſe myght well endure ſo feruently wos take brought bed weſtmīſter fair chambur ¶and o lay bede aſkid chamberlayn called yt chamber yt lay anſuerid ſaid ieruſalem ſaid ꝓphecie ſaid ſhuld make ende die ieraſalem made redy vn god diſpoſed ſone died ̄ wos caried water weſtmynſter barge vn feuerſham then wos caried cantorberi land moch torche light brinnyng abbey crichurch ther wos entered beried 〈…〉 thus endid ye worthy kīg henri midlentyn ſonday ī yere lord mccccxiij who ſovle god haue merci anen artī v wos 〈◊〉 aft er iohn̄ xiiij yere mā choſen thee coūcell cōſtantinoplī othir wos depoſit yt ſtreffe ſo come pe chirch wich long tyme afore wos deſyrid neceſſari thee defence faith myghtieſt 〈◊〉 eu er wos rich gret iugge edefied tounys wallis ſtretis diſtroyd heriſes moch good thurgh nobull prince sygmunde gadred moch monay holy land geten ayen bot deth come oppon lettid made coūcell afore deth mater ther deceſſed ugeniꝰ wos 〈◊〉 aft er martin xvij yere eugeny wos choſen peſablie deth martin man dowtid bot wos 〈◊〉 bot ſhortly wos expulſit rome wos ſo fled nakid alſo wos cited coūncell baſiliens depoſit bothe chargid ayen began thee ſtriffe wich ſtode deth ̄ tho fauoured ſaid worthy moch louyng cō trari ſaid tho yt wer ayens bot ſum eu er wos hee takyn dignite vpō hī fore wos gret abſtenēs good fame ̄ yt aft er leue thee iugemēt god circa annum domini miiijcxiij kyng henri thee fifth wos kyng henris ſone • nd deth kyng henri iiij regned kyng henri ſone borne monmouth wale worthy kyng gracious man gret conquerour thee friſt yere regne gret loue goodneſſe ſent freris langely ther fad er berie kyng richard ſecūd let take body erth • yen bring weſtmynſter ī riall chare cou er ed wt blake veluet baners diuerſe armes hors drawyng chare wer trappid blake beten diu er ſe armes ̄ many torche brennyng way till come weſtmī ſtre ther let make riall ſolempne enterement▪ ̄ beried hī quene anne wife deſire ferther ſide ſent edwardis ſhrine abbey ſeint petris weſtmynſtre who ſoule god haue merci ¶and ſame yere wer certayn lollers taken fals heritikis purpoſed thurgh fals treſon haue ſlayn king ̄ haue diſtroid clargie reame myght haue ther fals purpoſe ¶but lord god wold ſuffre haſt kyng warnyng ther ther falſe ordynaūce wurchyng come ſodēly wt pouer ſent iohanes without ſmythfeld anone toke c er tayn lollerres fals heritikes brought vn kīges priſence ̄ ther told ther fals purpoſe ordynaūce wold haue wrought myght haue regned ther ther told wich wer ther capitayns ̄ gou er nours ̄ kīg comaunded tour londō toke mo wt cite ̄ ſent newgate ̄ coūtres ̄ wer brought ī examinacion clargie ̄ kinges iuſtices ther wer conuicted clargie thir fals heriſi dampned iuſtice ther fals treſō ¶ wos ther iugemēt yt ſhuld draw frō toure london ſent gilesfeld ̄ ther honged brēt galewes ¶and alſo ther taken ſir rog er acto • knyght hereſi eke treſō ayens kyng reame come fore clargi ꝯuicte hereſi brēt dampnid iuſtices draw frō tour londō thurgh ye cite ſent gilesfeld ̄ honged ̄ brent ¶and ī ſecūd yere kyng hēris regne ye fifth held coūcell lordis reame weſtmynſter ther put hī demaūde praye • beſought ther goodneſſe ̄ ther good councell good ſhew touchyng titell right normandie gaſcoyn guyhenue wich kyng fraunce withheld wrongfully vnrightfully wich aunceſtres trew titell conqueſt right heritage ye wich normandie gaſcoyn guyhenne good kyng edwarde wyndeſore aunceſtres holdyn ther life tyme ¶and lordis yaf coūcell ſend enbaſſetours vn kyng fraunce ̄ coūcell ſh̄uld yeue vp vn right heritage ſay normandye gaſcoyn guyhenne wich prediceſſours hold afore▪ hī· el wold wynne dynt ſwerd ſhort tyme wt help almyghti god ¶and dolphyn fraunce anſuerid embaſfatours ̄ ſaid man er ye kyng ou er yong tendre age make ayens ̄ wos like yet good weriour make ſuch cō queſt ther vpon ¶and ſomwhat ſcorne deſpite ſent tone full tenys baules cauſe wold haue ſū play lordis come hī bettir thā maynten ony ¶and anōe lordis wer embaſſatours token ther leue come englond ayen told kyng coūcell vngodli anſuer dolphyn preſent wich ſent vn kyng ¶and whan kyng herd ther wordis anſuere dolphyn wos wond er ſore agreued right euell apayed toward frenſhmen ̄ toward kīg dolphyn thought avenge hī vpō ſone god wold ſend grace myght anōe let make tēnys balles dolphyn haſt myght wer gret gonſtonys dolphyn play ¶and anone kyng ſent lordis held gret coūcell weſtmynſter told vn anſuer dolphyn worthy preſent ſent lordis play ¶and ther kyng ̄ lordis wer accordid ſhuld redy ī armes ther pouer beſt aray myght done ̄ get men armis ar • hiers myght geten othir ſtuf longed ̄ redy ther retenue mete ſouthampton lammaſſe next ſuyng ony del • wherfore kyng ordeyned nauy ſhippis man er ſtuff ̄ vitaill longed ſuch weriour man er ordenaūce hauen ſouthampton ī nombre ccc xx ſailles ¶and fell ther gret diſſeſe foull miſchief ther wer iij lordis wich kyng truſtid moch thurgh fals couetiſe purpoſed ymagined kīgꝭ deth thought haue ſlayn brethir take ſee wich wer named thus ſir richard erle cambrigge brothir duke yorke ſecund lord scrope treſorer englond thrid wos ſir thomas gray knyght northcuntre· ¶and thees lordis afore ſaid lucrie mony made ꝓmiſſe vn frenſhmen haue ſlayn kyng henri fifth brethir fallis trayn ſodenli war ¶but myghti god gret grace held holi hand ou er ſaued frō thees ꝑllous menye ¶and haue done reſaued frenſhmen million gold wos ther openli pruued ¶and thir fals treſon wer ther iuggid vn deth iugemēt ſhuld lad thurgh hampton without north gate ther heded ̄ thus endid ther life ther fals couetiſe treſon ¶and anone wos done kyng menye made redy went ſhippe ſailled forth xv hondred ſhippis ariued within seyn kydecauſe vpō lady eue aſſumpcion normandie ordinaūce ſo went forth harflet beſeged toune lād eke wat er ſent capitayn toune charged deliu er toune capitayn ſaid deliu er id none ne none wold yeld bad beſt ¶and kyng laid ordinaūce vn toūe ſay gonnys engynes ̄ tripgettes ſhetten ̄ caſt walles ̄ began tyme eu er wer borne ¶and morow kīg crie eu er gate toūe eu er man ſh̄uld redy thee morow erly make aſſaute vn toune ¶and willyam bouchier iohn̄ graunt xij othir worthy burgies come kyng beſought riall princehode ̄ power withdraw malice deſtruccion vn beſought viij dayes reſpite trews ony reſcu might cum vn el yeld vp toūe vn hī wt ther goodis kyng ſent forth capitayn kepid remenaūt ſtill ¶and lord gaucorte capitayn toune went forth royn ye haſt vn dolphyn help ſocour bot thir none ne mā reſcue dolphyn wold abide ¶and thꝰ capitayn come ayen vn kyng yild vp ye toune deliu er ed keis called vncle ye erle dorſet made capitayn ye toune harflet deliu er ed hī ye keis bad go ̄ put frenſh peple mē woman child ſtuff toūe harflet engliſh pepull ¶and kyng ſent englond crie ī eu er good toune englond crafti man wold cum thidd er inhabite ther toune ſh̄uld haue houſe houſhold hī heiris euer ¶and ſo thed er went mony diuerſe marchantis crafti men enhabyted ther ſtrength toune welcome ¶and whan kyng ſaw toune wos well ſtuffed vitaill men worthy prince toke leue went calais ward land frenſhmen herd commyng thought ſtop • e way ſh̄uld paſſe yt way haſt myght brekyn brigges ther wher ony peſſage wos hors man ſo moch ther myght man paſſe ou er riuers nothir hors ne fote bot ſh̄uld drenchid ¶and therfore kīg pepull went ſought way ferre vp paris ward ther wos riall pouer fraunce aſſembled redy yef bataill diſtroy pepull almyghti god wos gyde ſaued menye defendid hī enmys pouer purpoſe thanked god ſaued ſo knight king rightfull titell ¶and kyng beholdīg ſeyng multitude ̄ nombre enmys ſtond way yef bataill kīg meke herte good ſpirit liften vp handis almyghti god beſought help ſocour day ſaue trew ſeruaūtis ¶and kīg gadred lordis od er pepull bad good chere· ſhold haue fair day ̄ gracious victorie ̄ bettir thir enmys ̄ prayed make redy vn bataill wold rathir dede day feld take enmys wold neuer put reame englond ranſome parſon ¶and duke yorke fell knee ̄ beſought kīg abone yt wold graūt day avaūteward batall kyng graūted aſkyng ̄ ſaid graunte merci coſī yorke prayed make redy ¶and euery man ordeyn ſtake tre ſharp endis ſtake myght pight erth ſlope ther enmys ſhuld ouer cum hors bake wos ther fals purpoſe araied ther ou er ride menye ſodenli friſt commyng friſt brunt ¶and nyght bataill frenſhmen made mony gret fiers moch reuel howting ſhowting plaid kīg lordis ye diſe ̄ archier alway blanke ther mony wend bene theris morne aroſe day gune ſpringe ¶and kyng good auiſe let aray bataill ̄ wenges chargid eu er man kepe hole gedres praid good chere ¶and whan wer redy aſkid time day wos ̄ ſaid prime ſaid kyng good time englond prais v thir fore good chere let v go iournay ſaid high vois name almyghti god ſent georgy vaunte baner ſent georgy day thyn help ¶and thees frenſhmen come prickyng doune thei wold haue ridden meny▪ bot god archiers made right ſone ſcombull archiers ſhot neuer arow amys pariſſhed brought vn ground hors ̄ man ¶for ſhot day wager ſtakes made toppe terue eche ou er othir lay heps two ſpere length hight ¶and kyng meny ̄ men armes archiers thakkid ſo thike arowes layed ſtakis kyng hys handis faught manly yt day ¶and thus almyghty god ſent georgi brought enmys groūd yaf v day victorie ¶ther wer ſlayn frenſhmen day ī felde agincourt mo xi thouſand wtout priſon er yt wer take ̄ ther wer nombred day frenſhmē feld mo ſex ſcore thouſand engliſhmē vij thouſand god yt day faught v ¶and come ther tydynges owr kyng ther wos new bataill frenſhmen ordeyned redy ſtele ̄ come towardis anone kyng let cri eu er man ſhuld ſle priſoners taken anone aray bataill ayen redy fight wt frenſhmē ¶and whan ſaw men killed doune priſoners thei drew brake ther bataill ther aray· ¶and thus kyng worthy conquerour day victori feld agencourt picardie ¶and thā kyng retourned ayen ther bataill wos ſe pepull wer ſlayn engliſhmen ony wer hurt myght holped ther wer dede feld duke barrie goddis name kyng come ou er ayen englond haſt myght ſent lukis eue come lambithe monday next aft er come ī ꝑlamēt weſtmynſtre ¶and ī ſame yere gret derth corne ī englond bot thankid god laſted thurgh cite takyng leue man er pepull well poer rich prayng gen er pray ¶and ſo rode forth ſent george ̄ ther offred toke leue maire chargyng kepe well chambur ¶and ſo rode forth hampton ther abode gonnys tripgites engynes ſowes baſtiles brigges lether ſcaling laddres malles ̄ ſpadis ſhoueles pickis paueys bowes arowes bowſtringes tonnys cheſtis pypis full arowes nedid ſuch worthi weriour thing next ther made xlviij knyghtis landyng ¶and kyng hering mōy enmys vpō ſe ſay ix gret carickes hulkis galeis ſhippis wer cumē diſtroy nauy anone commaundid erle march chief chiuetayn mony othir worthy lordis men armes archiers go ſee none enmys defoulid nauy ne entred land partie diſtrouble viage ne iourney ¶and anone erle toke menye went ſhip ſcummed ſee kepid ſe coſtis man er enmye durſt rowt vpon ſee anone king ſent heraudes vn capitayn touke charged deliu er caſtell toune el wold nothir leue man ne child liue ¶and anone capitayn iiij othir burgeſis toune brought keis vn kyng beſought grace kyng deleuered keis ſir iohan kekeley made capitayn commaundid put frenſhmen caſtell alſo toune ¶and ther beſide wos ye caſtell lous ̄ thidd er ye kīg ſēt ye erle marchal wt fair meny ̄ ſauted toūe anōeit wos yolde erle ̄ brought hī keis ̄ brought ye kīg kyng toke ayen made capitayn caſtell louers yt longed ther ̄ chargid deliu er frenſhmē ¶and kīg held forth way cane yt ſtrōg toūe afair riall caſtell ther anōe ſent heroudis capitayn chargid deliu er toune caſtell el wold get ſtrength hand anſuered ſayd toke none kepe ne nōe wold deliu er vn ¶and anone laid ſege vn toune laid gonnys eu er ſide bet doune walles toures ſlew moch pepull thir houſes alſo ſtretis good duke clarence laid doune walles ſide vn groūd ſo within ye kyng councell ſawted toune ¶and anone duke clarence entred toune ſlew un right till come king ſparid nothir man ne childe euer cried clarence clarence ſent george ¶and ther wos dede walles kyngis ſide worthy man wos called springes wich king commaundid beried abbey cane faſt wyllm cōquerour who ſoule god haue merci ameij ¶and ye king come ī toūe brothir duke clarence mony othir worthy lordis moch ſolempnite mirth ¶and king commaūdid capitayn deliu er caſtell ſought kyng yef xiiij dais reſpit reſcue wold cum yf none wold cum delyuer keis thee caſtell cōmaūdement ¶and vnder compoſiciō toūe caſtell baious othir toūes fortreſſes village nombre xiiij vpō hill caſtell cane kyng pight tentis ſemed toūe moch cane yt tyme com tidingꝭ yt reſcu wold cum ther ¶and ſo xiiij day end capitayn caſtell com deliu er id keis ̄ caſtell kyng baious ye othir xiiij· toūes wer deliu er id vn alſo anone kyng deliu er ed keis duke clarence ̄ made capitatn toūe alſo caſtell made capitayn baious othir tounes alſo ¶and ſo entrid thee toune caſtell ther held sent georgi feſt ther made xv knightis bath ther wos ſir lowys roberſart ſalyn chaynye mougomery mony othir worthy men· kyng commaundid put frenſhmen woman man ſo hardy difoule woman ne take maner good away let paſſe pee ī payn deth ¶and ther paſſid toune day mo xvc woman ¶and kyng let ſtuffe toune caſtell engliſhmen ordeyned ther two capitayns toune othir caſtell chargid vpon ther life kepe well thee toune caſtell ¶and kyng went then gatte valeys newelyn ̄ laid ſege chirburgh ſege laid duke glouceſtre ſtrong power myghti proceſſe tyme gate made ther capitayn ¶how kyng henri vi regned beyng child oon yere age bataill vernaill perche kyng henri v regned henri ſon child fulli yere age who regne began friſt day septembre yere lord mccccxxij king beyng ī cradell wos moch dowtid drad cauſe gret ꝯqueſt fad er ̄ alſo wyſdō guydyng vncles duke bedford ̄ duke glouceſtre ¶this yere xxi day october dyed charles kyng fraūce lieth beried ſent denys wos duke bedford made regent fraunce duke glouceſtre wos made ꝓtector defendour englond ¶and friſt day march aft er wos ſir willm taillour preſt degradid preſthode morow aft er wos brint ī ſmythfeld heriſe ¶thys yere ſir iames ſtiward kyng ſcottis maried dame iane duches dought er clarence hir friſt houſband erle ſomerſet ſent mari ouays ¶alſo yere xvij day auguſt wos bataill vernaill perche bitwen duke pepull duke borgoyns ¶and ſide duke alaunſon ye duke turon yt wos therle douglas erle boughan wt mōy lordis fraūce ̄ gret cō ponie ſcottis armynakis erle douglas called duke bedford iohan leden ſwerd ſent word ayen ſh̄old find day ſwerde wos ſtele ¶and ſo bataill ioyned ſides faught long tyme ther wiſt man ſh̄old haue bett er gret bot laſt god wold victori fell vn engliſh partie ther wer ſlaī erle douglas wich litel wos made duke turon erle boughan erle almarre erle toūar erle vaūtedor viſcount nerbonne wich ſlew duke iohn̄ borgoyn knelyng dolphyn ̄ mony mo vn nombre x thoſand mo wēt ou er ſe wt hir henaude take poſſeſſion hys wyfes heritance wher wos honorably receyuid taken lord land bot ſone fayn returne home ayen tho left wyfe ̄ treſour broght toune yt called mounſe henaud wich promiſed trew notwithſtondyng deliu er ed lady vn duke borgoyn wich ſent hir gaunt then ſhe aſcapid man ny clothyng come zeland toūe hir callid ziorixee then ſhe went toune holand called ghowde ther ſh̄e wos ſtrong ynowgh withſtode ſaid duke burgoyn ¶and ſone duke glouceſtre ſent ou er zeland lord fitzwater c er tayn men archiers help ſocour forſaid duchefſe holand wich • andit place xx ſoudiours midſomer euen com lord regent ̄ wife london abowt tyme pope martin died eugeyne thee fourth wos pope man peſabuly choſin rome cardinales u er indubytate pope· ſhortly put expulſid rome cardinall englond othir lordis wer ther kyng wherfor duke burgoyn wich bene long engliſh ſworn ſoke partie retourned frenſh meyn forſaid legat made pee frenſh kyng reſauyng kyng recompenſing fadris knyghtis ſquiers moch othir pepull ſent dominikys day ¶and ſame yere wer ſeyn iij ſonnys ons anone folowid threfold gou er nance ī chirch wit eugenye concell neutralite ¶alſo ſame yere mccccxxxiiij wos paſſing gret wynd wich ſtepillis houſes treis wer ou er throwen tyme wos holi maid holand called lydwith wich liued onli miracle etyng mete yere duke burgoyn began ordre lyle golden flyes ordeyned c er tayn knightis order made ſtatutis ordinaūces moch accordyng vn ord er gart er ¶alſo ſame yer frenſhmē ent er priſed haue ſtole calais ī fiſſhīg tyme mony botis fraunce ſafecōdithes cum woman nyght fore told hir ther coūcell ſh̄e morow told leuetenaunt wich forthwith commaundid eu er man ſhuld kepe wapen hand ſakring time othir ¶and whan ꝑſauyd wer miſpoynted ſayled ſtreght depe ſtole toke toune ¶and newyeres euen tokē harflet· thus engliſhmē began leſe litell litell normandie ¶how calais guynes wer beſegid ye duke burgō wer reſcued duke glouceſtre thys yere wos gret noyſe thurgh englond duke burgoyn wold cum beſege calais wherfore thee erle mortayn armye haue go fraūce wos contremaūdid ̄ chargid ſhold go calais wich wos time well vitailled ̄ mānyd ſir iohn̄ ratclife wos leuetenaūt kyng toune ye baron duddeley liuetenaūt caſtell ¶and ix day iulij duke borgoyn power flaundres moch othir pepull com calays ſet ſege toūe eu er toūe flaundres ther tentis ſelf ¶and ſege endurid iij wekis meyn ye duke glouceſtre beyng ꝓtector englond toke ye moſt ꝑtie lordis englond went ou er thee ſee calays reſcue toūe fight thee duke hoſt yf wold haue byden time london ̄ eu er good toūe englond ſent ou er ſe thys reſcu c er tayn pepull well arayd beſt choſin men ¶and ſecund day auguſt forſayd duke glouceſtre ariuid calays wyth armie v hondreth ſhippis ̄ mo ¶and duke hoſt yt lay ſege ſone aſpied ſaylles thee ſee apporched calays hauen ſodenly mornyng deꝑtid ſege leuyng behynd moch ſtuffe vitall fled flaūdres picardye lyke wyſe dide ſege lay fore guyns wher guyns token gret gonne braſſe called digeon mony othir gret gonnys ſerpentins ¶and whan duke glouceſtre wos ariued al hoſt went flaundres wos ther xij dayis litell harmi except brent two fair vilages choſe felix wich wos duke sauoye began ſciſme wich endurid vn yere lord ihū criſt mccccxlviij felix wos deuoute prīce ̄ ſawe ſonnys ſon aft er leued holi life wos choſin pope councell baſile eugenye depoſed ſo ſciſme wos long time felix moch obedience cauce neutralite moſt parte well nygh criſtyndome obeied reputid eugenye veray pope god knawoth veray pope occupied life eugeny ¶this ſame yere ſir richard wiche vecarie hermetteſworth wos degratid preſthode poules brint toure hill heritike ſent botulphus day well deth died good criſtyn man wher aft er deth moch pepull come place wher wos brent ſentorie v ꝑſons wich afterward wer reſtorid ayen ſentorie kīgꝭ iuſtices ¶after albert thrid frederike wos choſin emprour frederik duk oſterik wos long emprour ̄ differid crouned rome becauſe ſciſme vnite wos wos crouned imꝑiall diademe gret glorie triumphe pope nicholas iiij wos peſabull man quiet ſīgular paciens hating chirch weddid kyng portingales doughter c ¶how ducheſſe glouceſtre wos areſtid treſon committed ꝑpetuall priſon ile mā deth maſtir rog er bolingbroke yere elinour cobham ducheſſe glouceſtre areſtid certayn pointes treſon laid ayen hir wher vpō ſhe examined ſent stephenys chepell weſtmynſter erchebiſſhop cantorburi ther ſhe wos enioyned open penaunce go thurgh chepe bering taper hir hand ꝑpetuall priſon ile man vnder kepyng ſir thomas ſtanley ¶alſo ſame tyme wos areſtid maſter thomas ſouthwell chanon weſtmynſter maſtir iohan hume chapelayn ſaid lady maſtir roger bolingbroke clarke vſing nigromancie mariorie iurdemayn called wicch eye beſide weſtmynſtre thes wer areſtid beyng councell ſaid ducheſſe glouceſtre maſtir thomas ſouthwell died ī toure nyght ſh̄uld haue reyned morne ſelf ſayd yt ſhold die ī bed iuſtices ¶and ī xx yere maiſtir iohn̄ hume maſtir roger bolingbroke wer brought gild hall london ther mair lordis chief iuſtices englond wer rayned dampned drowen hanged quartired maſter iohn̄ hume chartre wos ꝑdoned kyngo· bot maſtir roger wos drawen tyburne wher confeſſid died giltles neu er treſpaſid died fore notwithſtondyng wos honged hedid quartired who ſoule god haue mercy ¶and margeri iurdmain wos brent ſmythfeld ¶alſo yere wos gret fray london flete ſtrete nyghtis tyme bytwen men court men london diu er ſe men ſlayn ſum hurt herbotell chief cauſer miſgou er naunce ̄ affray ¶alſo yere cheſing maire londō comūes named robert clopton raulin holand taliour ald er men toke robert clopton brough right hand meir cuſtom c er tayn tailours othir hond craftis men cried nay nay man bot raulyn holand wherfore maire wos padyſly ſent ſo cried newgate abode agret wer poniſſhed ¶in ſame yere wer diu er ſe enbaſſatours ſent guyan mariage kyng erles doughter armynake wich wos ꝯcludid meyn erle ſuffolke let put parte ¶and cite drofe then ſent ſum ſtolen newgate ¶and yong man wos reſcued felowes ſaw gret romur afray roborie enſhewed friſt meuyng lumbard deꝑtid went weſtmynſtre ſentorie el coſt life anōe aft er come wer inpurpoſed haue rongyn comune bell wich called bow bell wer let ſad men wich come knowleche duke bokyngham othir lordis incontinente aroſe durſt nolanger abide doutid yt hole cite ſh̄uld haue mannys ſoule xxv yere vn xxv becauſe curſedneſſe haboundid ſo ſore grace haboundid alſo ſore sixtus iiij ianuens frere minore wos pope paule yit makyng boke man wos generall order thee frere minoris
